Chapter 101: Fabricating Nonsense Impromptu

|| Tang Yunsheng, male, 102 years old, Nascent Soul Stage, current inspecting officer of the Everlasting Creed

Having received a message from Branch Leader Chu to come earlier, he decided to adjust his schedule and first arrived in Qinghuai Commandery, which was from Yanjiang Commandery by only one mountain.

“After going over this mountain, I’ll reach the place Little Chu mentioned.” Suddenly, Tang Yunsheng sensed a strange fluctuation of aura waves. “Hmm? What aura wave is this?”

Following the sensation, he found himself at a stable of a posthouse. Inside the stable was an old horse with dragon scales on its forehead and a small brown mare snuggled together, seemingly an indication of their deep affection for each other.

The servant boy at the stable brought a bundle of carefully handpicked grass feed and placed it in the manger. The old horse glanced at it in disdain, not deigning to eat it at all.

The servant boy muttered under his breath, “Already striking it off with a new horse? The white pony just left.”

As if the old horse could understand his words, it glared at the servant boy. Afraid of provoking the aberrant beast, the servant boy quickly scurried away.

The high-quality grass feed provided by the owner of the old horse had long been eaten up. Despite the finished supply, there was still no word from its owner. The postmaster speculated whether something had happened to the owner or if he had died. After all, the horse’s owner was headed for Pine Mountain.

After the premium feed ran out, the postmaster had the servant boy feed the horse with regular fodder. If the owner still didn’t return, he would sell the old horse to cover the cost of the fodder. However, the old horse scorned the stable’s fodder, unwilling to eat even a single bite, and a whole month had passed since.

The postmaster grew increasingly fearful. This isn’t just an aberrant beast with scales on its forehead but an extremely high-level demon beast, one that has reached the realm of fasting!

Aberrant beasts were a species between demon beasts and wild beasts. They possessed bloodlines of demon beasts, but these were so diluted that they couldn’t activate it. For their outer appearance, they would exhibit some atavistic traits such as scales, feathers, and horns. They were stronger than regular wild beasts, but their strength was limited.

When Tang Yunsheng caught sight of the old horse, he was over the moon. This is actually an extremely rare dragon horse! I just don’t know how pure its bloodline is.

“If it wasn't for me happening to visit the vast Eastern Sea once, I wouldn’t have recognized it.” Tang Yunsheng was very excited to stumble across this unexpected surprise.

Dragon horses are so rare, yet there’s one in the stable of such a remote and small commandery! It must be that the owner couldn’t discern the treasure they have, and since the dragon horse has yet to awaken, it’s left here in this backwater like a pearl buried by dust.

“As a Nascent Soul expert, I haven’t found a suitable mount all this while. This is definitely a gift from the Everlasting Immortal for my devotion!”

Tang Yunsheng prayed to the Everlasting Immortal for a moment before leaping into the stable.

The old horse turned its head to glance at Tang Yunsheng but paid no heed to him, continuing to nuzzle the brown mare tenderly.

“Poor dragon horse, you are unaware of your noble heritage and have fallen in love with a mortal horse. Come with me; I’ll show you how powerful you truly are!”

Tang Yunsheng reached out his golden hand, attempting to take the old horse away, but the old horse kicked backward with its hooves, breaking Tang Yunsheng’s hand. Feeling stiflement in his chest, Tang Yunsheng spat out a large mouthful of blood, his breathing instantly becoming feeble.

He looked at the old horse in terror, the excitement he felt moments before completely replaced by endless fear. Then, he turned and ran.

There must be a formidable master capable of treating life as a game staying here, and they are keeping the dragon horse as just an ordinary horse in the stable! My actions from earlier definitely couldn’t have escaped the formidable expert’s notice. I must flee as fast as possible and hope that they will let me off the hook on account of my ignorance!

The old horse neighed, flaunting its strength to the brown mare.

Tang Yunsheng fled for some time. When he found no signs of the puissant figure coming after him, he realized that the other party probably hadn’t taken offense to his actions.

“Ugh!” He spat out another mouthful of blood. Randomly finding a secluded spot, he sat down in a meditative state and ingested a pill to heal his injuries. The kick from the horse’s hooves was a severe blow to his vitality.

When he opened his eyes again, he heard a rumbling sound from the other side of the mountain, as if something colossal had plunged to the ground.

“It’s already night?” Tang Yunsheng was surprised to see that the sky was already dark, not expecting him to take such a long time to recover from his injuries.

Having regained sufficient strength to protect himself, he crossed over Pine Mountain and arrived at the crash site of the flying vessel. There, he saw Branch Leader Chu getting impaled by Lu Yang’s sword, his life force extinguished.

“...This is the surprise Little Chu was talking about?”

I can’t say whether it’s a surprise, but I am definitely shocked.

Before embarking on his trip, the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed had instructed him to pay attention to Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu, even providing him with their portraits. Now, even if he didn’t want to, he had no choice but to pay attention.

“Who are you!” Lu Yang raised his sword warily as he stared at Tang Yunsheng.

Tang Yunsheng looked at Lu Yang with an ambiguous smile. “Lu Yang, you dare to point your sword at me? I am Tang Yunsheng, the Inspecting Officer of the Everlasting Creed.”

Hearing Tang Yunsheng’s identity, he gestured behind his back for Lan Ting to swiftly leave the scene, for it would be tricky to explain her presence to Tang Yunsheng.

“Oh, it’s Inspecting Officer Tang.” Lu Yang’s tone became more polite, but he still eyed Tang Yunsheng suspiciously, clearly not fully trusting his identity yet.

Tang Yunsheng couldn’t be bothered to explain anything else to Lu Yang and instead asked, “Why did you kill Li Shouyi?”

Li Shouyi was the commandery governor of Yanjiang Commandery and Branch Leader Chu’s real name. Tang Yunsheng was used to calling him “Little Chu.”

Lu Yang replied gravely, “That’s because he nearly exposed his identity as a member of the Everlasting Creed!”

“Oh?” Tang Yunsheng looked at Lu Yang, curious to hear what explanation the latter could give.

Suddenly, there was a commotion from the foot of the mountain. Fang Qingyun was leading a large group of men to investigate the crash of the flying vessel. Among them were also physicians in charge of rescue efforts.

“Let’s leave first!” Tang Yunsheng was still seriously injured and didn’t want to run into the authorities. With a sweep of his sleeve, he wrapped up Lu Yang and the other two and escaped to a faraway place.

Tang Yunsheng skillfully took the trio to the Yanjiang Branch—the safest place in Yanjiang Commandery.

“You can tell me now. Li Shouyi has always been prudent. How did he expose his identity?”

Lu Yang revealed everything about the Lifespan-Reversal Array, then added, “Branch Leader Chu...wait, I mean, Commandery Governor Li’s plan could be considered airtight. He first made One Zhang Red a scapegoat, then set up the Lifespan-Reversal Array in secret. As long as he destroyed the small flags afterward, there would be no traces left.”

Tang Yunsheng nodded. Li Shouyi has always been cautious, and he had used the extremely obscure Lifespan-Reversal Array. The plan this time was flawless.

“But an accident still happened. The three of us opened a barbeque shop here, since such a place is best for gathering local intelligence. We noticed a disciple from the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace passing by, and she seemed to be proficient in arrays and have seen through the Lifespan-Reversal Talismans on the small flags!

“We can’t lay our hands on disciples from the Five Great Immortal Sects. As we were worried that Governor Li might get found out and implicate the whole creed, we urged him to quickly go into hiding. However, he insisted that it was a critical juncture. As he had to use the Lifespan-Reversal Array to advance to the Nascent Soul Stage, he absolutely couldn’t hide. Out of options, we could only try to kill him before the Great Xia Dynasty captures him, stamping out any potential complications in the future!

“You also noticed the people from the authorities earlier, right? The one leading them is Chief Constable Fang Qingyun. Why else did he bring so many people? They were certainly there to stop the Lifespan-Reversal Array from activating and arrest Commandery Governor Li!”

Tang Yunsheng nodded, agreeing with the trio’s actions. The matter regarding the disciple from the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace is easily verifiable, so they can’t lie about that. Li Shouyi was indeed also obsessed with rising to the Nascent Soul Stage.

Usually, branch leaders would be at the Nascent Soul Stage. It was only because Yanjiang Commandery was small that the branch leader stationed here was at the Golden Core Stage. If Li Shouyi wanted to be promoted to a branch leader of a prosperous region, he needed to progress to the Nascent Soul Stage now. This also applied to his identity as a government official. Without adequate cultivation, the path to promotion would be fraught with challenges.

Man Gu looked at Lu Yang in astonishment. It was totally not in the plan to encounter Tang Yunsheng after killing Branch Leader Chu. I have also not thought about a reason for killing him. How did Brother Lu manage to do it impromptu?

Meng Jingzhou inwardly gave Lu Yang a thumbs-up. The reason Lu Yang came up with is pretty similar to the one I’ve just fabricated on the fly.

Chapter 102: Your Mission Is To Infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect

“Since Li Shouyi is already dead, we will forget about his promotion. Based on his identity, the authorities may suspect that a diabolic creed is situated in the area. Everyone here has to lie low for a while.” Tang Yunsheng swiftly came to a decision, a result of his experience from rising through the ranks and decisive style of handling matters. “As for the three of you, take out your bone tablets.”

The trio handed over their bone tablets which had the characters for “Administrator” written. Tang Yunsheng stopped before the Everlasting Immortal’s statue and bowed three times, his hands glowing with golden light as he chanted rapidly under his breath.

With a swipe of his hand, the characters for “Administrator” changed to “Branch Leader.”

As the inspecting officer, Tang Yunsheng had been authorized by the higher-ups to adjust the ranks of members who were branch leaders and below. Promoting the trio to branch leaders was not Tang Yunsheng’s decision but the higher-ups. As for which higher-up it was in particular, Tang Yunsheng wasn’t sure. However, he had heard that it was from the tier the deputy creed leader was in or even higher than that. I’m just executing orders.

“Which commandery do you want us to go to as branch leaders?” Meng Jingzhou was eager to display his full potential.

Tang Yunsheng shook his head. “What are you thinking? You are only at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage. How can you command respect and convince those below you? It’s not even possible at a place like Yanjiang Branch. A branch leader will be parachuted to Yanjiang Commandery. That’s not something you need to worry about.”

“So our status as branch leaders...”

“Making you branch leaders wasn’t my idea but the higher-ups’. They promoted you to branch leaders without official duties so that you can enjoy the many benefits and power that comes with being a branch leader, effectively reducing the restrictions you face. They have assigned you a secret mission. You can’t tell anyone else other than the four of us!”

The trio stood at attention, readying themselves for what was to come.

Tang Yunsheng whispered, “The higher-ups have given you a year’s time to find a way to infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect, and I will be your handler!”

The trio’s pupils constricted, startled by the mission.

Tang Yunsheng waved his hand. “I know that this mission is extremely difficult. Among the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Hanging Monastery has too few members, which makes it tricky to plant someone there, while the Dao-Seeking Sect are overly erratic thinkers, making it a challenge to infiltrate. Even if you do get in, your identity will get exposed from not being able to fit in. However, the three of you have very high compatibility with the Dao-Seeking Sect. Perhaps you’ll be the breakthrough in successfully infiltrating them.

“I’m not exactly requesting you to become disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. According to analysis from our intelligence, the Dao-Seeking Sect has a prosperous entertainment and recreation industry that recruits people every year. You can use this opportunity to infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect!

“Of course, what I’m suggesting is just one method. The creed won’t interfere, so you have the freedom to explore other options. The deadline is in one year. If you can’t complete the mission then, the higher-ups will assign a new mission for you!”

Seeing the confidence brimming from the trio’s expressions, Tang Yunsheng couldn’t help but shake his head and chuckle. They still don’t know how much of a hurdle it is to infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect. I can’t remember how many people have tried and lost their lives there.

He passed three talismans to them. “These are Faraway Escape Talismans. The Dao-Seeking Sect is fraught with perils. If you fail your mission, use this immediately to flee!”

These three are rare talents for the Everlasting Creed, especially Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. The creed leader naturally has to provide them with adequate protection.

Meng Jingzhou thought to himself, The Dao-Seeking Sect is fraught with perils? When I go back to the Dao-Seeking Sect, it's like going back to my own home. What dangers are you talking about? If there really is a danger, then that is Big Senior Sister.

“One more thing, did Little Chu tell you how to resurrect the Everlasting Immortal?”

Lu Yang shook his head. “Branch Leader Chu only revealed to us the first step, which is killing to please the Everlasting Immortal. As for the second step, he said that our ranks were too low, so the rules forbid him to tell us.”

Tang Yunsheng said, “Now that you are branch leaders, you are qualified to learn how to resurrect the Everlasting Immortal. This is the duty of every branch leader. Come, I'll demonstrate it to you once.”

Tang Yunsheng knelt before the statue of the Everlasting Immortal, both his hands raised as he called out loudly, “Everlasting Immortal Miao Muzhen above us, your most devout followers are here sincerely calling upon you. Please bestow us with your immortal traces and bless humanity!” He bowed three more times before getting up.

The ritual was complete.

Question marks were popping out from the trio’s heads. That's all?

Man Gu wondered, Why does the Everlasting Immortal’s name sound like one from the Ancient Barbarian Tribe?

Tang Yunsheng stressed, “You must strictly follow the steps I took in calling upon the Everlasting Immortal, but you can't say ‘Miao Muzhen.’”

“Why is that?”

“Because Miao Muzhen is not the Everlasting Immortal’s real name.”

The trio became even more bewildered. What’s the point in you saying it when it’s not even the real name?

Tang Yunsheng explained, “To resurrect the Everlasting immortal, one must call out their title and immortal name. The reason for the first step being killing to please the Everlasting Immortal is because once the Everlasting Immortal is happy, they will somehow guide us to say their immortal name.

“We have already discovered from the ruins that their title is the ‘Everlasting Immortal,’ but the ruins don’t have their name recorded. Before the Everlasting Immortal grants an immortal trace, we at the Everlasting Creed can only keep trying.

“Out of respect for the Everlasting Immortal, there must be a one-month interval between calling out their immortal name!”

Tang Yunsheng fished out a tattered Great Xia Dictionary. “Most names have already been tested with. Recently, I suspected that the Everlasting Immortal was from the Barbarian Tribe, so I have been trying names from the Barbarian Tribe.” The Ancient Barbarian Tribe was once a pivotal force in protecting humans, so it aligns with the Everlasting Immortal’s identity.

Tang Yunsheng pulled out three thick notebooks, which were titled Immortal Names Already Called (Version 120), and handed them to the trio. The numerous immortal names recorded made Lu Yang suspect that the Everlasting Creed had already tried every conceivable name.

“Every few decades, we will compile the immortal names again to prevent repetition. This is the latest compilation. Take a look and try calling out a name that’s not in the notebook.”

Lu Yang called out loudly, “Everlasting Immortal Archimedes above us, your most devout followers are here sincerely calling upon you. Please bestow us with your immortal traces and bless humanity!”

Meng Jingzhou called out loudly, “Everlasting Immortal Li Dog Egg[1] above us...”

Man Gu called out loudly, “Everlasting Immortal Yelü Salade[2] above us...”

Clearly, there were very few remaining options for the Everlasting Immortal’s name.

After their attempts, the Everlasting Immortal did not descend and display any immortal trace.

“That will do. I’ve already relayed the mission assigned to you by the higher-ups. Pack up your things and find your own way into the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Understood.”

When they returned to the barbeque shop, Lan Ting was already waiting for the three of them. Lu Yang and Lan Ting cross-checked their testimonies and briefly shared with her what had transpired afterward, including the mission Tang Yunsheng had informed them about.

Lan Ting stared at the trio with a peculiar expression. The Everlasting Creed will meet its end sooner or later.

“Since you’ll be leaving, I should also return to the celestial palace to report my mission. It has been a pleasure spending the past ten days with you. Many thanks for your assistance. Although I didn’t join the diabolic creed, helping you to kill the branch leader is a great meritorious achievement. I’ll be able to earn a few contribution points for that,” Lan Ting sweetly said, reluctant to bid goodbye.

Fate truly works in miraculous ways. Initially, I had aided Lu Yang in killing the tiger demon out of obligation to help a fellow immortal sect member. I was also on a mission to infiltrate the diabolic creed. Who would have thought, the person with the mission didn’t join the diabolic creed, while the trio that weren’t aware of the diabolic creed in the beginning ended up joining it?

As Tang Yunsheng was still in the commandery, they might get discovered by him if they had prolonged contact, leading to unnecessary trouble.

“The journey in the jianghu is an arduous one. May we meet again if fate allows!”

“Goodbye!”

“Take care!”

After bidding goodbye to Lan Ting, the trio began packing their things when Meng Jingzhou suddenly remembered, “Where’s our horse?”

1. There was sometimes a culture of giving vulgar names to children especially among impoverished peasants in ancient China because it was thought to ward off evil monsters and spirits. ☜

2. Yelü Salade was the leader of the Diela Tribe from the Khitan clan during the Tang dynasty. ☜

Chapter 103: It Seems Like We’ve Gotten the Correct Immortal Name

The old horse was very lucky to be found before it promised a lifetime with the little brown mare. Meng Jingzhou paid the money as he collected the old horse and the carriage.

“No, no, no, it doesn’t cost so much to stay at a stable,” the servant boy declined.

“What about the money for the feed? Don’t you want that?” Meng Jingzhou was puzzled. The old horse has long finished the premium fodder, so I thought that it would have no choice but to eat ordinary fodder out of hunger.

The servant boy shook his head. “Your horse didn’t eat anything.”

“Hmm?” Meng Jingzhou was bemused. He stroked the old horse’s mane and asked, “You managed to fast?”

The old horse snorted loudly but didn’t reply. After all, how could a horse speak?

Meng Jingzhou summoned his inner fierceness to threaten the horse, “If you don’t reply, there’ll be no more fodder for you!”

One man and one horse were at a stalemate for a long time. The old horse never replied to him, and Meng Jingzhou eventually admitted defeat as he pieced some things together.

No wonder it went without a hitch when I left my home back then. Even my younger sister knows that I was leaving home, which means that the others at home must have known too, yet no one stopped me and were unconcerned about my safety. Excluding the possibility that I’m not their biological child, the only explanation is that they knew I would be safe.

Now, the answer is clear—the horse pulling the carriage is the greatest assurance. I wonder what the old horse’s cultivation is. It should be quite high to be able to protect me.

Meng Jingzhou grumbled, “If you’re so strong, why didn’t you stop Big Senior Sister from boarding the carriage back then?”

Meng Jingzhou still remembered how he had foolishly treated Yun Zhi as a candidate, inviting her into the carriage and revealing that he had obtained the examination questions for entering the Dao-Seeking Sect.

That was utterly embarrassing, so much so that I felt like running all the way to my grandma’s house to hide. If only the old horse had stopped Big Senior Sister from getting on, none of all those would have happened!

The old horse gave Meng Jingzhou the side-eye, as if the latter was a fool.

~~~

Before Lu Yang departed, he paid a visit to Constable Captain Wei, who was not surprised that the trio were leaving. Which cultivator would really run a barbeque shop for life? It was just for the experience. Once the novelty wears off, they will close the shop.

Captain Wei lamented, “What a pity, I won’t get to enjoy such delicious barbeque anymore. I was even hoping to catch criminals at your barbeque shop until I rise to the position of Chief Constable.” Captain Wei estimated that if he could arrest three more diabolic cultivators, he could finally get promoted to Chief Constable. “It’s not a bad thing that you’re leaving. Things in Yanjiang Commandery likely won’t be peaceful for a bit.”

“What do you mean?”

Captain Wei whispered, “You mustn’t tell this to anyone else.”

“I know that.”

Captain Wei had faith in Lu Yang’s character. “You know Commandery Governor Li, right? There are currently rumors that he had colluded with diabolic cultivators to get promoted. Whether it was with rogue diabolic cultivators or someone from a diabolic creed remains uncertain, but the other party’s cultivation was definitely high enough to have collaborated with Commandery Governor Li.

“Commandery Governor Li’s corpse was discovered on Pine Mountain. Chief Constable Fang suspects that there was a conflict of interest between the diabolic cultivators and Commandery Governor Li which resulted in his death, while the diabolic cultivators remain at large. This implies that their cultivation was higher than Commandery Governor Li’s. Commandery Governor Li is only one step away from the Nascent Soul Stage. Just think about how high the diabolic cultivators’ cultivation must be!”

Lu Yang recoiled slightly. “What vicious diabolic cultivators!”

“That’s why I said that it’s not a bad thing that you’re leaving. Yanjiang Commandery may seem peaceful, but you never know where diabolic cultivators are hiding. For all we know, they may be right beside us!”

Lu Yang fully agreed with him. “Indeed.”

~~~

Man Gu reluctantly bid farewell to the barbeque shop. In the end, the splendor of the Man Family’s barbeque can’t be brought to new heights in my generation.

The two tiger-henchman ghosts were dancing in ecstasy, celebrating their freedom from having to barbecue day and night.

~~~

Before their departure, Tang Yunsheng saw the trio off, reminding them that infiltrating the Dao-Seeking Sect would be fraught with obstacles and that they must be cautious.

Lu Yang reassured him, “Don’t worry, we are not planning to disappoint the creed. We will definitely infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect, steal their secrets, and bring glory to the Everlasting Creed.”

~~~

The old horse pulled the carriage unhurriedly, appearing to move at a leisurely pace, but it was in fact covering immense distance. This involved profound knowledge of space.

The three chatted about the Everlasting Immortal on board the carriage.

“Look, the notebook even has our names: Everlasting Immortal Lu Yang, Everlasting Immortal Meng Jingzhou, Everlasting Immortal Mangu.” Lu Yang laughed. Seeing his name in the diabolic creed’s notebook was quite the amusing thing.

He could find the names of all the people he knew in the notebook, indicating that the diabolic creed was assiduous in reviving the Everlasting Immortal.

“Say, what do you think the Everlasting Immortal’s real name is? Mendeleev? Socrates?”

Meng Jingzhou giggled. “Maybe it’s a vulgar name like Dog Egg or Dog something? They were too embarrassed to say their name out loud, so they hid it and only used an honorific title.”

“It could also be a name from our Barbarian Tribe.”

The trio lacked any form of reverence for the Everlasting Immortal. They tossed Tang Yunsheng’s instructions about the one-month interval between guessing the names to the back of their minds, casually throwing out guesses.

“Tone it down a bit, guys. What if we actually guess the name correctly?” Lu Yang warned. It’s still uncertain whether the Everlasting Immortal is a friend or a foe. The Everlasting Creed’s one-sided claim of the Everlasting Immortal protecting humanity also can’t be fully trusted.

“How about this? Let’s call the ‘Everlasting Immortal’ as the ‘Everlasting Immortal Fairy’ from now on. That way, even if we guess the correct name, the Everlasting Immortal can’t get resurrected,” Lu Yang proposed.

“I agree, Lu Yang has a point.” Meng Jingzhou raised his hand in approval.

Man Gu thought, I have to give it to Brother Lu for being so thorough.

After the carriage had traveled for a while, the trio began to feel hungry. They alighted at a grove, planning to eat something.

The grove shielded them from the irksome sunlight. The atmosphere was tranquil, and faint birdsongs could be heard from the distance, easing one into relaxation.

Meng Jingzhou laid out a picnic cloth, Lu Yang took out pots, bowls, and utensils along with fire-starting talismans, while Man Gu summoned the tiger-henchman ghosts.

The two tiger-henchman ghosts had just been unemployed for half a day when Man Gu summoned them back. They returned to their old profession, skilfully barbecuing.

Meng Jingzhou fished out a cookbook and a bunch of bottles and jars, pushing them all to the two tiger-henchman ghosts. “Don’t barbecue anymore. Let's change up the flavor. Come, follow this cookbook.”

Lu Yang and Man Gu cast sidelong glances at him. Why do you bring a cookbook around with you?

The two tiger-henchman ghosts could only start learning from scratch, planning to begin with the simplest scrambled eggs. Despite not working hard when they were alive, they had to study diligently now that they are dead.

The three had no intention of ingesting Fasting Pills at all. If we can enjoy delicious food, why do we have to resort to things like Fasting Pills?

Lu Yang asked, “Tang Yunsheng speculated that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was from the Barbarian Tribe. Are there related legends from the Ancient Barbarian Tribe?”

Man Gu shook his head. “I heard from the elders about how the Ancient Barbarian Tribe fought against heaven and earth and were capable of battling immortals, but never have I heard of an immortal ever being born in our tribe.

“The ruins are also very strange. If it records the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s greatness, why didn’t it include their name along with it?”

Meng Jingzhou analyzed logically, “Think about it. During the ancient times, everyone had imposing titles and names, and they would report their names prior to battles. If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy just came up and introduced themselves as “I am the Everlasting Immortal, Li Dog Egg, wait, I mean, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy Li Dog Egg, they would have lost in grandeur even before the battle began! The Everlasting Immortal Fairy would definitely want to erase this kind of embarrassing blemish from their past!”

Lu Yang laughed. “It could also be that the name was too cute and not intimidating at all, something like the ‘Everlasting Immortal Fairy Huang Doudou.” [1]

The words ‘Everlasting Immortal Fairy Huang Doudou’ seemed to have triggered a cosmic secret, causing a shift in the fabric of heaven and earth. An incomprehensible power swirled above the trio and formed a silhouette.

The old horse instantly became vigilant, positioning itself in front of Meng Jingzhou protectively as it stared fixedly at the power in the air.

The three swallowed nervously.

Uh oh, it looks like things have spiraled out of control.

1. Huang Doudou translates literally to ‘yellow bean bean.’ Names with repeated characters also tend to sound cuter. ☜

Chapter 104: Still Have To Count on Big Senior Sister

“What’s going on?!” The three of them glared at one another, unsure of what to do.

“Is the Everlasting Creed even reliable? Isn’t it supposed to be the ‘Everlasting Immortal?’ Why is there a response when I said the ‘Everlasting Immortal Fairy?!’” Lu Yang berated the unreliability of the Everlasting Creed. You can’t even be sure whether you worship the Everlasting Immortal or the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. What kind of creed are you?!

“Enough of the nonsense, let’s run!” Meng Jingzhou yelled. It’s not the time for complaints now.

The figure congealing in the sky was like an illusionary bubble, its existence extremely unstable. She had sensed the karmic relationship with Lu Yang and realized that it was Lu Yang who had called out her real name. Turning into a beam of light, she entered Lu Yang’s body.

“Only reached the Foundation Establishment Stage recently? Such a weak being.” The figure arrived in Lu Yang’s mental space, which was only a small area as it had yet to be opened up by Lu Yang. As the figure arrived in the mental space, Lu Yang also found himself there.

The mental space was shrouded in darkness, as if it was surrounded by invisible walls, with only a tiny area in the center illuminated, where Lu Yang and the figure stood.

Lu Yang eyed the figure warily. “Who are you?!”

The figure chuckled, observing Lu Yang’s reaction with interest. Her voice was supposed to be melodious, but to Lu Yang, it sounded like a judgment from the depths of hell. “Heh, you’ve already called my name, yet you don’t know who I am?”

Initially clinging on to a sliver of hope, Lu Yang’s heart now sank. The worst-case scenario has occurred. I didn’t expect the other party to really be the Everlasting Creed’s faith.

The other party is a bona fide immortal, and one that has revived from the dead at that! Only her name needs to be called to be resurrected. What a truly terrifying existence!

“What do you want?”

The figure didn’t deign to answer Lu Yang and instead asked, “What is the current year? And who controls the universe?”

“It is currently the Great Xia Dynasty, and the supreme ruler of humans is the Xia Emperor. A hundred thousand years ago, it was the Great Yu Dynasty. I don’t know the dynasties before that.”

“Xia Emperor? Great Xia? Great Yu? They’re all dynasties I’ve never heard of.” The figure shook her head and continued to ask, “How long have I been dead?”

This question was beyond Lu Yang’s realm of knowledge. “As far as I know, you are an immortal from ancient times. You protected humans when the Nameless One refined the stars into the Central Continent.” Lu Yang tried to hint to her that she had once performed heroic feats of protecting humanity and was thus a righteous immortal, so she shouldn’t do anything beneath her status to a junior like him.

“Nameless One? Refined the stars into the Central Continent? Protected humans? What kind of nonsense is all of that?” The figure was utterly bewildered.

Lu Yang almost cursed out loud. I knew the Everlasting Creed couldn’t be trusted. Is there even a modicum of truth in their intelligence? Why does the other party know nothing about these matters?

The figure realized that her era had long passed, and in fact, so long that humans had completely forgotten about her. Had there been just one person who called out my title and immortal name, I would have been resurrected long ago and not be completely oblivious about the Great Yu and Great Xia dynasties like I am now.

So be it. Since the world has forgotten my name, I’ll use this young man’s body to make my name, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy Huang Doudou, resound throughout heaven and earth once more.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy set her gaze on Lu Yang, a trace of approval and amusement in her eyes.

An ominous feeling wrapped around Lu Yang as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s cold laughter sounded in his ears. “I see that your cultivation is low and that you have just broken through to the Foundation Establishment Stage. However, your spirit root is excellent, and so are your fundamentals. As such, let me take over your body and lead you along to discover this splendid world!”

Body takeover! Things were progressing step by step in the direction Lu Yang had hoped for the least. However, Lu Yang was unwilling to let his body get taken over so easily. He assumed his stance as he prepared to square off against the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Then, he performed a set of fist techniques that resembled that of a female.

“Don’t think you’re anything impressive just because you’re an immortal!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scoffed. What can such feeble punches do? She had already examined her surroundings—two tiger-henchman ghosts, two Foundation Establishment cultivators, and one dragon horse. No one can stop me from the body takeover!

If Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were here, they would certainly have recognized that Lu Yang was delivering the ultimate technique of Animal Form Fist—Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist.

~~~

At the Dao-Seeking Sect, Yun Zhi was currently in the Discussion Hall, discussing various matters of the sect with the eight elders.

“I believe that there should be more spirit stones allocated to our Pill Cauldron Peak. We are about to make a major breakthrough in the Dao of Pills! We only need some spirit stones to make it happen. This is a historic moment. Any amount of spirit stones invested is worth it!”

“The spirit stones might as well be given to our herb garden instead. We can replace the bottom arrays to let the herbs grow stronger!”

The elders were expressing their opinions on the allocation of the spirit stones, not willing to budge an inch. When Yun Zhi was about to speak, the eight elders stopped talking.

Suddenly, Yun Zhi paused. That sensation is back again. Is it Lu Yang borrowing my power? A wisp of power materialized at her fingertip. Should I give it to him?

Previously, Lu Yang had easily borrowed power from Yun Zhi because she wasn’t on guard, but since she was prepared this time, she didn’t let even a thread of power leak out. With some contemplation, Yun Zhi decided to withdraw her power and personally check on what Lu Yang was up to.

“Please continue your discussion first, elders. I’ll be back shortly.”

Yun Zhi’s soul left her body and soared through the sky, leaving the elders exchanging confused glances. Leaping forward at inconceivable speed, her soul found the target location and entered Lu Yang’s body.

As soon as she arrived, she heard the Everlasting Immortal Fairy taunting, “Just surrender obediently and let me take over your body.”

At one glance, Yun Zhi could tell that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was an immortal soul. Though weak, it was complete.

“You dare lay your hands on my little junior brother?” Yun Zhi extended her delicate hand, slapping it at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Who is it?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was astounded. I didn’t detect the other party’s arrival at all. Even though this is partially due to my weak immortal soul after just getting resurrected, that was still very impressive.

She felt somewhat glad. During this long period I was dead, humanity has actually given birth to such a genius.

“Dao-Seeking Sect. Yun Zhi.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy wanted to block Yun Zhi’s hand, but although the attack seemed weak, it actually encompassed the essence of the universe with ineffable splendor and ingenuity, as if all spell principles had been exhausted within it, rendering it impossible to resist.

“Wait, perhaps there’s a misunderstanding between us! I was just joking with a junior!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s expression changed drastically as she mustered all possible means to deflect the palm attack. The other party’s power had far exceeded her wildest expectations.

Yun Zhi saw no reason to listen to what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was saying. Without hesitation, her palm slammed down, suppressing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was enraged as she vehemently struggled, “Little lass, you’re pushing your luck. Don’t think that I am scared of you! Immortals shall not be humiliated!”

Seeing that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t given up on resistance, Yun Zhi furrowed her brow and hurled Lu Yang out of the mental space. With Lu Yang here, it’s not convenient for me to employ my methods.

Whoosh! Lu Yang finally left his mental space and returned to reality. He let out a long breath, relieved after his narrow escape.

When Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu saw that Lu Yang had regained his senses, they quickly rushed forward to check how he was. Just a while ago, Lu Yang’s eyes had suddenly gone vacant. Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were thrown into panic and at a loss for what to do. After that, they saw a soul resembling that of Yun Zhi’s entering Lu Yang’s body.

Lu Yang shook his head. “I don’t know.” It’s not that I don’t have confidence in Big Senior Sister, but the other party is an immortal after all, and from the ancient era at that. Big Senior Sister has said that there are no immortals in the world, which means that she can’t be one.

Lu Yang didn’t know who would emerge victorious out of the two.

“If Big Senior Sister is here, there should be no problem.” Meng Jingzhou said with uncertainty. I know that Big Senior Sister is strong, but I don’t know exactly how strong she is.

“Alright, come in.” Soon, Lu Yang heard Yun Zhi’s voice from within him, her voice as cool and crisp as ever.

Lu Yang returned to his mental space again and saw that the once almighty Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been reduced to a miserable state, trying her best to explain to Yun Zhi that she was a good person. “It wasn’t easy for me to get resurrected, and I just wanted to make a harmless joke with a junior. I’m a woman, so how could I take over a male’s body? I, Huang Doudou, also have my pride. I won’t do something so disgraceful.

“Besides, I’m just an immortal soul. A Foundation Establishment cultivator’s body wouldn’t be able to withstand my power.”

Yun Zhi quietly observed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy for what seemed to be ages until she finally replied, “Oh.”

It could somewhat be taken as her believing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words.

Chapter 105: The Unlucky Everlasting Immortal Fairy

“Is your name really Huang Doudou?”[1] Lu Yang asked skeptically.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face stiffened. “Little one, how can a mortal call out this esteemed one’s immortal name? You have to address this esteemed one as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy!”

“So, Everlasting Immortal Fairy, is your name really Huang Doudou?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face fell. “My parents gave me this name. It’s not like I can change it.”

Yun Zhi interrupted their pointless conversation. “Tell me, what have you been up to? You were only gone for two months, and you already got entangled by an immortal.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy corrected Yun Zhi, “Mind your words. I didn’t entangle myself with him. The way you’re putting it makes me seem like some lovelorn fool!”

Yun Zhi responded with nothing but a cold gaze.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy contemplated for a bit. I’ve just been resurrected, my immortal soul is weak, and I know nothing about the outside world. I shouldn’t be making an enemy.

However, I’m after all a dignified immortal who once commanded the wind and clouds in ancient times. I still have to uphold my pride and be more assertive to warn them that I’m not someone to be trifled with.

“Do as you wish.”

Lu Yang glanced at the well-behaved Everlasting Immortal Fairy, then at Yun Zhi’s cold gaze, and obediently recounted what had transpired over the past two months. “I wasn’t up to much, really. Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu looked for me, saying that there was a tiger demon causing trouble in Yanjiang Commandery and that killing it would earn us contribution points. The three of us agreed that it was a sure-win mission, so we went ahead.

“Things went smoothly when killing the tiger demon. While sorting through the loot, we discovered that the tiger demon was connected to the diabolic creeds, so we followed the trail to locate the diabolic creed and see if we could kill off a few diabolic creed followers to rid the people of harm.

“Later, we heard that the diabolic creeds were recruiting, so we seized the opportunity to slip in and test the waters. To our surprise, we got quite lucky and made it in.

“After getting in, the diabolic creed’s local leader thought highly of us and made us administrators.

“Although we are physically with the diabolic path, our hearts lie with the righteous path. During our time in the diabolic creed, we tracked down all kinds of clues and discovered that the local leader had secretly set up a Lifespan-Reversal Array to break through to the Nascent Soul Stage. After a series of gallant battles and some cunning machinations, we successfully killed him.

“At the same time, the inspecting officer dispatched by the higher-ups of the diabolic creed felt that we have a solid foundation and quick thinking, so he promoted us to branch leaders, and they even sent us back to the Dao-Seeking Sect as spies.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy listened with amusement. “What a stupid diabolic creed, sending you three back as spies. What is this diabolic creed called? If I ever encounter them, I’ll be sure to mock them through and through.”

“The Everlasting Creed. They worship you,” Lu Yang replied.

The smile on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face froze.

Lu Yang continued, “The people of the Everlasting Creed told us that when the Ancient Nameless One refined the stars into the Central Continent, the Everlasting Immortal had saved the human race. As long as we call out the title of ‘Everlasting Immortal’ along with their immortal name, we’ll be able to revive the immortal and save humanity once again.

“On our way back, we got bored and started guessing what the Everlasting Immortal’s name might be, but we were also worried about the consequences should we accidentally resurrect an immortal, so we changed ‘Everlasting Immortal’ to ‘Everlasting Immortal Fairy.’ As for the outcome, Big Senior Sister, you saw what happened. I ended up reviving her.”

Yun Zhi nodded. “You three certainly have had quite the experience, successfully infiltrating the Everlasting Creed and even rising to the rank of branch leaders. This is indeed a great meritorious achievement. There are many technicalities to their selection process which enable them to distinguish real devils. It’s genuinely not easy for you to have entered the Everlasting Creed.

“I have also heard of their attempts to revive the Everlasting Immortal, though I didn’t know the specifics. Never would I have expected you to accidentally succeed.”

Yun Zhi cast her gaze on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, whose brow was knitted as she was in rumination. “And what about you? Do you have anything to say?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “I’ve never heard of any Everlasting Creed, and neither do I know anything about the Ancient Nameless One refining the stars. I also don’t recall saving the human race.

“The era I came from was known as the Golden Age of Heavenly Mandate, referring to how the heavens were merciful and benevolent and that one’s fate lay in our own hands. I was born a human and attained the immortal Dao Fruit during this prosperous era, becoming an immortal. Due to the special ability of the Dao Fruit, I was called the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.”

Yun Zhi calmly stated, “The Golden Age of Heavenly Mandate is what we often call the ancient era.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “Apart from me, there were four other people who became immortals. Later, someone ambushed me and killed me thoroughly.

“Just like what the Everlasting Creed says, as long as someone calls out my title and immortal name, I can be resurrected. But I don’t know why my name was mistakenly propagated as the ‘Everlasting Immortal,’ which resulted in me only getting revived now. And even now, I still don’t know how long I’ve been dead.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was full of grievances. I just got resurrected and wanted to strut around and show off a bit in front of a junior to intimidate him into obedience. However, he ended up directly calling his Big Senior Sister over. And if that wasn’t bad enough, this Big Senior Sister of his is so ridiculously powerful that she suppressed me right away.

Who can I complain to?

Why do I have to bump into such a powerful person right after I got revived?

Yun Zhi analyzed, “It might not have been a mistake in propagation. It could also be that someone wanted to revive you but didn’t want to get entangled in karmic ties with you, so they made use of the Everlasting Creed to call out your title and immortal name, even intentionally altering your title to ‘Everlasting Immortal.’ When the Everlasting Creed has tried every single name and realized that nothing was working, they might speculate that the title was incorrect. That way, if the Everlasting Creed resurrects you, they will be the one getting intertwined in karmic ties with you, not the mastermind behind.”

The higher one’s cultivation was, the more they valued karma, believing that karma manipulated the invisible threads of fate.

Yun Zhi furrowed her brow slightly. Now, it’s not the Everlasting Creed that has karmic entanglements with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it’s Lu Yang who has accidentally borne this tremendous karmic burden.

“As for how long you have been dead,” Yun Zhi paused before asking, “You don’t know who refined the stars?” Her tone was still light, but Lu Yang could sense a trace of solemness within it, indicating that Yun Zhi placed great importance on this question.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head, her visage one of bewilderment. “I don’t know. What’s going on now? When I was alive, everyone lived on the stars. Did someone refine the stars into a continent?”

Yun Zhi nodded. “Before the Great Xia Dynasty was the Great Yu Dynasty, and before that was the Great Qian Dynasty. Only before that was the Golden Age of Heavenly Mandate you spoke of and what we call the ancient era.

“The Great Qian and Great Yu dynasties each existed for one hundred thousand years before getting replaced. The Great Xia Dynasty has also existed for a hundred thousand years. Some say that this is a curse from ancient times, that every dynasty can only last for one hundred thousand years, after which it will inevitably collapse and a new one rises from the ruins.

“At the end of the ancient era, an immortal refined the stars into a continent, completely changing the entire world into what is now the Central Continent.

“In other words, you have been dead for at least three hundred thousand years.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was flabbergasted. “That long?! If I had known, I would have deposited my spirit stones in the bank. Imagine the amount of interest I could’ve earned!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, are you sure you’re focusing on the right thing?

1. Huang Doudou translates literally to ‘yellow bean bean.’ Names with repeated characters also tend to sound cuter. ☜

Chapter 106: Triumphant Return

“How did you use my power?” Yun Zhi looked at Lu Yang, somewhat puzzled. From what Lu Yang described, it doesn’t sound like he was qualified to access such a profound and complex spell like the Divine Invocation Technique.

“Uh... I simply happened to obtain a set of Animal Form Fist. When I was practicing, I thought of how Animal Form Fist is a type of fist technique that mimics a target, so why do I have to limit myself to mimicking animals? Humans can also be imitated. Among all the people I know, you are the most powerful, Big Senior Sister, so I decided to copy you. That was how I obtained your power.”

Yun Zhi, “...” She had been proficient in spells and techniques since her childhood and was considered a prodigy. Not only could she learn any spell after one look, she would also correct their flaws to make them even more impeccable. She even derived many long-lost spells such as the Divine Invocation Technique.

But I have really never encountered a situation like Lu Yang’s.

“Even if I share a sliver of my power with you, it’s not something the current you can bear. Don’t use this type of fist technique without good reason.”

Lu Yang could discern the underlying connotation in Yun Zhi’s words—solve your own problems; don’t call me over unless necessary.

“And you, leave Lu Yang’s body.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s attitude firmed up, a rare occurrence for her. She shook her head as she refused, “I can’t leave him.”

“Hmm?” Yun Zhi raised her voice by two degrees.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hastily explained, “I was just resurrected, and my immortal soul is weak. I need a body to reside in. Since Lu Yang called out my name and revived me, this has engendered a special karmic relationship between us, forcing me to reside within him. Only until this special karmic tie disappears and my immortal soul strengthens can I leave his mental realm.”

Lu Yang pondered, “Is it something similar to a ten-month pregnancy term?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rebuked angrily, “Can’t you raise a more fitting example?!”

Lu Yang shrugged. I lack imagination and can’t think of a better example.

“Alternatively, I can also directly shatter your immortal soul and then resurrect you myself.” Yun Zhi’s gaze landed on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, which the latter felt was like a tremendous pressure weighing down on her.

“That won’t do. How did you learn my name? From Lu Yang. This means that Lu Yang is essentially still the one who resurrected me. Your method wouldn’t work.”

Yun Zhi fell silent for a moment before forming a seal with one hand and casting a golden mark that imprinted itself into Lu Yang’s mental space. It then became fainter, eventually vanishing.

“This is...”

“This is a soul mark I have branded in Lu Yang. As soon as you try to act against him, this mark will be activated and shatter your immortal soul. If that happens, you'll just have to hope some other fool calls out your name correctly another three hundred thousand years later.” Yun Zhi’s tone was thick with warning.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shuddered. “Actually, you don’t have to be so wary of me. After my immortal soul recovers, I can directly reconstruct an immortal body, so I wouldn’t need to take over a body then. Besides, I need to sleep to regain my strength, and I don’t know when I’ll wake up.” She yawned as she spoke.

“Immortals can get sleepy too?” Lu Yang was surprised.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy kept yawning. “Isn’t it all because of the fight just now that depleted most of my strength...” Her eyelids drooped and she began to nod off. “Goodnight, don’t wake me up until the end of the world.”

Yun Zhi confirmed that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was truly asleep before leaving the mental space, manifesting in the real world in her soul state.

“Thank you for going through the trouble, Big Senior Sister!” Meng Jingzhou greeted Yun Zhi with deference he never knew he had.

“Hello, Big Senior Sister.” Man Gu was as honest as ever. Although I have never done anything bad, I don’t know why I can’t help but be scared whenever I see Big Senior Sister.

“Don’t tell anyone about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s resurrection.”

“Yes!” the two of them as well as the old horse chorused.

“Also, don’t dawdle and indulge in fun on the road. Hurry back to the Dao-Seeking Sect!” With that, Yun Zhi’s soul transformed into a streak of light and returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect to continue with the meeting.

The trio put away thoughts of having fun as they got onto the horse carriage and hurriedly left.

“Hmm? Why are we moving so fast?” Through the carriage window, Meng Jingzhou could see that the scenery outside was changing ten times more rapidly than before!

The old horse totally discarded its previously sluggish pace and galloped at lightning speed, employing spatial spells to traverse through space, its speed so rapid that it was almost flying. The journey which would have originally taken several days now took less than half a day to reach the Dao-Seeking Sect.

The old horse could tell that Yun Zhi’s last sentence to hurry back to the Dao-Seeking Sect wasn’t directed at the trio but at itself.

“Haha, Dao-Seeking Sect, I’m back!” Meng Jingzhou spread his arms and guffawed, somewhat feeling like he was a scholar who had returned to his hometown in glorious silk robes.

The three of us have endured humiliation and slaved away in the diabolic creed, arduously pretending to be bad guys. What for? It’s so that we can earn contribution points and show off how amazing we are!

As such, the first thing the trio did upon returning to the Dao-Seeking Sect was to head to the Great Mission Hall to exchange for contribution points. They swaggered in with their heads held high and chests puffed out, disregarding anyone else, as if they were three big crabs that had just come ashore.

Inside the Great Mission Hall, tons of missions gathered from various places plastered the walls, with disciples searching for suitable missions.

Lu Yang noticed that the mission to locate the winged tiger was still up on the wall. It looks like Daoist Li Hong from the Mountain Sea Pass has yet to find his beloved little pet. I no longer see the mission regarding the suspected discovery of a cave domain on Kunwu Mountain, likely because exploration was completed.

There were also new missions available, such as reported sightings of Nascent Soul diabolic cultivators that needed to be eliminated, some discoveries of ancient ruins that required the formation of teams for exploration, and divorce disputes between experts that requested mediation.

The senior male disciple on front desk duty noticed their amusing gait and teased, “Have these three junior brothers saved the world?”

Lu Yang tried to reply modestly, “Pretty much. We’ve just completed a confidential mission and need to report to First Elder.”

The senior male disciple’s expression turned stern. Completing a secret mission is of great importance and not something I can handle. No one would dare joke about such a thing. “First Elder is currently in a meeting in the Discussion Hall. Senior Brother Dai is overseeing the Great Mission Hall for him. What about reporting to him instead?”

The meeting in the Discussion Hall had been ongoing for more than half a day, but there were no signs of it ending anytime soon. The Great Mission Hall was located on Reward Punishment Peak, which First Elder was in charge of. When First Elder wasn’t around, Dai Bufan would sit in for him.

“We’ll have to trouble you to notify him.”

When Dai Bufan heard the message from his junior brother, he was quite baffled. I don’t remember assigning any secret mission to Lu Yang and the others. Could it have been arranged by Shifu? That doesn’t make sense though. Shifu would always inform me about such matters. Suppressing his confusion, he said, “Let them in.”

“Yes.”

The trio were invited into the core zone of the Great Mission Hall. Dai Bufan was reclining in a chair and flipping through documents that summarized intelligence from various places, some of which were possible locations for a mission.

Dai Bufan set down the documents and picked up a teacup filled with freshly brewed Wudao Enlightenment Tea.[1] “Alright, tell me, what have you done?”

Making an effort to sound cultured, Man Gu kept it succinct. “We’ve defected to a diabolic creed.”

“Pft!” Meng Jingzhou shot a glare at Man Gu and clarified, “Don’t listen to Man Gu. We didn’t defect to a diabolic creed; we joined one.”

1. Wudao Tea can be translated literally to ‘Dao Enlightenment Tea.’ ☜

Chapter 107: Weapon for a Confucian Cultivator

In the end, Lu Yang was still the one who stepped forth and succinctly explained the ins and outs of the situation. Had Lu Yang not spoken fast enough, Dai Bufan would have done some purging for the sect. I’ve long wanted to throw you two black sheeps out of the Dao-Seeking Sect! Look at how honest Man Gu was. What has he become after mingling with the two of you?! The first thing he says is that he's with the diabolic creeds.

“So, you joined the Everlasting Creed? And even rose to the rank of Branch Leaders?” Dai Bufan saw them in a new light. A Branch Leader is a middle-level position, and they are qualified to access many secrets, even the specifics of the process of resurrecting the Everlasting Immortal.

The Four Great Diabolic Creeds were top-notch when it came to maintaining secrecy. Dai Bufan had always wanted to find out how the Everlasting Immortal could be revived.

Lu Yang thought to himself, I don’t just know the process. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy is currently sleeping in my mental realm. Speaking of which, since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is residing within me, why should I settle for being a branch leader? I should be the creed leader instead!

“Great, you have done very well!” Dai Bufan slapped his thighs.

It was hard to track down traces of the diabolic creeds as they would guard against the righteous path in every aspect. Struggling to obtain first-hand intelligence, he had wanted to plant people inside, but all attempts had ended in failure.

He never expected Lu Yang and the other two to bring him such a pleasant surprise.

“That person called Tang Yunsheng wants you to go undercover for the Everlasting Creed and infiltrate the Dao-Seeking Sect, right? Then let’s go along with his wishes. Half a month later, the Dao-Seeking Sect will be recruiting a new batch of service staff and expanding our inner entertainment industry, and I shall slip the three of your names into the selected list.” Dai Bufan quickly came to a decision. “As for the Yanjiang Branch...do you have a name list of their members?”

“Yes, we do.” Lu Yang took out the name list he had prepared a long time ago and passed it to Dai Bufan.

Dai Bufan gave Lu Yang a meaningful look. Although this brat can be slippery, he is quick-witted. He knew what I would want and made the necessary preparations beforehand.

“When you get into contact with Tang Yunsheng again, you must put on a convincing facade and try your best to acquire intelligence from the Everlasting Creed. Being spies of the Everlasting Creed is in itself a mission, so you don't have to complete the annual requirement of three missions like everyone else.

“As for your contribution points, the highest reward possible for a Foundation Establishment mission is one thousand. You exterminated two tiger demons, four diabolic creed members, including one at the Advanced Golden Core Stage, and successfully prevented the Lifespan-Reversal Array from activating. Your contributions are immense.

“The two Foundation Establishment tiger demons and three Foundation Establishment diabolic creed members will be counted as seven hundred and fifty points.

“Slaying Branch Leader Chu and stopping the Lifespan-Reversal Array will be counted as one thousand contribution points.

“Infiltrating the diabolic creed and becoming a branch leader will also be counted as one thousand contribution points.

“Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu, that will make it 2750 contribution points in total. Lu Yang, you performed excellently throughout this mission. On top of the 2750 contribution points, I will grant you an additional two hundred and fifty points, which sums that up to three thousand contribution points.”

The trio’s eyebrows were arched in elation, dazed by the whopping number of contribution points they have received. We can now buy many things we wanted on the rewards board, enough for us to splurge for a while.

“If you obtain further intelligence on the Everlasting Creed, you will also be rewarded with contribution points.”

Once Dai Bufan finished instructing them on some confidentiality matters, Dai Bufan dismissed the three.

After Lu Yang left, he bumped into a familiar face in the Great Mission Hall—Senior Brother Li Dan, who had previously recommended weapons to him. Next to the fierce-looking Li Dan was a petite senior female disciple.

“Senior Brother Li Dan,” Lu Yang and Man Gu greeted.

Lu Yang and Man Gu looked at each other in surprise, not expecting the other party to know Li Dan.

Man Gu introduced, “This is Senior Brother Li Dan, the one who spent a hundred contribution points to buy my barbeque recipe.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou immediately connected the dots. Man Gu had previously mentioned that a senior brother bought his barbeque recipe and won the heart of a senior sister with it.

“Hello,” Li Dan greeted them with a smile that grew increasingly malevolent-looking.

Suddenly, Dai Bufan used his spiritual consciousness to summon Li Dan. “Junior Brother Li Dan, Junior Sister Ding Xiang, come over here for a moment. I have a mission that is suitable for you two.”

“We have to leave first. Senior Brother Dai is calling for us.” Li Dan and Ding Xiang hurriedly took their leave.

~~~

Dai Bufan passed the Everlasting Creed’s roster to the two of them. “This is the name list of Everlasting Creed members I have obtained through special means. However, specific addresses aren’t recorded. I need both of you to make a trip to Yanjiang Commandery, locate everyone on this roster, and strive to annihilate them in one fell swoop.”

“Yes!” The two were delighted. Dai Bufan’s mission had come at the right time; they no longer had to go through the frustration of deciding which mission to take on.

“Get ready and set off.”

“Understood!”

“Hold on, there’s one more thing,” Dai Bufan called them before they left. “Don’t open a barbeque shop when you’re undercover in Yanjiang Commandery.”

“Ah? Oh.”

~~~

Lu Yang asked Man Gu, “What do you want to buy?”

“I want to buy a weapon suitable for a Confucian cultivator. I can’t use Brother Meng as a weapon every time I fight.”

Meng Jingzhou felt somewhat offended.

Lu Yang spotted an interesting weapon. “What do you think of this fan? It has poems written on it. Fanning it gently can unleash a wind blade, and there are even Soul-Shattering Needles hidden within, which can also be secretly shot out when unleashing the wind blades.”

“It feels too refined. Is there something that feels more powerful?”

“How about this Dark Sand Iron Hammer? It is forged from Dark Sand Iron, weighs two thousand jin and has a Weight Augmentation Array embedded in it. When you swing it down, its weight will be augmented, and when you swing it up, the augmentation will disappear. A powerful swing can crush hills, and no Foundation Establishment cultivator would dare to take a hit from it. It costs seven hundred and eighty contribution points.”

Man Gu was a little tempted, finding the weapon similar to his combat style, but he still declined it.

“That doesn’t work either. I want a weapon for Confucian cultivators.”

Lu Yang wasn’t discouraged. He scrolled through the rewards board until the end and found something good.

“Sleep Talisman. It contains the full text of Words of Sages to be recited and has the effect of promoting sleep. It costs one contribution point.

“Stick this talisman on the iron hammer so that during a battle, the iron hammer will automatically play the content of Words of Sages. Wouldn’t this iron hammer then be the perfect weapon for a Confucian cultivator?”

Man Gu’s eyes lit up. Brother Lu really knows how to think out of the box. Why didn’t I think of such a good idea?

“I’m buying it!” Man Gu spent 781 points to purchase his beloved weapon.

Swinging his large iron hammer which had quotes of sages on its handle, Man Gu felt that it was obvious at first glance that he was a Confucian cultivator.

Since Meng Jingzhou didn’t need to buy any weapon, he bought a few carts of premium fodder to reward his old horse.

Lu Yang bought a few items that might come in handy during battles.

White Bone Flesh Regeneration Pill—if one had their flesh sliced off in battle, ingesting this pill would allow them to instantly regrow the chunk of flesh and regain their strength.

Golden Light Incantation—it would form a protective golden light and withstand several attacks during battle, protecting the entire body. Its effects were better than the shaobing from the dining hall.

Lu Yang felt that the Golden Light Incantation was a good item and bought ten in one go.

Automatic Self-Cleaning Garment—clothes that could remain pristine even without the use of the Garment-Cleansing Spell. It was an essential piece of clothing for eating Sichuan Hotpot.

Plus, these clothes are considered to have been refined, so there won’t be problems of an enemy taking them away with their storage ring.

Lu Yang planned ahead thoroughly, worried that his opponents would be as imaginative as he was.

Chapter 108: Remove This Talisman, and Your Shifu Can Come Out

When Lu Yang returned to Heaven’s Gate Peak, he still didn’t see Yun Zhi around; only the puppet was guarding the place.

“Why is the meeting taking so long this time? It probably has to do with the allocation of spirit stones, right?”

Based on Lu Yang’s impression, only a situation like this would warrant such a lengthy meeting. The elders always have a multitude of strange ideas which are limited by the availability of spirit stones. Whenever an opportunity to obtain spirit stones arises, they will definitely fight to the end with all sorts of reasoning.

Just then, he saw eight beams of light flying out from the Discussion Hall, signifying that the eight elders had departed. Yun Zhi sauntered out of the Great Hall leisurely as the meeting adjourned.

“Back already?”

“Just got back.”

Yun Zhi used her spiritual consciousness to scan Lu Yang, verifying that Huang Doudou was still sleeping in his mental realm. “There are still many points of doubt regarding the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Perhaps even she herself may not know the answers to these questions. I will be going out to visit some friends to see if I can make any headway. Cultivate diligently here on Heaven’s Gate Peak and aim to reach the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage as fast as possible.”

“Understood.”

Yun Zhi said nothing more and flew into the sky, her figure becoming blurred and leaving Lu Yang clueless about her destination.

After Yun Zhi was gone, Lu Yang turned to the puppet that had once accompanied him in his cultivation training, eager to spar with it. However, he was soon beaten to a pulp.

I can’t even defeat a puppet. Overwhelmed with the feeling of failure, Lu Yang decided to obediently sit down in a meditative state and cultivate. Big Senior Sister is busily on the move to attend to my matters; I can’t afford to be lazy.

“Is this my disciple? Has my disciple returned?”

A ghost-like whisper streamed into Lu Yang’s ears. He instinctively covered his ears but realized that it did nothing to help. The voice held unfathomable power.

“Who is it!” Lu Yang examined his surroundings warily. I don’t remember having any shifu. It has been Big Senior Sister guiding me all this time.

Wait, I think I do have a shifu.

“Lu Yang, you’re back. I’m your shifu, the Taciturn Daoist Priest.”

It was the current sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Taciturn Daoist Priest, who had disappeared for ten years. Despite his absence, the Dao-Seeking Sect had operated smoothly and even recruited a new batch of disciples, as if there was practically no difference between having a sect leader and not having one.

“Shifu?!” Lu Yang was astonished. Even after becoming the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple for a year, he still hadn’t met his master once. Big Senior Sister always said that Shifu is in seclusion and has no time to meet me. Could it be that he is finally done with his seclusion?

“It’s me. Although you’ve never met me, I’ve always been paying attention to you. I am very glad that you were able to draw qi into your body and have also successfully broken through to the Foundation Establishment Stage.” The voice was filled with the sense of the vicissitudes of life, sounding like it belonged to a benevolent old grandfather.

“Shifu, where are you? Are you in seclusion and unable to come out to meet me?” Lu Yang felt that something was amiss. If Shifu can see me and talk to me, why hasn’t there been any news from him in the past year?

The voice sighed deeply, as if it carried an ineffable bitterness. “This is a long story. I have always been on Heaven’s Gate Peak, but I’m temporarily unable to leave my current position. Some things can’t be explained in a few words. Just follow the route I’m about to tell you, and you’ll get to see me.”

Despite Lu Yang’s misgivings, he figured there wouldn’t be any danger. After all, this is Heaven’s Gate Peak, and he is my shifu. Most importantly, Big Senior Sister has never warned me about matters like this. If there were any danger, Big Senior Sister would have told me a long time ago.

“First, you need to locate the pine forest halfway up the mountain. There is a three-hundred-meter tall ancient pine tree, the largest in the entire pine grove.”

Lu Yang quickly found the ancient pine tree the Taciturn Daoist Priest mentioned. He remembered that the puppet had previously picked the pine nuts from here and made pine nut corn for him, which was very delicious.

“Gently knock on the ancient pine three times, pause for three seconds, and then knock three more times.”

Lu Yang followed the instructions and saw that a spatial distortion had occurred to the east of the ancient pine, as if a piece of camouflage cloth had been removed, revealing the truth behind it. A huge area of pine trees had vanished, replaced with a pitch-black cave abode with a radiant gold talisman affixed at the entrance; it was hard to miss it. The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s voice had emitted from within this cave abode.

Lu Yang tentatively called out, “Shifu?”

“Ah, good disciple. We finally meet.” An elderly man with a celestial deportment walked out from the cave abode with a horsetail whisk[1] resting on his arm, as if he was an immortal that had descended from above. Upon laying his eyes on Lu Yang, he grew visibly excited. So this is my youngest disciple?

The Taciturn Daoist Priest stopped at the entrance, not taking another step forward.

“Shifu, what’s the matter? Are you trapped here? When Big Senior Sister comes back, I’ll ask her to rescue you!” Lu Yang anxiously said.

“No no no,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest immediately stopped Lu Yang. If Yun Zhi hadn’t left Heaven’s Gate Peak, I wouldn’t have dared to call Lu Yang over.

“Don’t tell your Big Senior Sister that you have met me.”

“Why is that?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest looked up at the ceiling of the cave, his gaze complicated. “One lives for nothing but fame and fortune. As the sect leader of one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, I wield tremendous power, and naturally, it would attract the attention of many people who wish to take my place. That I can understand. Back then, I also had to go through harrowing battles before emerging victorious among my senior and junior brothers.

“I originally thought that everything would be resolved after I became the sect leader, but I never expected that I would be betrayed by those closest to me.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest revealed an expression of agony, as if he was reluctant to recall the past but was forced to relive those memories. “Your Big Senior Sister is exceptionally gifted. After I step down, the position of sect leader will definitely belong to her, but she couldn’t even wait for that day to come, breaking our promise and imprisoning me here, while she took over as acting sect leader to manage all affairs of the sect.

“How has the sect been the past ten years? Did your Big Senior Sister follow the plans I outlined?”

Lu Yang was astounded. I’ve heard a few senior brothers and sisters say that the sect has been flourishing by the day and thriving with exuberance during these ten years and that most of the credit belongs to Big Senior Sister. Could all of this have been based on Shifu’s plans?

Lu Yang relayed the truth, to which the Taciturn Daoist Priest replied with a tinge of comfort in his voice, “Little Yun has done well. Even without me, she can still manage the sect smoothly. It’s just a pity...”

“What’s a pity?”

“It’s just a pity that I’m not personally managing the sect. If it were me, I would have better management strategies.”

“Then can you come out?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest smiled bitterly as he attempted to walk out of the cave abode. As soon as he took one step forward, countless bolts of purple lightning burst forth from the entrance, enveloping the Taciturn Daoist Priest. He instantly retreated in fright, using the horsetail whisk to extinguish the flames on his body.

“You saw that, right? I can’t come out.”

“Then how do I rescue you?”

“There’s a golden talisman written by Little Yun at the entrance of the cave abode. You just have to remove it, and I’ll be able to come out.”

Lu Yang eyed the Taciturn Daoist Priest suspiciously. “That simple?”

“It’s that simple. Little Yun said that as long as someone removes the talisman, it signifies that I’m not destined to be imprisoned here, and I will naturally have to be let out to comply with heaven’s will.”

Lu Yang leaned in to take a closer look, only to see that it lacked the strange patterns that one would normally see on a talisman. Instead, it only bore seven huge words left by Yun Zhi.

Let me see who dares remove this.

1. Fuchen or horsetail whisk ☜

Chapter 109: The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s Past

Lu Yang silently retreated a few steps back in an attempt to prove that he completely had no intention of removing the talisman. Even if Big Senior Sister were to suddenly descend from the heavens, I can also disassociate myself from this situation. This is probably what they mean by “even a gentleman knows not to stand beneath a dangerous wall.”

Although there was not a trace of spirit energy on the talisman by Yun Zhi and removing it didn’t seem to pose any danger, Lu Yang just didn’t dare to take it down.

I’ll only remove this talisman if I have given up on living. Shifu, it’s not that your disciple is unfilial. It’s simply because I only have one life. There’s also an immortal inside my mental space. If Big Senior Sister beats me to death, that would result in two deaths. Not worth it.

When the Taciturn Daoist Priest saw Lu Yang’s hesitating, he naturally knew what Lu Yang’s concerns were. He was not surprised since Lu Yang wasn’t the first one to exhibit such a reaction. The Taciturn Daoist Priest chuckled. “It’s understandable that you don’t understand me. You can inquire about me from the other elders so that you can gain a more comprehensive understanding of me. Then you’ll know that what I’m saying is not false.

“However, don’t tell them about how Little Yun has imprisoned me. Since Little Yun has managed the sect for ten years, some elders may not necessarily be on my side.”

Lu Yang thought that his words made sense. I only know that my shifu is the Taciturn Daoist Priest, but I have never carefully thought about what kind of person he is. Maybe this is an opportunity. With that in mind, he left the pine forest.

After Lu Yang was gone, the Taciturn Daoist Priest scratched his head. I’ve asked several people to remove the talisman, but no one was willing to do so.

“Is there something written on the talisman that’s making them so scared?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest mumbled to himself as he craned his neck to look at the talisman but to no avail.

~~~

Lu Yang returned to the Great Mission Hall once more, only to be told that First Elder was out on business, so he could only make his way to the Impartation Peak, where Second Elder was.

The Impartation Peak was responsible for teaching some basic cultivation knowledge. Back when Lu Yang had just joined the Dao-Seeking Sect, he had crammed there for a month, but he had never seen Second Elder.

“Senior Brother, may I know if Second Elder is here?” Lu Yang asked a disciple on duty at the Impartation Peak.

The senior male disciple looked at Lu Yang with a strange gaze. “You’re looking for Second Elder? Then you should head to the herb garden. He’s the one lying at the entrance.”

Lu Yang was startled. He never expected that the Grandpa Ba who had made him dig in the herb garden was Second Elder.

He thanked the senior male disciple and arrived at the herb garden. Grandpa Ba is indeed here.

“Hmm? Back for more digging?” Grandpa Ba asked cheerfully.

“No, I just wanted to ask about my shifu.”

“Old Nine? Of course, I know.” Grandpa Ba immediately perked up.

“Old Nine?”

“That’s right, from First Elder to Eighth Elder and then to your master, the Taciturn Daoist Priest, we were all taught by the same master. Your master is the youngest and joined the sect the latest, so he is ranked ninth.

“Old Nine is a chatterbox, always babbling away nonstop. Have you seen the Introduction to Xiangsheng Comedy on the first floor of the scripture library? That was donated by Old Nine.”

Lu Yang nodded. He vividly remembered how he was stunned for a long time when he saw the book, thinking that he had entered the wrong place.

“Later, our shifu really didn’t want to hear Old Nine speak anymore, so he gave him the title of ‘Taciturn Daoist Priest,’ hoping that he’d speak less.”

Lu Yang asked, “Did it work?”

“No, it didn’t. Old Nine said, ‘Confucius is taciturn about the supernatural, as long as I am taciturn and don’t talk about the supernatural, I’ll be fine.’ Then that mouth of his continued blabbering away; what he needs is to have his mouth sewn up.

“However, Old Nine’s cultivation talent was the strongest among the nine of us, though, of course, he can’t compare to Yun Zhi. I reckon that Yun Zhi’s talent is rare even throughout history.
