“After our shifu went to live in isolation, the nine of us discussed who should be the sect leader, and we unanimously agreed that Old Nine should be the one. With his silver tongue, he would definitely do the job well. However, Old Nine adamantly refused, so we suggested going by the rules of the jianghu. Whoever was stronger would decide, and Old Nine agreed.

“Then the eight of us ganged up and gave Old Nine a beating, forcing him to become the sect leader.”

Lu Yang recalled the “harrowing battles” his master had mentioned. I can’t say that’s completely inaccurate.

“Our judgment was indeed spot on. Old Nine had the talent for management, keeping the sect in order and sweeping away the previously gloomy atmosphere. This could also have been related to this personality.

“Then, I don’t know what happened, but ten years ago, Yun Zhi suddenly came to us and said that she would be the one managing the sect from then on. Thinking that the time for the younger generation would eventually come around, taking over the reins earlier might not be a bad thing, so we just let her take charge if she wanted to.

“As for where Old Nine went, we didn’t really pay attention. After all, he’s almost two thousand years old and his mind is even more agile than that of young people. Who knows, maybe he’s alive and kicking somewhere? He couldn’t possibly have gotten lost, right?” The concept of time for a formidable cultivator like Grandpa Ba was different from the masses. Ten years was not a long time for them.

After bidding goodbye to Grandpa Ba, Lu Yang went to the Physique Refinement Peak to look for Third Elder. As Meng Jingzhou was around, he quickly found Third Elder with his help.

Third Elder was currently at the edge of the fields playing chess with the old ancestor of the Blue-Eyed Water Buffalo clan. His short stature would have made it a challenge to associate him with a top-tier physique cultivator had Lu Yang met him somewhere else. However, Lu Yang knew that terrifying power was harbored within Third Elder, capable of moving mountains and filling seas as if it were just the flick of a finger. The “Heaven-Shaking Six Forms” he created was highly acclaimed among physique cultivators, all who wished to learn even a fraction of it. Countless people wanted to become Third Elder’s disciple but were unable to.

Lu Yang had also tried to search the fields for the ten water buffaloes he had once summoned, only to find that all the buffaloes looked alike to him.

“You’re asking about Old Nine? Haha, you’ve come to the right person! I’m the one who picked him up and raised him on poop and urine!” Third Elder had an expression that seemed to say “You’re lucky that you met me.”

Meng Jingzhou softly reminded by the side, “Shifu, it’s not ‘raising him on’ but ‘raising him through.’”

Third Elder waved his hand impatiently. “Whatever, it doesn’t make a difference. Stop being nitpicky about wordings like Old Four.

“Old Nine was known to be clever. He was the first among us to learn the spell ‘Size At Will.’ As the name suggests, it allows one to become big or smaller in size. Old Nine wondered if he could modify it to localize the effects to a part of the body. It wouldn’t have to grow too big, just one or two inches would suffice. Not only would it be convenient, easier to use, and require less power, but it would also surely be very popular between men and women. The men could use it for below and the women for above.

“Following this line of thought, he actually developed it successfully.” Third Elder slapped his thigh, praising the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s ingenious idea.

“Later, he wrote a book on a new spell called Size At Will (Localized Version). As soon as it was released, people went wild over it. At that time, we earned quite a lot of spirit stones. Whenever we went out for a meal, we could order the most expensive items on the menu, and we wouldn’t even bother to pick up the spirit stones that we accidentally dropped.

“Unfortunately, good times don’t last long. The Great Xia Dynasty soon came forth and banned the sale of this spell.”

“Why is that?”

“They said that it was classified as obscene material.”

Lu Yang muttered, “...It doesn’t seem like they’re entirely wrong.”

Chapter 110: Translation of Ancient Sayings

It was evident that Third Elder was full of praise and admiration for the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Perhaps it was because Third Elder was the type to envy others for having whatever he lacked.

After bidding goodbye to Third Elder, Lu Yang now arrived at Gentleman Peak.

Gentleman Peak was Fourth Elder’s territory. The mountain was cool and refreshing, akin to a painting of elegance. One could easily spot pavilions and streams wherever they ambled through, while the emerald green bamboo stood tall and straight. It was clear at first glance that this was a place favored by scholars and literati who would linger around and compose poems. Even if the bamboos were to suddenly start reciting a few lines from the sages, Lu Yang wouldn’t be surprised at all.

Having witnessed all kinds of strange things in the Dao-Seeking Sect, Lu Yang’s mental fortitude had reached an all-time high.

He even saw black-and-white Iron-Eating Beasts[1] tumbling around in the mountains. On the other hand, senior male disciples drank wine and made merry as they freely moved their brush and let the ink flow, bringing the canvas to life. They then dived into the paintings themselves and frolicked around with the people inside, unfettered and at ease.

An Iron-Eating Beast even nudged Lu Yang until he almost fell over. It was trying to play with Lu Yang, but the latter had business to attend to, so he could only try his best to reason with the beast until it finally let him go, even giving him a half-eaten piece of bamboo as a parting gift.

“Hello, Senior Brother. May I ask where Fourth Elder is?” Lu Yang respectfully inquired while still holding the half-eaten bamboo.

This senior male disciple possessed an absolutely terrifying level of mastery in the Dao of Painting, where his works were almost indistinguishable from reality.

Upon hearing Lu Yang, the senior male disciple extended half of his body out of the painting. “Who are you?”

“I am Lu Yang.”

The dots connected once he heard Lu Yang’s name. “Oh, I know you. You’re the newcomer, Lu Yang, Yun Zhi’s disciple.”

“...Big Senior Sister accepted me as a disciple on behalf of my shifu. I am the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple,” Lu Yang corrected the senior male disciple earnestly.

“I’m Ji Hongwen. I was from the same batch as Big Senior Sister when we joined the Dao-Seeking Sect. I am Fourth Elder’s first disciple.” Ji Hongwen didn’t put on any airs around him and judged Lu Yang for his low cultivation.

“Nice to meet you, Senior Brother Ji.” Lu Yang was surprised to hear that Ji Hongwen was in the same cohort as Yun Zhi. He only knew that Dai Bufan was in the same cohort as Yun Zhi and the most senior of the disciples, commanding great respect among them. His cultivation was nearly on par with the elders, and First Elder was also very confident in his management of affairs.

Lu Yang hadn’t expected to encounter someone else from this same cohort. By extension, Senior Brother Ji’s cultivation is likely not low either.

Those big shots people in the outer world couldn’t meet were commonplace in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“You want to meet Shifu? Let’s go, he is probably teaching students right now.” Ji Hongwen drifted out from the painting. With a flick of his finger, another person appeared within the painting.

Only then did Lu Yang notice that Ji Hongwen wasn’t the only one in the painting; there was another captivatingly beautiful woman. The woman seemed to have walked straight out of the water towns in Jiangnan.[2] She appeared gentle and graceful, her cheeks tinged with a soft blush. Dimples adorned her smiling visage which resembled a blooming flower, while her eyes seemed to convey a river of emotions. Not only was her beauty peerless, her attire was also bold and revealing, causing even an innocent young man like Lu Yang to blush.

“Haha, is she beautiful? I painted her. Do you want me to paint one for you too? She can even accompany you to sleep at night,” Ji Hongwen teased.

Lu Yang quickly shook his head. I must protect my kidney’s vitality well.

The beautiful woman clung to Ji Hongwen’s arm, gazing at him with deep affection.

What Lu Yang didn’t know was that there were more people who wanted to learn this skill of Ji Hongwen than those who wanted to learn Third Elder’s “Heaven-Shaking Six Forms.”

Following Ji Hongwen’s lead, Lu Yang found himself in the depths of the bamboo forest, where there was actually a private school. Inside was the model teacher Fourth Elder, Man Gu, who embodied the idea of how rotten wood couldn’t be carved, and a bunch of random people paying attention to the lesson conscientiously.

Fourth Elder was explaining the meaning of ancient texts, “...Gazing to the southwest of the creek, it meanders like the Big Dipper and roves like a snake, sections of it bright and visible. The banks jut out like canine teeth, the source ever shrouded in mystery.[3] Come, Man Gu, translate this part. What does it mean by ‘The banks jut out like canine teeth, the source ever shrouded in mystery?’”

Man Gu lowered his head and pondered carefully before answering in a tone full of certainty, “There are two dogs fighting by the banks, and no one knows why.”

Fourth Elder silently closed the ancient book, rolled up his sleeves, and took out a ruler. Just as he was about to smack the back of Man Gu’s hand, he recalled the sages’ sincere teachings—education for all without discrimination and tailored pedagogy according to abilities. I have seen all of Man Gu’s diligent efforts in his studies. He’s a good child. What just happened should be an accident. I’ll ask him an easier question. If he gets it right, I won’t have to hit him, and that would help him save face.

“‘All those aristocrats in power, are they truly born to be superior.’[4] What does this mean?”

According to historical records, when the Great Yu Dynasty collapsed one hundred thousand years ago, the princes and aristocrats stepped forth, raising their banners in full display, seeking to reunify the world and restore the Great Yu Dynasty’s rule. The people firmly believed in the concept of bloodlines, thinking that the lineage of the Great Yu Dynasty was born noble, and the aristocrats’ claims successfully garnered a significant following.

However, the Great Xia Emperor’s ancestor was aware of how rotten these aristocrats were at their core, having suffered greatly at their hands. These people thought they were high above the rest, indulging in luxury and pleasure, completely out of touch with the sufferings of the common folk and the struggles of cultivation. Showered with myriad rare natural treasures since birth, their cultivation easily soared, and they were practically almost becoming rare natural treasures themselves. Even if these people could rebuild the Great Yu Dynasty, it would quickly decay once more.

As a visionary and sagacious individual, the Great Xia Emperor’s ancestor raised his arm and shouted, “All those aristocrats in power, are they truly born to be superior?’” This phrase became a timeless one, enduring through the ages.

Even Man Gu, a member of the Barbarian Tribe had heard of this phrase, held great admiration and respect for the valor of the Great Xia Emperor’s ancestors. “This phrase means ‘All those aristocrats in power, are you truly born with more balls?”

The whole hall erupted in laughter.

All signs of hesitation vanished from Fourth Elder as he slapped Man Gu’s hand with the ruler, causing the latter to grimace in pain.

However, Man Gu was still baffled about what he had done wrong. The Great Xia Emperor’s ancestor dared to challenge the aristocrats openly. Imagine the huge amount of courage that must have taken! But is that not what this phrase is trying to say?

Lu Yang who had been standing at the entrance all this while observed three seconds of silence to mourn for Man Gu.

Ji Hongwen couldn’t help but shake his head and laugh. “I really don’t know what Junior Brother Man Gu is thinking. As a member of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, instead of learning from Third Elder, he chose to become our shifu’s disciple. He certainly has had his fair share of beatings this year. That said, I realized that his mind seems to be sharper ever since he returned from his mission. Do you know why?”

Lu Yang shook his head. How would I know?

Faced with Ji Hongwen’s suspicious gaze, Lu Yang hurriedly changed the topic. “By the way, there seems to be a hidden rhythm to how Fourth Elder is hitting the back of the hand, or is it just me?”

Ji Hongwen looked at Lu Yang, slightly astonished. “You’re not mistaken. This is actually a method to stimulate the bloodline, but the pain is too unbearable for most. Shifu is using this tactic to stimulate the Ancient Barbarian Bloodline in Junior Brother Man Gu. By the way, don’t tell this to Junior Brother Man Gu.”

Lu Yang nodded.

“When Shifu gets off from class, you can look for him then.” Ji Hongwen then grabbed the beautiful woman’s hand and walked away.

Classes always seemed to drag on for eternity. Lu Yang continued listening from the entrance, and although Fourth Elder had taught for merely a quarter of an hour, Lu Yang felt as if several hours had passed. Finally, Fourth Elder wrapped up the class, and that was when he encountered the inquisitive Lu Yang.

“You’re asking what kind of person Old Nine is, the one who is full of mischief, always up to no good, and brimming with scheming ideas?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Thank you, I think I already have a pretty good idea of what kind of person my shifu is.

1. ”Iron-Eating Beast” was the name for pandas in ancient times. ☜

2. Jiangnan is renowned for scholarly and refined vibes. ☜

3. A poem from Liu Zongyuan. ☜

4. This is actually a rather famous phrase. The meaning has already been translated in the text. ☜

Chapter 111: And He Still Expects To Be Let Out?

Fourth Elder’s attire was that of a typical Confucian cultivator—unsullied white robes with a paper fan in hand. He had a steady gait and bore a gentle demeanor when interacting with others, handling matters thoroughly and treating his students fairly.

He advised Lu Yang, “You should keep your distance from Old Nine. Fortunately, he has been missing recently and you dodged an arrow. You have to cherish the opportunity to learn from Yun Zhi. There’s no future in learning from Old Nine.

“The sages say that a gentleman has five virtues: benevolence, righteousness, propriety, wisdom, and trustworthiness. These have nothing to do with Old Nine. There are no misdeeds he doesn’t engage in. I can’t remember how many times I’ve had to rescue him from prison. Do you know what your master’s unique art in Sword Dao is?”

Lu Yang answered, “I heard from Big Senior Sister that it is ‘One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords.’ Once fully unleashed, one sword can generate tens and thousands of swords, resembling a patch of dark clouds overshadowing a city and blocking out the skies while looking down on all. After the enemies are slaughtered, the ten thousand swords will return to one, with not even a single drop of blood.” Back when Lu Yang had listened to Yun Zhi’s description, he looked forward to it, thinking that this was the quintessence of a sword cultivator’s carefreeness.

Fourth Elder nodded. “That’s right, One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords. As someone with a Sword Spirit Root, Old Nine was indeed a rare genius in Sword Dao. Very few sword cultivators can currently reach his level.”

Lu Yang was puzzled. I can’t help but feel that there’s something indescribable in Fourth Elder’s tone...a combination of gnashing his teeth in anger, shame of being associated with him, and frustration at the disappointment he is?

That seems about right.

Fourth Elder continued, “Once, Old Nine unleashed his sword technique and transformed one sword into ten thousand swords, then sold them to the Luodi Merchant Guild. After receiving the payment, he reverted the swords back to one. If it weren’t for me intervening and mollifying the person in charge, your shifu would still be rotting in jail now!”

Lu Yang was stunned speechless. Shifu is actually locked up right now, so I suppose that counts as reaping what he sowed.

“Also, have you heard of the spell Size At Will (Localized Version)?” Fourth Elder asked.

“I just heard about it from Third Elder.”

“Don’t spread the news of the spell. Many young disciples nowadays are unaware of its existence. If it were a hundred years ago, the new disciples would be fighting to become Old Nine’s disciple just to learn this spell. Fortunately, Junior Niece Yun Zhi had the foresight to destroy the book. The original version is kept on the upper levels of the scripture library, and with deliberate attempts to conceal it, we no longer have disciples clamoring to learn such a spell.” Fourth Elder showed a doleful expression. “Public morality is degenerating by the day.”

Lu Yang was embarrassed to tell Fourth Elder that he actually also wanted to learn the spell.

I’m sorry, I will reflect on myself.

Fourth Elder’s tone softened slightly. “However, Old Nine is not without merits. At the very least, after he became the sect leader, our sect has overall become stronger. Of course, he doesn’t take sole credit. All eight of us made commendable contributions.”

For a moment, Lu Yang was unsure whether Fourth Elder was praising the Taciturn Daoist Priest or himself.

“By the way, why are you suddenly curious about Old Nine?”

Lu Yang chuckled to cover up his awkwardness. “It’s nothing much, really. It’s just that I haven’t seen Shifu ever since I became his disciple, so I was a little curious.”

After asking three people, Lu Yang had roughly figured out what kind of person his master was.

And he still expects to be let out?

~~~

The Heaven Strategy Sect was located on the eastern side of the continent, occupying a massive area. From above, one would realize that the Heaven Strategy Sect resembled an inverted bagua compass, forming a picturesque sight.

It was tranquil and sparsely populated in the Heaven Strategy Sect, like a hidden sect hidden in the deep mountains. In fact, it was so still that it felt eerie. However, the most important reason for the quietness was that they had sent their disciples out to repay debts, leaving hardly anyone in the gargantuan sect. While letting them train their hearts in the mundane world, the sect could also cut down on expenses, killing two birds with one stone.

A shout shattered the silence in the Heaven Strategy Sect.

“Shifu, Shifu, I’m back!” Luo Bu ran into the sect and went straight to find his master.

The sect leader of the Heaven Strategy Sect heard his disciple calling for him and walked out from his cave abode. “Good disciple, why are you back so soon? Have you already come up with a solution to repay all the debts?”

Luo Bu was still panting. “N-not yet. During my travels, I did some divination for others and bumped into a problematic figure. I wanted to come back to notify the sect so that we can be more vigilant.”

“Take a seat and tell me slowly.”

Luo Bu caught his breath before elaborating, “When I traveled to Yanjiang Commandery, I was strapped for money, so I thought I’d randomly do some divinations and scam a few unlucky souls for money. That was when I happened to encounter three disciples from the Dao-Seeking Sect and one from the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, easy lambs for slaughter.

“I originally didn’t intend to do the divinations seriously, thinking that I’d give them a half-hearted reading, but I didn’t expect one of them to be not at all simple. That person’s name is Lu Yang. Although his cultivation is low and he has just begun cultivating, his future is extremely terrifying.”

The Heaven Strategy Sect Sect Leader’s heart stirred. “Are you suggesting that we invest in him early so that he can help us repay our debts when he strikes it rich?”

Luo Bu immediately doused the flames of his master’s frightening thoughts. “No no no! I saw that Lu Yang’s future is destined to have karmic entanglements with several immortals.”

“Karmic entanglements with several immortals?!” the sect leader gasped. Usually, karmic entanglement with just one immortal is already enough to result in death, yet this person called Lu Yang will be deeply entwined in karmic ties with several immortals and still not die? What the Heaven Strategy Sect fears most is having our paths crossed with those with heavy karma as it can be detrimental for transcendence. The heavier the karma, the more challenging cultivation becomes, and struggling to break free will only deepen the karmic entanglements.

“That’s not all! I also discovered that Lu Yang will propagate the bad ethos of the Dao-Seeking Sect throughout the entire cultivation world.”

The sect leader inhaled a sharp breath of cold air. Why didn’t you say such an important thing earlier? Compared to this, what do the karmic entanglements with immortals matter? Karmic ties with immortals imply that he’ll achieve great things in the future, but spreading the bad ethos of the Dao-Seeking Sect means that there is something wrong with his brain!

“In any case, we must try our best to avoid contact with the Dao-Seeking Sect, especially the one called Lu Yang. The further we stay away from them, the better!”

Suddenly, there was a noticeable change in the sect leader’s countenance.

“Shifu, what’s wrong?”

“An extremely boorish and aggressive aura wave is approaching the Heaven Strategy Sect, and I reckon that the visitor bears ill intention! Quickly activate the great defense array first!” The sect leader swiftly came to a decision to activate the Great Sect Defense Array.

The nodes of the array lit up like stars in the night sky, forming the shape of a bagua compass. The enormous bagua compass enveloped the Heaven Strategy Sect, forming an impregnable and complex defense in all eight directions, making it challenging to find a way out. As soon as one was trapped within the array, they could expend a lifetime’s worth of effort but still not solve the array. Countless Fusion experts had returned empty-handed, while the ones harboring devious intentions were trapped until they died; these were a testament to the power of the Heaven Strategy Sect’s Great Sect Defense Array.

However, the visitor exhibited no signs of stopping upon seeing the Heaven Strategy Sect, exuding an overbearing air of arrogance. Despite facing the complicated great array, the visitor smashed it to pieces with just one hand.

Only then did the sect leader of the Heaven Strategy Sect catch a glimpse of the visitor’s appearance—graceful, celestial, and inviolable.

“Yun Zhi of the Dao-Seeking Sect is here to pay respects to the Grand Elder of the Heaven Strategy Sect. May I have an audience?”

The Heaven Strategy Sect Sect Leader’s face turned pallid. Speak of the Dao-Seeking Sect and they will appear.

Chapter 112: The Reason for the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s Imprisonment

Apart from its status as one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Dao-Seeking Sect also had a resounding reputation in the cultivation world—similar to how parents would admonish their children not to play with bad kids, the elders would frequently warn their disciples not to hang out with those from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

However, there would always be disciples who didn’t believe in their warnings and mingled with the Dao-Seeking Sect, bringing great distress to those around them.

One example was Lan Ting.

Fortunately, the higher-ups in the cultivation world knew that the Dao-Seeking Sect was not incorrigible. Ever since the previous sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect disappeared and the new sect leader, Yun Zhi, succeeded him, there had been a visible improvement in the ethos of the Dao-Seeking Sect—it was primarily reflected by how the Dao-Seeking Sect no longer harmed others but only targeted their own members. If one were to view the Dao-Seeking Sect as a mental institution, Yun Zhi would be the director, one of the rare sane individuals.

In any case, having Yun Zhi instead of someone else visiting is still better.

A bright voice echoed from beneath the Heaven Strategy Sect. In the blink of an eye, an elderly figure had appeared before Yun Zhi.

”Dao Amplification Savant,” greeted Yun Zhi with cupped hands.

The Dao Amplification Savant was the Heaven Strategy Sect’s Grand Elder, an antique in the cultivation world where few lived longer than him. He kept a low profile, never revealing his true cultivation.

“Fellow Daoist, why have you come?” The Dao Amplification Savant addressed Yun Zhi as “Fellow Daoist,” not daring to be dismissive toward Yun Zhi.

“I have some questions regarding immortals,” Yun Zhi replied.

“Please come with me.”

“Please go ahead.”

The Dao Amplification Savant invited Yun Zhi into a secret chamber within the sect and poured her some tea.

“Which aspects of immortals would you like to inquire about?” the Dao Amplification Savant asked.

“How much do you know about the Everlasting Immortal?”

A troubled expression spread across the Dao Amplification Savant’s visage as he smiled bitterly. “The Everlasting Immortal? Fellow Daoist, you have asked a good question. The Everlasting Immortal was the most mysterious entity among the Ancient Five Immortals. If it weren’t for the Everlasting Creed confidently claiming that they had discovered an ancient ruin containing records of the Everlasting Immortal, even I wouldn’t have known of their existence.

“However, even if there are ancient relics, they may not necessarily be real. I remain skeptical about the Everlasting Immortal’s existence.”

“Could you elaborate?” Yun Zhi pressed further.

“Relics from over ten thousand years ago may be considered ancient to us now, but does being ancient imply that it is legitimate? I heard that the ancient ruins were products of the Great Qian Dynasty, but what about it? We are already in a new epoch, with the ancient era being several hundred thousand years ago.

“Those with personal agendas could easily conjure an incomprehensible ancient ruin during the Great Qian Dynasty. After one or two hundred thousand years, if someone accidentally stumbles upon it and sees that it is an ancient ruin, they may exclaim in awe and assume that the records within are true.

“If there really was an Everlasting Immortal, then why is there no other supporting evidence apart from this ancient ruin? Numerous cave domains from the Great Qian Dynasty have also been excavated, but why haven’t we seen any records regarding the Everlasting Immortal?”

Yun Zhi nodded, finding that the Dao Amplification Savant’s reasoning did make some sense. “I believe you know that I recently located the headquarters of the Everlasting Creed. Unfortunately, they fled too quickly, and I couldn’t capture a single person. Nonetheless, I managed to glean some information from the materials they left behind.”

In reality, Yun Zhi hadn’t obtained any intelligence from the headquarters, but out of safety considerations for Lu Yang, she didn’t mention any of Lu Yang’s involvement.

“I would like to hear the details,” the Dao Amplification Savant said.

“According to the Everlasting Creed, the special trait of the Everlasting Immortal’s Dao Fruit could be termed as ‘imperishable.’ As long as someone calls out the Everlasting Immortal’s title and immortal name, the Everlasting Immortal can be resurrected,” Yun Zhi expounded.

The Dao Amplification Savant’s pupils constricted, shock written across his face. This is an incredible characteristic! They can’t die even if they want to.

“Every immortal’s Dao Fruit possesses a unique characteristic. Does that mean that this matter is true?” the Dao Amplification Savant lamented before continuing, “However, this is ultimately a one-sided claim by the Everlasting Creed. I stand by my opinion that this is an attempt to create an immortal.

“The method employed is similar to the case of the Great Xia Dynasty’s luck leading to immortal ascension. A mastermind behind the scenes fabricates a non-existent immortal and capitalizes on the Everlasting Creed’s faith. As the faith accumulates, the Everlasting Immortal gradually materializes. Once the power of faith reaches a certain threshold, the Everlasting Immortal will manifest from nothingness.”

Yun Zhi didn’t refute him but listened quietly to his theories. The Everlasting Immortal has already been revived, so they are definitely not creating an immortal, but the theory of creating immortals is not without merits. Maybe the other three diabolic creeds are creating immortals.

Yun Zhi thanked the Dao Amplification Savant and departed gracefully.

The sect leader of the Heaven Strategy Sect approached the Dao Amplification Savant, still shaken by the scene of Yun Zhi tearing through the defense array with her bare hands. “Founding Master, just how strong is Yun Zhi? Has she become an immortal?”

“Don’t ask, I don’t know anything.”

~~~

Yun Zhi had visited many people, with the Dao Amplification Savant being the last. Now that the matter was concluded, she went straight back to the sect.

Meanwhile, Lu Yang had returned to Heaven’s Gate Peak and attempted to find his master once more.

“How did it go? What did my senior brothers say? Did they say that the Dao-Seeking Sect has become more prosperous under my leadership?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest was puffed up with pride. I have made indelible contributions to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Lu Yang looked at his master with a complicated gaze. “Indeed, your contributions are significant, but everyone would rather have Big Senior Sister manage the sect.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s head drooped dejectedly, as if his heart had turned into a pile of ash from losing all hope. “Is that really the case? Oh well, let her take the position of sect leader then. It’s only reasonable for the new generation to replace the older one.

“However, if word gets out that a disciple imprisons their master to usurp power, it would ultimately tarnish the Dao-Seeking Sect’s reputation. Why don’t you let me out? I can run far away and not bring up the matter of the sect leader’s position again, and neither will I ever return to the Dao-Seeking Sect. How does that sound?” the Taciturn Daoist Priest tried to negotiate with Lu Yang.

Lu Yang hesitated, feeling that the Taciturn Daoist Priest made some valid points. Shifu doesn’t seem like someone who would vie for power.

Just as he was contemplating whether to release his master, a cold voice sounded from above him. “Shifu, do you really want to get out so badly?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s expression changed drastically in a dramatic turn of events.

Lu Yang raised his head, surprised to see that Yun Zhi had returned. “Big Senior Sister!”

Yun Zhi acknowledged him softly before landing gently, not sullied by even a speck of dust.

“Shifu, were you deceiving Little Junior Brother just to get out?” Yun Zhi questioned without a trace of warmth, but to the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s ears, her voice sounded like a terrifying volcano about to erupt.

Deceive? Lu Yang’s heart raced. Don’t tell me that everything Shifu told me was a lie? Then what is the truth? The gears in Lu Yang’s head rotated rapidly, and he soon came to a possible conclusion, one that seemed highly plausible!

Shifu had fallen to mad qi deviation., so Big Senior Sister placed righteousness before kin and suppressed Shifu here. Considering that dirty laundry shouldn’t be aired in public, she didn’t disclose the matter of Shifu’s mad qi deviation to the elders. Meanwhile, Shifu took advantage of Big Senior Sister’s absence to transmit an auditory message to me and sweet-talked me into removing the talisman so that he could wreak chaos in the world.

That was a close shave. Luckily, Big Senior Sister came in the nick of time.

Yun Zhi continued to say, “Look at the other sect leaders, they’re all diligently cultivating. Now look at yourself, idling away the whole day. Have you finished the daily cultivation homework I assigned you? Have you made any breakthroughs in your cultivation realm?” she reproached. “You’ve not completed a single thing, and yet you still want to come out and play?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest stammered, unable to utter a single word.

Lu Yang, “...”

What on earth was I thinking just now? How could such a melodramatic thing happen in the Dao-Seeking Sect?!

Chapter 113: Lu Yang’s Three Rounds of Questions

“Y-you can’t exactly say that. Cultivation emphasizes work-life balance. As they say, extreme stillness breeds restlessness. When you stay in a place for too long, you can’t help but want to go out and take a look.

“Little Yun, think about it. Isn’t cultivation all about achieving immortality and carefreeness? If one spends all their time in seclusion and sitting in a meditative position to cultivate, wouldn’t cultivation become a prison sentence? That’s putting the cart before the horse,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest advised earnestly.

As a frequent visitor of the prison, I have the right of speech toward imprisonment that no one else has.

“Besides, isn’t cultivation divided into secular cultivators and secluded cultivators? I’m the typical secular cultivator. Only by mingling around in the mundane world can I comprehend the Immortal Dao and break through!”

Lu Yang had heard of this viewpoint before. For instance, the cultivators who entered the imperial court of the Great Xia Dynasty as officials were considered secular cultivators, while the cultivators from the Five Great Immortal Sects tended to be secluded cultivators, though only a few were pure secluded cultivators like Yun Zhi.

No matter how flowery the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s words were, Yun Zhi remained unmoved, not even lifting her eyelids. “Shifu, back when you taught me, you told me that only with pressure comes motivation. Cultivation requires diligence, and the day’s plan should span across morning, afternoon, and night, while a year’s plan should span across spring, summer, autumn, and winter.”

And that was what Yun Zhi followed through with. She would cultivate from morning to night assiduously. As she was already a rare genius, combined with her hard work, her cultivation progressed rapidly. By the time the Immortal Sect Tournament was held, Yun Zhi pulled ahead right away, easily clinching the first position.

As was customary, the sect leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects would critique the shortcomings of the victor, while some sect leaders might also be worried that the victor would become arrogant, so they would join the arena for a battle with the victor.

That was when the five sect leaders suffered a crushing defeat at the hands of Yun Zhi.

When the next Immortal Sect Tournament came around, while the immortal sect disciples were struggling through battles, Yun Zhi was sitting in a sect leader’s seat as a critic; in fact, she was sitting right in the middle.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest grumbled inwardly, Isn’t that because I wanted you to cultivate diligently, quickly enhance your cultivation, and take over my position as sect leader so that I can sneak out to have fun?

Naturally, the Taciturn Daoist Priest would never verbalize such thoughts unless he had a death wish.

Yun Zhi was not averse to cultivation. On the contrary, she enjoyed the process. When she was cultivating, she felt an unprecedented peace, as if she had merged into one with the world, allowing her to distinctly sense herself continuously becoming stronger. After she was done training, her mind would become clear and invigorated, so she saw no harm in continuing to cultivate.

“Never mind, since you want to come out, then come out...” Yun Zhi said calmly, seeming to give in.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was overjoyed. All my efforts and saliva haven’t been in vain. Is Little Yun finally willing to let me out?

“By your own abilities,” Yun Zhi completed the second half of the sentence and turned to leave.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s mouth was agape, completely dumbstruck. If I could get out by my own abilities, I would have done that a long time ago!

“Lu Yang, you...” He wanted to ask Lu Yang to plead for him, but Lu Yang wore an expression that seemed to say, “Shifu, you’re on your own, good luck.” He then hurriedly scurried after Yun Zhi.

On one side is the omnipotent Big Senior Sister who dominates over the Dao-Seeking Sect, while on the other side is my Shifu who has been dominated. It’s very easy to choose which side to stand on.

“Little disciple, don’t go! As long as you remove the talisman, I’ll teach you the technique of One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords. Imagine tens of thousands of swords hovering in the air, their sharp, gleaming tips pointing downward. The imposing aura will give you an edge even before the battle begins!”

“Can it defeat Big Senior Sister?” Lu Yang scampered back. Which sword cultivator wouldn’t want to learn one or two cool and flashy sword techniques? What is power when there is style!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest shook his head, so Lu Yang wanted to leave again.

He quickly stopped Lu Yang, “I can teach you The True Insight to Sword Dao. It can deepen your understanding of the sword Dao, and when your swordsmanship has reached an apex, you can break all spells with one sword. None will dare take a strike of your sword! You’ll be invincible among those at the same rank!”

“Can it defeat Big Senior Sister?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest shook his head, so Lu Yang wanted to leave again.

He quickly stopped Lu Yang again, “I can also teach you the Supreme Four Sword Array. Once the array is unleashed, its power will surge like a raging bull. Sever all chances of life and causing everything to wither, you can sweep away all enemies in your way!”

“Can it defeat Big Senior Sister?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was now enraged. “Rebellious disciple, if I could defeat her, would I still be trapped here?!”

Lu Yang thought that his master made a valid point, so he decided to side with Yun Zhi.

~~~

“Big Senior Sister, during this mission, I discovered another problem.”

“What is it?”

“I realized that the Five Great Immortal Sects are not well-known enough. Many people don’t know that they can approach us when they encounter problems related to demons and monsters, so they can only rely on the authorities. If the authorities don’t care about them, these people would be left waiting helplessly.”

The Great Xia Dynasty lacked manpower, but due to pride, they found it inconvenient to seek help from the Five Great Immortal Sects. The civilians then ended up being the unlucky ones who had to suffer.

This was an issue Lu Yang had already noticed when he was on Pine Mountain. Although the old hunter and tiger-henchman ghosts were acting the whole time, their ignorance of the Dao-Seeking Sect was real. Similarly, in Yanjiang Commandery, Lu Yang had also randomly inquired around the place and realized that the commoners possessed limited knowledge of the upper echelons of society and were oblivious to the Five Great Immortal Sects.

Yun Zhi was somewhat astonished. I’ve really not noticed this problem before, or perhaps I should say that no one from the Five Great Immortal Sects has. Despite attending the Immortal Sect Summit Meeting every year, I’ve not heard anyone mention this before.

“That is indeed a problem. What about compiling the matters of the Dao-Seeking Sect into a book and spreading it among the people?”

Lu Yang offered his own proposal, as if he was presenting a treasure, “Writing a book is certainly a great way to spread awareness, but from what I know, the literacy rate among the commoners is low, with hardly any being able to afford books. Perhaps we could compile the matters of the Dao-Seeking Sect into the pingshu format[1], where a storyteller will narrate the stories.”

“Pingshu?” Yun Zhi was far from well-versed in this area. However, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was an expert in this field. After all, he once donated the book Introduction to Xiangsheng Comedy.

“That’s right, the pingshu format. Before joining the Dao-Seeking Sect, most of my cultivation knowledge came from the storyteller. However, the content and quality of pingshu in the market at the moment are inconsistent and oftentimes contradictory, not to mention that the records of cultivation are scant and superficial, so people are susceptible to misunderstandings about the concept of cultivation. If we compile the matters of the Dao-Seeking Sect into a storytelling format, it will definitely be a hit among the masses!” Lu Yang exclaimed excitedly, clenching his fists.

Yun Zhi was still somewhat skeptical. “There’s nothing unusual or remarkable happening in the Dao-Seeking Sect. Would they really attract an audience?”

Lu Yang responded in his heart, If even the matters of the Dao-Seeking Sect aren’t unusual or remarkable, then how outrageous must the cultivation world be?! Big Senior Sister, you are so devoted to cultivation that your knowledge of common-sense issues is lacking. You probably don’t know about the Dao-Seeking Sect’s reputation in the outside world.

With Big Senior Sister’s cultivation, those from the other immortal sects probably won't actively find trouble for themselves by saying to Big Senior Sister’s face that the Dao-Seeking Sect is not of a sound mind.

“Absolutely no problem!” Lu Yang declared with conviction.

Yun Zhi’s eyebrow was slightly furrowed as she pondered. “But who in the sect is most suitable to compile the pingshu and promote it outside?”

“I can recommend someone who will definitely be up to the task!”

“Who?”

“Shifu.”

1. Pingshu is a traditional folk art where one narrates stories with a folding fan and a storyteller’s gavel. ☜

Chapter 114: Big Senior Sister, Have I Succeeded in Learning It?

When the Taciturn Daoist Priest learned that he had a chance of getting released, he wished he could be Lu Yang’s disciple instead, frightening Lu Yang into hastily declining him.

After Lu Yang shared his ideas with the Taciturn Daoist Priest, the latter also felt that Lu Yang made a lot of sense. “Indeed, we have overlooked the importance of publicity. Mortals know too little about cultivation, the Five Great Immortal Sects, and other sects.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest stroked his beard. “Compiling a pingshu related to the Dao-Seeking Sect will not be a straightforward task. Please allow me some time to mull over it.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect has a history of one hundred twenty thousand years, and it can be divided into three phases: the Innate Daoist Priest’s establishment of the sect, the Primordial Heavenly Sovereign’s designation of the sect as one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, and the emergence of our Resurgence Ancestor known as the Vast Sea Daoist Lord. Every phase has numerous tales to tell. Just the beginning about the Innate Daoist Priest asking the universe for directions is already packed with details.”

Lu Yang commented to himself, As expected of Shifu. He can twist the matter of the Innate Daoist Priest getting lost to the grand tale of ‘asking the universe for directions.’ Just this skill alone will take me a long time to learn.

“Of course, it also can’t lack the current matters, which should be the focus. For instance, I can’t say that I was picked up by Old Three. It should be modified to ‘a person raised by heaven and earth and destined to rise at an opportune time, born with a short sword which had the character ‘kill’ inscribed on its handle...ahem, I’m just joking. I naturally wouldn’t say that.”

Meeting Yun Zhi’s frosty gaze, the Taciturn Daoist Priest instantly conceded defeat. “I will definitely describe everything truthfully!” He tried to negotiate, “Dear disciple, could you let me out first? Regarding the matters of the Dao-Seeking Sect annihilating demons and upholding righteousness, your eight senior uncles are the parties involved. In order to compile the pingshu, I must inquire about the detailed process so that there is room for elaboration and creativity.”

This time, Yun Zhi found his reasoning somewhat acceptable and decided to let her master out.

Then, she turned to leave.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest panicked and yelled from behind, “Dear disciple, you haven’t released me yet!”

Yun Zhi replied without looking back, “You just need to sit and meditate in the cave abode for three days, and the barrier will disappear on its own.”

Lu Yang exclaimed inwardly, Good heavens! So Shifu has been locked up for ten years because he hasn’t sat and meditated for three consecutive days. No wonder Big Senior Sister was unwilling to let him out.

Lu Yang sprinted to catch up with Yun Zhi, eagerly saying, “Big Senior Sister, I want to learn a spell that can be cast with just the mouth.”

“Why is that?”

“During my battles, I’ve discovered that my feet can dodge and attack, my hands can wield a sword and unleash covert weapons, but only my mouth is never used. Think about it, when I am locked in a stalemate with an enemy and our weapons are occupied, if I were to suddenly cast a spell with my mouth, it could catch them off guard and guarantee my victory!”

Yun Zhi couldn’t understand what Lu Yang meant by “being locked in a stalemate with an enemy” because her battles had always involved her one-sidedly wiping the floor. However, she had no reason to stop Lu Yang if he was willing to learn.

“I have one where you can spit out gold qi capable of slicing through hair. It requires a Gold Spirit Root, and your Sword Spirit Root just makes the cut. However, you would need a few moments to charge up, during which you can’t make other movements.”

Lu Yang shook his head. “The limitations are too great. It can be used for ambush, but there are few chances to use it in direct combat.”

“Then what about the Three Esse True Fire?[1] After accumulating energy in your abdomen, you can spit out upper, middle, and lower true fire. Nothing but sourceless water can extinguish the flames. The only issue is the difficulty of mastering it. You may need several months. As you have never learned elemental spells before, I’m not sure about your talent in this aspect.” Yun Zhi suddenly paused, recalling that the first spell Lu Yang had picked up was Shrinking Earth.

Lu Yang was thrilled. It’s actually the renowned Three Esse True Fire! I must learn it when the chance comes by. Even if I can’t master it, at least I won’t regret not trying.

“I want to learn the Three Esse True Fire.”

Seeing that Lu Yang had made his choice, Yun Zhi didn’t dissuade him and simply took him to the place where he first began his training. It was here that Lu Yang once lifted vats and grabbed tofu, successfully drawing qi into his body, so the place held significant sentimental value for him.

Yun Zhi explained calmly, “The so-called Three Esse True Fire refers to three types of fire: divine, essence, and mortal. Its classification is similar to the axes of the River Spirit. The heart represents the ‘Monarch Fire,’ also known as the ‘Divine Fire,’ with its name the ‘Upper Esse.’ The kidney represents the ‘Subject Fire,’ also known as the ‘Essence Fire,’ with its name the ‘Middle Esse.’ The bladder, which is the sea of qi below the navel, is known as the ‘Civilian Fire,’ with its name the ‘Lower Esse.’[2]

“When unleashing Three Esse True Fire, you must pay attention to the three positions: the heart, kidneys, and bladder. I have told you before that you must ensure an abundance of your kidney water at all times, and here is the reason. As the human body embodies the five elements, elemental spells often rely on the respective five organs, so the kidney water is of utmost importance.

“I’ll demonstrate once. Watch closely.”

Yun Zhi aimed her mouth at a large tree, spitting out a stream of Three Esse True Fire. The massive tree disintegrated into ashes before Lu Yang could even react. And this was after Yun Zhi had tried her best to restrain its power. Had she unleashed her full power, whether Heaven’s Gate Peak could remain would be up for debate.

“Have you learned it?”

Lu Yang hesitated. Big Senior Sister’s teaching methods have always been enigmatic, so the key lies in my own comprehension. “Let me give it a try.”

He had created the Clear Heart and True Nature Mantra to see through the essence of all things, but another reason was that he wanted to learn the spells and techniques Yun Zhi taught him.

It’s time I showcase the power of my self-created cultivation technique!

Lu Yang gathered the energy within him and concentrated it in his heart, kidneys, and bladder before spitting it in one breath.

His saliva flew three zhang away.

“Three Esse True Fire!” Lu Yang yelled again, not convinced of the results.

His saliva flew three zhang away again.

“Ptui!”

“Ptui!”

Lu Yang kept trying to cast the spell. By the end of it all, he had spat until his mouth turned dry.

It’s truly hard to learn the Three Esse True Fire.

Noting Lu Yang’s hard work, Yun Zhi handed him a gourd. Lu Yang took a sip and found it exceptionally sweet, as if it was fine jade wine.

“What kind of water is this? It’s so sweet!”

“Sugar water.”

...Of course, I do know that sugar water is sweet.

Pushing through with his perseverance, Lu Yang practiced repeatedly from noon to evening, until he finally began to grasp the knack of it.

“I will succeed this time, for sure! Three Esse True Fire, spit!” Lu Yang mustered his strength and spirit energy, circulating them with his dantian, and with a sudden spit, blazing flames burst forth from his mouth and ignited a large tree, causing it to crackle.

“I did it!” A bright smile spread across Lu Yang’s visage. I do have a talent for learning spells. I could master it in one afternoon when it would have taken several months.

As Yun Zhi watched from the side, she couldn’t brush off the feeling that something was amiss with the flames. Undeterred by the heat, she walked forward, pinched a small bit of the flame, and rubbed it between her fingers before licking her fingertip. “It’s sweet?”

Why does the flame have a taste?

“Cast it again.”

Despite his bafflement, Lu Yang spat out the true fire again, and Yun Zhi tasted it once more. “It’s salty?”

“One more time.”

Yun Zhi tasted it once again. “It’s spicy?”

After tasting it over and over, Yun Zhi discovered that not only were Lu Yang’s flames powerful, they also had very special flavors: sweet, salty, or spicy.

Lu Yang ran over in high spirits. “Big Senior Sister, have I succeeded in learning it?”

Yun Zhi stared at Lu Yang with an odd expression. “Yes, you have succeeded, but what you have learned is the Three Flavor True Fire.”[3]

“Three Flavored True Fire?”

1. This actually refers to the Samadhi True Fire, but the current translation choice is for a reason. ☜

2. You also see such “rankings” and “titles” that are given to organs in Traditional Chinese Medicine. ☜

3. The original spell is “san mei zhen huo” while the new spell is “san wei zhen huo.” Both “mei” and “wei” sound similar and look very similar to each other. For reference, “mei” is “昧” and “wei” is “味.” ☜

Chapter 115: A Waste of Talent To Not Do Barbeque

“Three Flavored True Fire?” Lu Yang couldn’t make sense of the situation. The names may be similar, but Big Senior Sister can’t distinguish between “esse” and “flavor?” [1]

But then, Lu Yang remembered that Yun Zhi’s education level was probably higher than this.

He pretended to be unperturbed as he laughed. “Hahaha, Big Senior Sister, you really know how to joke. You taught me the Three Esse True Fire, so how could I have learned the Three Flavored True Fire?

“No way, that can’t be, it’s impossible.”

Yun Zhi didn’t explain and simply called over the puppet, instructing it to fetch a piece of demon beast meat from the kitchen. She then somehow made the demon beast meat hover and spin in mid-air. “Roast it with your true fire.”

Lu Yang spat out the true fire, causing the demon beast meat to sizzle and ooze oil. Soon, a fragrant aroma wafted through the air, making Lu Yang swallow his saliva. Although Lu Yang’s true fire wasn’t as strong as Yun Zhi’s, it was still more powerful than ordinary flames, fully roasting the meat in no time.

“Try it yourself,” Yun Zhi told him.

Using his finger as a sword, Lu Yang sliced off a small piece and popped it into his mouth. It burst with so much flavor that it almost knocked his teeth out. Despite no seasoning added to the meat, it tasted as if it had been seasoned with salt for the tang, sugar for enhanced freshness, and spice for the extra kick.

It’s truly the Three Flavored True Fire.

Lu Yang solemnly analyzed, “Something must have gone wrong somewhere.” I followed Big Senior Sister’s method step by step and even watched her demonstration in person. It couldn’t possibly have gone wrong!

“Let me try again. I’ll definitely succeed this time!”

Yun Zhi nodded. “It’s good that you have the determination. I’ll leave tonight’s dinner to you then. It can also help you solidify what you’ve learned today.” With that, Yun Zhi returned to her cave abode to cultivate while waiting for Lu Yang’s dinner.

“Hold on, no, that’s not what I meant...” Lu Yang felt that Yun Zhi had misunderstood his determination, but it was too late. Yun Zhi had already vanished from sight, leaving behind only the puppet to keep him company.

Lu Yang sighed and called the puppet to join him in the kitchen.

It was his first time in the kitchen of Heaven’s Gate Peak. In the past, the puppet had always been the one preparing the meals. I’m already exhausted from training every day, so how would I have the energy to cook?

As expected of Big Senior Sister’s personal kitchen, it’s even larger than the gymnasium in my previous lifetime.

The gamut of ingredients was displayed neatly, and the corpses of demon beasts several meters in height could be seen everywhere. The demon beasts still appeared intimidating, a testament to how powerful they had been when they were alive. Unfortunately for these demon beasts, they didn’t know their place when they were still alive, rampaging across the Central Continent and wreaking havoc. When they ran into Yun Zhi, she killed them in a single blow before they could even realize it.

Lu Yang had some basic cooking skills, but that was only with ordinary ingredients. He didn’t recognize a single ingredient in front of him.

“What should I make? What does Big Senior Sister like to eat? It seems like she always eats a bit of everything. I haven’t seen her taking a special liking to something.”

“Master loves barbeque the most.” A sudden voice startled Lu Yang.

He turned his head, surprised that the puppet had talked.

The puppet was made of wood and resembled a female, though its facial features had not been carved. It had stayed by Lu Yang’s side ever since his first day of cultivation training. Why have I never known that it could speak?!

“Why are you staring at me?” the puppet spoke again, confirming to Lu Yang that he wasn’t hearing things.

“You can talk? Then why haven’t I heard you speak before?”

“Why should I talk to an idiot?”

“You...” Lu Yang was stumped for words. If I had the ability, I swear I’d have to dismantle this lousy puppet.

“You said that Big Senior Sister loves barbeque? Why haven’t I seen her eat it?” Lu Yang glanced at the puppet suspiciously.

He knew that there was an art called Puppet Technique, and those proficient in it were known as puppet masters. Among the first-class sects, there was even a sect, the Puppet Craftsman Sect, which was completely made up of puppet masters.

But what I don’t know is where the limits of the Puppet Technique lie. Could puppets really possess such high intelligence? Or should I say that it’s expected of the puppet created by Big Senior Sister?

“Master doesn’t have the habit of revealing personal preferences to outsiders,” the puppet replied as disdainfully as before. “See the kui[2] ox on your right? Chop off the thigh. Master likes this part the best.”

“I’ll trust you this time.” Lu Yang felt that the puppet had no reason to trick him.

Drawing his Qingfeng sword, he struck at the kui ox’s thigh. However, the kui ox glowed and repelled Lu Yang, sending him flying straight into a pile of flour. Cough, cough. Lu Yang was buried in white from head to toe.

“What level was this ox at when it was alive?” Lu Yang was certain that the ox had ridiculously high cultivation when it was alive, so much so that he couldn’t harm it even after its death.

The puppet didn’t answer, simply smashing the golden light protecting the kui ox with a single punch. “Try again.”

“Slash!” Lu Yang cast the Slashing Word Mantra, creating a shallow cut in the kui ox’s skin.

Although the Slashing Word Mantra wasn’t as powerful as the Breaking Word Mantra, its advantage was its wide coverage and multiple uses.

“Slash!”

“Slash!”

Lu Yang unleashed the Slashing Word Mantra three times in a row, depleting his spirit energy. The puppet would then feed him with Great Rejuvenation Pills whenever appropriate.

“Slash!”

“Slash!”

“Slash!”

Great Rejuvenation Pill.

Just like that, after numerous cycles of “slash slash slash and Great Rejuvenation Pill,” he finally sliced off enough meat for one meal. Right after Lu Yang finished with the preparation of the ingredients, he was already panting, and he lay sprawled out on the floor, while the puppet continued feeding him Great Rejuvenation Pills.

Lu Yang found this scene uncannily familiar.

To give credit where it was due, the Great Rejuvenation Pills were actually effective. Lu Yang was back to his energetic self after ingesting them, and he continued with the meal preparation.

“Use sword qi to mince the tendons,” the puppet instructed by the side.

The tip of the Qingfeng Sword pierced the kui ox meat, releasing sword qi. However, Lu Yang felt that the sword qi was like a stone sinking into the ocean, not triggering even a ripple.

“Jiayou[3], keep going, you’re the best,” the puppet cheered Lu Yang on, though its tone was so flat that Lu Yang didn’t feel the least bit encouraged.

Lu Yang yelled angrily, “Can you put some emotions into it?!”

The puppet quickly complied, “Lu Yang, although you have very low cultivation, learn everything the wrong way, and can’t even defeat me, you’ve already tried very hard. Jiayou!”

Veins bulged from Lu Yang’s forehead as he kept increasing the amount of sword qi he released. At long last, the sword qi penetrated the kui ox, slicing through the tendons bit by bit.

After completing all the steps, Lu Yang was so worn out that he didn’t have the energy to argue with the puppet.

When it was time to roast the meat, Lu Yang stuffed himself with Great Rejuvenation Pills while using his Three Flavored True Fire. Soon, the aroma of the roasted meat drifted out of the kitchen.

“It’s so fragrant! What’s smells so good?” Grandpa Ba walked into the kitchen to track down the source of the aroma. That was when he caught Lu Yang barbecuing.

“Grandpa Ba, what brings you here?” Lu Yang was surprised.

Grandpa Ba grinned as he took out a jar of tea leaves. “The Wudao Enlightenment Tea has just been prepared, so I was planning to bring some to Yun Zhi, but then I caught a whiff of this aroma, and I was curious to see what was being roasted. Turns out it’s kui ox meat. With your cultivation, it must have taken you quite the effort, huh?”

Lu Yang smiled sheepishly.

“By the way, you were asking about Old Nine previously. Is it because you know where he is?”

Lu Yang figured that since his master was about to be released, there should be no harm in telling Grandpa Ba, so he related the whole matter of his master being in seclusion in the pine forest.

Grandpa Ba’s eyes lit up. A wicked person will meet another wicked person to torment them. That goddamn Old Nine had been locked up by Yun Zhi!

He placed the Wudao Enlightenment Tea down and left. “I have something to attend to, so I’ll be heading off first.”

I’ve got to quickly tell this to all my junior brothers so that we can gather in a circle and watch Old Nine together!

1. The characters do look similar, but their pronunciations are different. This should be the original text, but it doesn’t really make sense in the translated version, so I tweaked it a little. ☜

2. The kui is a mythological beast. ☜

3. Jiayou is what one says to cheer someone on. ☜

Chapter 116: In Weal and Woe

Lu Yang went all out in roasting the kui ox. This was a contest of wisdom, perseverance, and luck; there was no room for carelessness. He naturally didn’t notice Grandpa Ba’s expression of schadenfreude.

After the kui ox was finally ready, it emitted a mouthwatering aroma that would linger in the kitchen for three days. The Three Flavored True Fire indeed had its merits—as one would expect from Lu Yang’s unique creation. There were only a total of 108 types of true fire in the world, and Lu Yang had forcefully added one to that number with his talent. Such a flame must be extraordinary!

As long as Lu Yang wanted to, he could easily open a chain barbeque restaurant spanning across the continent! Even establishing a barbeque sect might not be beyond the realms of possibility! In fact, this was an opportunity Man Gu could only wish for in his dreams!

However, Lu Yang was not one to chase after fame and fortune, so he had no plans of expansion in this direction.

Lu Yang placed the kui ox on a plate, which was decorated with roasted potatoes, roasted carrots, and roasted cauliflower, and prepared to carry the dishes to the table. The puppet looked at Lu Yang in surprise, not expecting him to be so thorough.

Just as Lu Yang was about to leave the kitchen, he noticed a big chunk of meat missing from the kui ox, exposing its ghastly white bones.

Lu Yang recalled the White Bone Flesh Regeneration Pill he had just exchanged for. “What would happen if I gave the kui ox the White Bone Flesh Regeneration Pill? Would the chunk of meat grow back?” If this were to succeed, it would be a massive business opportunity!

Acting on his ideas right away, Lu Yang pried open the kui ox’s mouth and force-fed it with the pill.

A miraculous scene unfolded as a faint glow emanated from the wound of the kui ox’s corpse. The roasted kui ox slowly levitated and became uncooked again as the wounds were seamed tightly under the golden light.

Lu Yang, “...”

Is this even scientific? I went through all that effort to roast you, yet you turned back into raw meat just like that?!

The puppet couldn’t stifle its laughter and giggled softly.

Lu Yang had no choice but to start over.

Fortunately, with the experience from his first attempt, he was much faster this time. At the same time, he also realized that his proficiency in the “Slashing Word Mantra,” sword qi, and Three Flavored True Fire had improved.

He ruminated over it. Could this be Big Senior Sister’s intention, letting me grow through the process of cooking?

That must be it! There’s a type of cultivator known as a spirit chef, and this is precisely what they do—cultivating through cooking. Our cultivation methods are different but lead to similar outcomes.

“Big Senior Sister really cares about me!” Lu Yang was extremely moved.

~~~

Yun Zhi sat before the dining table. As she cultivated, myriad mystical phenomena appeared in her surroundings; great stars fell, all things resuscitated, and lightning tribulations materialized, as if all the wonders of the world had converged right here.

Noticing Lu Yang’s arrival, she slowly opened her eyes, and the myriad phenomena instantly withdrew into her body, as if everything before was just a figment of one’s imagination.

“Roasted kui ox?” Yun Zhi took a glimpse at the dinner Lu Yang had meticulously prepared. She didn’t make any further comments and signaled for Lu Yang to eat together.

Lu Yang sat up straight at the table, anxiously waiting for Yun Zhi to have the first bite.

Yun Zhi sliced off a piece and sampled it. “Not bad.”

Only then did the grip around Lu Yang’s heart relax.

Yun Zhi opened her storage space and took out a bottle of pills, handing it to Lu Yang, who saw the words “Stomach-Invigorating and Digestion-Aiding Pills” on the label. “This is a classic pill from the Pill Cauldron Peak. It can promote your digestion and absorption of food. The spirit energy contained in the kui ox is far beyond your capacity. You have to eat slower and use the pills to assist you in gradual uptake.”

The Pill Cauldron Peak had been established ever since the founding of the Dao-Seeking Sect, and it was not without reasons that it continued standing strong today; the pills they concocted were sometimes very effective.

Lu Yang took a small piece and chewed on it gently. The kui ox meat was like gelatin, sliding down into his stomach. Copious amounts of spirit energy surged within his stomach and rushed straight to the crown of his head, instantly sweeping away all fatigue from roasting the kui ox; he felt completely rejuvenated.

His eyes lit up, and he quickly ingested the pill before sitting in a meditative position to cultivate, feeling the waves of spirit qi flowing within him.

A demon beast that was worthy enough to let Yun Zhi personally take care of it was naturally one with exceptionally high cultivation.

On the other hand, Yun Zhi elegantly savored the barbeque, nibbling on it slowly to appreciate the flavors. There are very few things that can enhance my cultivation now.

~~~

Seven elders gathered in the pine forest of Heaven’s Gate Peak; apart from First Elder and Yun Zhi, all the higher-ups of the Dao-Seeking Sect were present.

Even the elusive sect leader was around.

“Say, Old Nine was just doing fine, yet you never know when something could happen.”

“Life is unpredictable. Who can foresee the future?”

The seven elders discussed animatedly, while the Taciturn Daoist Priest sat in meditation, fuming so much that he felt the urge to draw his sword and duel. “I mustn’t get angry, I mustn’t get angry. I must sit here quietly for three days and not break away from my meditative state,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest repeatedly admonished himself not to lose his temper.

The seven elders gloated over his misfortune. Old Nine had toyed with us all the time, and today, we finally get the chance to laugh at him. We must seize this once-in-a-lifetime opportunity!

“I must say, Old Nine is too petty. It’s a good thing to have a very talented disciple. Why would he get so angry until he has cerebral thrombosis?”

“Nonsense! How can you call this cerebral thrombosis? He’s clearly in a vegetative state!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest could no longer hold himself back, roaring in rage, “Don’t go overboard with your bullying!”

Who on earth divulged my situation?!

Little Yun? No, I can’t beat her.

That means it must be Lu Yang!

“Serves you right, Old Nine! Even you have gotten your just desserts!” Grandpa Ba laughed, reveling in his misfortune.

Since Grandpa Ba was young, he had liked plants. At that time, the Taciturn Daoist Priest told him that there was a type of plant cultivation method where one would bury themselves in the soil with only their head exposed and use their body to comprehend the earth’s spirit qi, thereby boosting their cultivation.

To this day, Grandpa Ba refused to recall his past foolish self!

The embarrassment of a lifetime!

“Ha! Suffer my sword!” The Taciturn Daoist Priest unleashed the Supreme Four Sword Array toward the seven elders, who immediately assumed defensive stances. However, lightning suddenly burst forth at the entrance, blocking the sword array’s attack.

The seven elders heaved a sigh of relief. Yun Zhi’s defense is indeed reliable.

“Haha, Old Nine, your sword technique has regressed! It can’t even leave a small cave. If it were me, I would have broken out long ago!” Grandpa Ba laughed without restraint.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest sneered. “If all of you are so capable, then go ahead and blast the cave open!”

“Hmph! It’s a mere cave mouth. How hard can it be to blast it open!” Grandpa Ba struck out a mighty palm that hit the cave’s entrance, but it was similarly shattered by lightning.

“That was an accident, I’ll try again!” Grandpa Ba wasn’t ready to accept defeat. He attempted once more, but his attack was again neutralized by lightning.

A drop of cold sweat trickled down his forehead. “I’ve already calculated the position of the array’s focal point, but my offensive methods are limited. I would like to ask all of you to lend me a helping hand!”

The six elders readily agreed.

The seven elders exerted their powers simultaneously, attacking the array’s focal point as directed by Grandpa Ba. For a moment, lightning flashed and thunder roared, and the whole pine forest was engulfed in the atmosphere of primal chaos and multicolored rays of light.

The seal of the cave abode appeared to be enraged, brewing a force that seemed capable of sucking in everything in the world. Judging that the situation had turned awry, the seven elders resorted to a multitude of methods to escape, but it was futile as they got sucked into the cave abode.

The seven elders, “...”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was very moved. Is this what true camaraderie between senior and junior brothers looks like—sticking through weal and woe?

~~~

Meanwhile, Yun Zhi suddenly stopped eating, sensing that the seal used on her master had been triggered.

As the people of the Dao-Seeking Sect were full of imaginative and unconventional ideas, Yun Zhi was worried that someone might forcibly break the seal, so she had it set up such that if there was such an attempt, the seal would suck the culprit into the cave, sealing them together inside.

“There can’t be such a person, right?” she mumbled to herself uncertainly.

Chapter 117: I Am a Heart Devil

Yun Zhi couldn’t shake off the feeling that the thing she dreaded had happened. After all, this is the Dao-Seeking Sect—it would be strange if nothing happened.

Lu Yang had entered an abstruse state. He felt every one of his orifices overflowing with spirit qi, while the circulation within his meridians and the spirit qi from the external world merged seamlessly, completing the exchange of spirit qi with each breath. He attained an inner peace he never had before. As he relished in the benefits from refining the kui ox, he could clearly sense his body continuing to strengthen.

“Best to check what’s going on.” Yun Zhi glanced at Lu Yang, who was immersed in cultivation, and decided not to disturb him. She headed for the pine forest by herself, asking the puppet to guard Lu Yang’s cultivation in the meantime.

It was already deep into the night and especially quiet on Heaven’s Gate Peak, where the only people around were Yun Zhi and Lu Yang.

Yun Zhi walked through the mountain, like an immortal traversing the clouds. Then, she saw her master and elders trapped inside the cave abode and making a din. She could hear them even from a distance.

Yun Zhi sighed. What’s meant to happen will happen.

She walked toward the cave abode, wondering if she should let them out.

~~~

Inside the cave abode, the higher-ups of the Dao-Seeking Sect were gathered together.

“I know that all of you, my senior brothers and sisters, are kindhearted souls. You couldn’t bear to see me alone in here, so you specially came inside to keep me company.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest expressed his deepfelt gratitude, though he couldn’t stop the corners of his lips from curving up. “Especially you, Old Two. On the surface, you appeared to be breaking the array, but in fact, you saw that I was lonely here and pulled everyone in here to accompany me!”

Grandpa Ba immediately felt immense pressure from the malicious glares his junior brothers and sisters were giving him. He pretended to be composed as he urged, “Everyone, don’t be nervous! This is just a seal set by Junior Niece Yun Zhi, not the real person. As long as everyone works together, we can surely tide through this difficulty together and break the seal! Think about the Dao-Seeking Nine we once were, and think of your esteemed positions now. What kind of challenge can beat us down?”

When they were young and carving out their path in the jianghu, they exterminated demons and devils, leaving a mighty reputation on the Central Continent. “The Dao-Seeking Nine” was how people had referred to them at that time.

Now, the Dao-Seeking Nine were united once more in a cramped cave.

“So, Old Nine, how on earth do we get out of here?” Grandpa Ba glowered at the Taciturn Daoist Priest. I only came here to watch the spectacle, yet I have become the spectacle myself instead.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest giggled inwardly. It’s not easy to have everyone come and keep me company. How can I let them leave so easily?

He solemnly replied, “I’m not afraid of anyone laughing, but Little Yun’s cultivation has already surpassed mine, so her purpose in setting this seal is to encourage me to cultivate diligently and push past my boundaries. In other words, to break the seal, we must go beyond our limits and transcend ourselves!”

Everyone realized the gravity of the situation. Transcending oneself was easier said than done.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had already predicted how the events would play out. First, everyone will step forward and attempt to break the seal. After they get repelled, they’ll definitely become downhearted. This is when I’ll say that I suddenly have an epiphany and that I am about to break through, which requires me to sit in meditation for three days. When the three days are over, I’ll feign a surge of power and unleash a flashy sword technique to strike the cave entrance. At that point, the seal would have just come undone automatically, and my senior brothers and sisters would be amazed by my comprehension ability.

A perfect plan!

“If that’s the case, as the second senior brother, this is where I’ll step up and take the lead in attempting it first!” Since First Elder wasn’t around, Grandpa Ba was the most senior person present, so he felt the need to set an example.

Everyone else looked at Grandpa Ba in anticipation.

Figuring that he would probably fail, Grandpa Ba felt that it would be very embarrassing, so he turned the rest, “Step back, everyone. I have a unique skill that I’d prefer not to display in front of others.”

Everyone heeded his words and retreated into the depths of the cave, where the entrance was out of sight.

With everyone out of the way, Grandpa Ba inhaled a deep breath and shook out a few seeds from his sleeves. As Grandpa Ba murmured incantations, the seeds instantly transformed into thick vines that struck at the cave entrance, glowing faintly as lightning erupted and shook the heavens and the earth.

This was the rare Purple Lightning Vine, rumored to have been born from bathing in lightning tribulations. It was engraved with the mark of heaven and earth since birth, carrying a portion of a lightning tribulation’s formidable power.

After a frenzied barrage of explosions, there was no change to the cave entrance; the seal remained completely untouched.

“Hmm?” Grandpa Ba furrowed his brow as he saw a graceful figure in the thick smoke.

As the smoke dissipated, it revealed Yun Zhi’s figure.

With his vast amount of experience, Grandpa Ba instantly understood what was happening. What I’m seeing must be my heart devil![1] Didn’t Old Nine say that if we want to break the seal, we must transcend ourselves? And how does one transcend themselves if not by defeating their heart devil?

“I thought I’d already come to terms with it, believing that every generation grows stronger and that it’s a good thing for the young to surpass the old. I didn’t expect that I still haven’t let it go!” Grandpa Ba’s fighting spirit soared.

With this thought in mind, he no longer hesitated and launched an all-out attack on Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi had originally intended to come in and see what the elders were up to, pondering whether she should release them. To her surprise, as soon as she reached the cave entrance, she witnessed Grandpa Ba’s indiscriminate bombardment.

Yun Zhi had no choice but to retaliate. Extending her delicate hand, the bells on her wrist rang melodiously, and with a single strike of the palm, she sent Grandpa Ba flying deep into the cave until the other elders caught him.

“Second Senior Brother, what’s the matter?”

Grandpa Ba coughed a few times, his eyes carrying a trace of terror. He raised his trembling hand to point at the cave entrance. “Be careful, Old Nine wasn’t lying to us. Junior Niece Yun Zhi possesses unrivaled talent and has set a heart devil seal. If we want to break through to destroy the seal, we must first resolve our heart devil!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was perplexed. Heart devil? What heart devil?

Third Elder was not convinced and stepped forward to test it out, and he also met Yun Zhi. As he was originally not good with his brains, he naturally believed whatever Grandpa Ba said.

When Yun Zhi defeated the five sect leaders at the Immortal Sect Tournament, she had once become the heart devil of the older generation, making them question what they had accomplished in their cultivation for the past thousand years. Third Elder was no exception.

Upon seeing Yun Zhi, Third Elder immediately assumed a fighting stance and engaged in battle. The result was the same as Grandpa Ba’s—sent flying with a palm.

“What a powerful heart devil!”

And so, Fourth Elder, Fifth Elder, all the way until Eighth Elder, took their turns trying it out, and they were all defeated by Yun Zhi.

Unable to wrap his head around what was happening, the Taciturn Daoist Priest went to the cave entrance, and everything clicked the moment he saw Yun Zhi. How is this a heart devil? This is clearly Little Yun herself!

“Little Yun?” the Taciturn Daoist Priest called out tentatively.

Yun Zhi replied with an impassive face, “I’m a heart devil.”

Without giving her master a chance to react, she sent him flying with a palm and turned to leave the cave abode.

All of you treated me as a heart devil and attacked me right away, yet you still want to be let out? Just stay put and sit in meditation for three whole days.

~~~

Lu Yang slowly opened his eyes, feeling a warm sensation flowing through his body; he was now only a step away from a breakthrough.

Yun Zhi was already back in her seat which was across from him. Lu Yang wasn’t sure if it was his imagination, but he felt that Yun Zhi seemed somewhat happy.

“Big Senior Sister, is there something you’re happy about?”

“No,” Yun Zhi replied in her usual indifferent tone.

1. It’s something like one’s inner demons but the cultivation version. ☜

Chapter 118: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy Awakens

After dinner, Yun Zhi asked, “Did Dai Bufan give you some contribution points for your undercover mission?”

“Yes, quite a few.” Lu Yang was pleased as he had the most contribution points among the peers of his cohort.

“Three days from now, the sect will organize a marketplace which most people will attend. You can go and check it out if you’re interested. You might find something you like.”

Lu Yang nodded. He had long heard that exchange of items within the sect would take place in the form of a marketplace. In the past, Yun Zhi hadn’t allowed Lu Yang to participate in such events so that he could focus on cultivation. Now that Lu Yang was at the Foundation Establishment Stage and made some progress in his cultivation, she saw no need to intervene as much.
