The Dao-Seeking Sect held a marketplace every three months, allowing for barter trade, purchases with contribution points, eating, drinking, and merrymaking.

The disciples traveled to all corners of the world to carry out their missions and would often encounter local specialties and various novelties. After obtaining them, some chose to keep them for personal use, while some opted to take them to the marketplace to exchange for things they needed.

Yun Zhi exhorted, “Also, Shifu is currently sitting in deep meditation, so don’t go to him for a while.”

That came off as puzzling for Lu Yang. I wasn’t planning to visit Shifu. In any case, he will definitely come out in three days. “Oh.” Regardless, nothing can go wrong by listening to Big Senior Sister.

~~~

Three days later, the marketplace kicked off as scheduled.

An arena platform had been set up for the disciples to spar freely. It was crafted from a special type of rock that was indestructible, and it was even enveloped in an array to ensure that the battles wouldn’t spill over and affect the spectators.

Two Golden Core senior male disciples were fighting it out in the arena. Their golden cores were full and flawless and resembled the beauty of nature, evidently high-grade golden cores the world sought after but rarely attained.

“Moon Shattering Slash!” one of them shouted, wielding a broad saber shaped like a crescent moon as he hacked it down with sheer brute force, a scene that made Lu Yang’s eyelids twitch.

If Branch Leader Chu had similar strength to this senior brother, it would have been disastrous for us.

The other senior male disciple was not to be outdone, emanating a golden light that coated his body with a layer of golden membrane. “Buddhist Golden Body!” He had somehow learned the Buddhist Golden Body with some degree of success and managed to withstand the blade.

The mesmerizing display of saber techniques and spells was remarkable while the two disciples switched between them seamlessly. Lu Yang watched with rapt attention; it was a rare opportunity to witness a battle between two top-tier Golden Core experts.

However, Lu Yang had seen an even higher-level battle where a formidable cultivator clashed with an immortal. Perhaps Yun Zhi’s palm technique was too fierce, so the just awakened Everlasting Immortal Fairy stood no chance, and it could be said to have been a one-sided battle—Lu Yang didn’t learn anything at all.

“The Everlasting Immortal Fairy is unreliable,” Lu Yang sighed. If I could master even half a move from Big Senior Sister, wouldn’t I be unmatched at my rank?

“Wait, Big Senior Sister taught me Shrinking Earth To Inches and Three Esse True Fire.”

“Kid, I advise you to watch your words! What do you mean I’m unreliable?!” A woman’s voice rang out in Lu Yang’s mind.

“Senior, you’re awake?” Lu Yang exclaimed in surprise. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy slept for a few days, and now she’s finally awake?

“Calling me senior doesn’t sound too bad,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked lazily.

Lu Yang could imagine her stretching herself after just waking up.

“Let me tell you, I’m currently far from my peak and still need time to recover slowly. That person called Yun Zhi can only beat me now. Once I regain my strength, I’ll defeat her with just one hand,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared fiercely. In ancient times, I, Huang Doudou, commanded the wind and clouds, so how could I lose to a junior?

Lu Yang pondered for a bit and thought that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy made a valid point. “I’ll relay that to Big Senior Sister truthfully.”

“Wait wait wait! We can talk this out,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s tone immediately deflated.

Lu Yang asked, “...Senior, so are you reliable or not?”

Logically, with an ancient immortal’s soul within me, I should be unstoppable and able to crush all opponents, encounter bountiful fortuitous opportunities rolling in, level up as easily as drinking water, become invincible among my peers, and slay opponents beyond my level. All of this would be a cinch.

But the Everlasting Immortal Fairy just gives off an unreliable feeling. I might as well quickly latch onto Big Senior Sister’s thigh and curry favor with her.

“Hmph, who do you think I am? I’m the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Huang Doudou!”

“Why do I remember you referring to yourself as ‘this esteemed one?’” Lu Yang still remembered how arrogant the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was previously.

The Everlasting Immortal fell silent for a moment before repeating, “This esteemed one is the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Huang Doudou... No, that’s too awkward.” She tried to explain, “The main thing is that I heard from others that referring to myself as ‘this esteemed one’ will make me sound very impressive. When I just woke up, my brain wasn’t functioning properly, so I wanted to try it out, but I now find it too strange. I shall just refer to myself as ‘I.’”

That piqued Lu Yang’s curiosity. “Who did you hear it from?”

“Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and immortals, you name it. It’s not easy to cultivate to the highest realm, so everyone would refrain from combat if possible, but how then would they know who’s stronger or weaker? Hence, someone started the trend of speaking very arrogantly to intimidate others.

“After that, everyone found this method of speaking to be a good idea, so they would frequently say things like ‘This esteemed one was born as mandated by Heaven,’ ‘Those who defy this immortal shall be slain,’ ‘How dare mortals defy immortals,’ ‘This esteemed one bears tremendous power, don’t force this esteemed one to undo my seal.’

“Let me think, who started it... Oh right, it was the Heaven Mandate Immortal!

“At that time, I thought the way they spoke was quite interesting, so I recorded everything they said and compiled it into a booklet called Immortals’ Quotes. I don’t know where that booklet has gone now.”

Lu Yang, “...”

I think I have found the reason for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy getting backstabbed.

“Let me demonstrate what an immortal is capable of so that you won’t think I got here by sheer luck.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy deemed it necessary to showcase some of her true power to earn Lu Yang’s admiration and respect.

“Come, give me control of your body. I’ll let you experience what it feels like to battle beyond your level.”

Since they were in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s territory, Lu Yang wasn’t afraid that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would seize this opportunity to take over his body, so he willingly relinquished control.

At the moment, there was no one in the arena. Controlling Lu Yang’s body, the Everlasting Immortal stepped into the arena and cupped her fists as she addressed the crowd, “Dear elders and heroic friends, I have gained some comprehension in my cultivation today. May I know if there is any Basic Golden Core senior brother or sister willing to come up to offer me some guidance?”

She then explained to Lu Yang, “The ancient prodigies were just like this, provoking the crowd and counting on their own fists to establish a resounding reputation and laying the foundation for their path to invincibility. I’ll demonstrate it once today. Make sure to learn!”

“I’ll do it!” A bald senior male disciple leaped onto the stage, radiating golden light of merit[1] from head to toe.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy drew in a cold breath of air. Premier-grade golden core, fortified with merit, the embodiment of Arhat,[2] and a basic mastery of the Immeasurable Golden Body. How am I going to fight him? With my head?

“So-someone else, please”

The bald male disciple wasn’t offended, simply laughing as he jumped off the stage while another Confucian cultivator male disciple leaped onto the platform. He donned gray robes and held a bamboo book, wearing an unruffled smile.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stiffened again. A natural Confucian cultivator, blessed by almighty beings, speaks words imbued with laws, and wields supreme treasures in hand. How do I fight him?

“Someone else, please!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gritted her teeth.

“I’ll do it.” After the Confucian cultivator male disciple left the arena, a down-to-earth, stout senior male disciple took the stage.

In one glance, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could tell that his core contained the five qi and was considered to be a first-tier high-grade core. Not only was he endowed with fortune and protected by his bloodline, his cultivation technique was also top-notch. There was not a single flaw with him that she could discern.

Only then did the Everlasting Immortal Fairy realize that she couldn’t defeat any of the Golden Core cultivators present.

1. A concept in Buddhism that is obtained from doing good deeds. ☜

2. Another name for the founder of Buddhism. ☜

Chapter 119: Let You Witness the Keen Judgment of an Immortal!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was supposed to have had it all planned out. Since Lu Yang was personally trained by Yun Zhi and his constitution and talent would have made him a rare prodigy in ancient times, fighting beyond his level wouldn’t be a difficult matter, so she could take advantage of this opportunity to shine in the arena.

Now, she confirmed that Lu Yang could indeed fight beyond his level in ancient times, but that didn’t imply that he could do so in the Dao-Seeking Sect. What the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t know was that despite being one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s reputation wasn’t built on their outstanding spells and techniques—unparalleled imagination was their forte.

The Dao-Seeking Sect had stood the test of time for 120,000 years not just because of luck but also their capabilities. During the generation of the Dao-Seeking Nine, the Nine had their respective methods in elevating the sect to greater heights.

One example was Seventh Elder, who managed the Pill Cauldron Peak. When he was young, he had the experience of a hundred attempts at breaking through to the Foundation Establishment Stage, paving a solid foundation for future disciples, including Lu Yang. At the Great Perfection Foundation Establishment Stage, Seventh Elder proposed that the world didn’t stipulate that a person could only have one golden core, so why not have two or even three golden cores?

He began deducing the configurations for two and three golden cores. Two golden cores were still manageable; both of them would attract and rotate around each other with a discernible pattern. However, when it came to three golden cores, Seventh Elder began to struggle; their rotation patterns were as unpredictable as a fog of primordial chaos.

Through sheer tenacity, Seventh Elder listed out eighteen equations of the Heavenly Element Math Technique (Tianyuan-Shu)[1] formula and borrowed his master’s spiritual consciousness to calculate the results. However, the computations required for the rotation of three golden cores were enormous, and since three golden cores were beyond what a Golden Core cultivator could bear, the idea of three golden cores was abandoned.

Although it ended in failure, the new calculation methods derived from the process of solving the problem were of immense help to Seventh Elder. After generations of research at the Dao-Seeking Sect, they already had a profound understanding of forming a golden core. Standing on the shoulders of giants, one could easily form a high-grade golden core by following the procedures.

Any random disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect could be considered a prodigy in the outside world. Although they couldn’t guarantee that they would be unmatched among their peers, defeating 99% of those at the same level wouldn’t be a problem.

Inside the mental space, Lu Yang was silently watching the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

I understand all the reasons, but why am I the one embarrassed when the useless one is the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had failed miserably even before getting started, like how one died before sending the troops out.

“Return my body to me!” Lu Yang regretted letting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy control his body.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy decided to educate her junior, “Youngster, cultivation is not only about violence. Does strength represent everything? Of course not! Cultivation embodies knowledge and is a test of one’s judgment. There are many good things in this marketplace of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Let me demonstrate to you what the judgment of an ancient immortal is like!”

Lu Yang decided to trust her one more time.

“Come take a look! Liuli-Glazed Blue-And-White Vase, retrieved from ancient cave ruins, a rare magical treasure!”

“Crouching Dragon[2] Jade Pillow! It lets you cultivate in your dreamscape. A specialty from the southern regions, definitely good stuff!”

“Minor Circulation Pill! Ten contribution points for one, buy three get one free! The more you buy, the more you get! Buy a hundred pills, and we’ll throw in the pill formula for free!”

“Person for rent, I am available for rent! A Golden Core cultivator that can accompany you outside for missions, is able to endure hardships, and willing to do work. One hundred and twenty points per day!”

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s marketplace had everything that one might possibly need, ranging from cave treasures to people on sale.

Controlling Lu Yang’s body, the Everlasting Immortal squatted down, and as she did so, she reflexively swept her hand behind her rear, but that was when she realized that Lu Yang was not wearing a dress.

Lu Yang grumbled to himself, Seriously? I’m a man. Why would I be wearing a dress?

“How much is this Liuli-Glazed Blue-And-White Vase?” The vase had attracted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s attention. Inside was a withered flower, its species indistinguishable, and it was unclear how long it had been dead.

“888 contribution points.”

“So expensive?!”

“Junior Brother, don’t be put off by the price. This Liuli-Glazed Blue-And-White Vase was a treasure I found in a cave belonging to a Divine Transfiguration cultivator. Look at the exquisite craftsmanship, look at its sturdy material, it’s a great bargain.”

“Apart from it being sturdy, are there other strengths? It can’t be that the magical treasure’s strength is only its sturdiness?”

The male disciple was a bit embarrassed. This vase had been in his possession for a long time, and he never found a use for it, so the only selling point he could promote was its sturdiness.

“One hundred contribution points. I’ll buy it back as a decoration.”

“Junior Brother, you’ve slashed the price too much. Seven hundred, it can’t go any lower.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy turned her head and walked away.

“Wait, don’t be in a hurry to leave! Four hundred! That’s the lowest I can go!”

“Two hundred.”

The male disciple gritted his teeth. This vase has been on display for a very long time, and no one has shown interest in it. It’s not easy to have a potential buyer. I mustn’t let this opportunity slip away!

“Deal!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy bragged to Lu Yang, “Did you see that? That’s my keen sense of judgment!”

Lu Yang was curious. “Does this vase hold some kind of secret?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head in a cryptic manner. “The only characteristic of this vase is its toughness, but the secret doesn’t lie in the vase but this withered flower! There’s a cultivation technique hidden in this flower. Let me analyze it for you!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy moved to a corner of the marketplace and began softly chanting what sounded like an ancient scripture. As the words left her lips, the withered flower began to revive, turning into a bud ready to bloom. When the flower was in full bloom, a stream of characters floated out from the flower.

Her expression appeared to imply that everything had gone according to her expectations. She diligently translated and soon attained the results.

“This is Liuli-Glazed Bone Art, a cultivation technique that can be practiced until the Void Refinement Stage. It is divided into three stages, Non-Transmuted Bone, Vajra Bone, and Liuli-Glazed Bone. However, this is an incomplete version, and it only contains the Non-Transmuted Bone stage, which is the part from the Qi Training to the Golden Core stages. If we ever get a chance to enter an ancient ruin, we might even find the second half of the cultivation technique!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was feeling smug. This is an incomplete version of a Divine Transfiguration cultivation technique. If this were in ancient times, it could have easily wiped out middle- or small-sized tribes. Countless people would have fought tooth and nail to cultivate it.

Lu Yang fell silent for a bit, then quietly recited a passage.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was astounded. This is the final section of the Liuli-Glazed Bone Transmutation Art!

“I haven’t even translated it for you. How did you know that? You can understand the meaning of these characters?”

Lu Yang sighed and explained, “The Dao-Seeking Sect had retrieved the complete version of the cultivation technique from ancient ruins a long time ago. I read this as a reference when I was delving into cultivation techniques.

“Big Senior Sister even fixed a few flaws and extended it. She deduced that what comes after the Liuli-Glazed Bone stage is the Imperishable Bone, so now, the Liuli-Glazed Bone Transmutation Art can be cultivated all the way until the Apex Fusion Stage.

“If you are interested, I can take you to see it. It’s right on the first floor of the scripture library. It’s free of charge, so you can read it whenever you want.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “...”

Why did your sect place such a precious cultivation technique on the first floor of the scripture library?

Lu Yang also had a question. Can I get my two hundred contribution points refunded?

1. Tianyuan-Shu is something like ancient Chinese algebra. Instead of x, the 元 (yuan) character is used to denote the unknown variable. ☜

2. Fun fact: “Crouching Dragon” was a nickname of Zhuge Liang. It also refers to geniuses who have yet to show themselves to the world. ☜

Chapter 120: Ancient Tales of Wonders

To be fair, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy did have a keen judgment, though this time was an exception. If it had been some other treasure, it might have been a serendipitous encounter.

However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t see it that way. This is an utter disgrace. As an immortal, I actually embarrassed myself twice in front of a junior. How can I, Huang Doudou, lose face?!

“Immortal Fairy, if there’s nothing else, you can go back to sleep,” Lu Yang suggested.

“Kid, don’t be misled that this is any indication of my abilities!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was unconvinced, still trying hard to prove her worth. “During the ancient times, I was one of the top formidable figures and owned innumerable treasures throughout my life. For instance, I buried an immense number of treasures on the North Star, including numerous immortal treasures. I still remember the exact locations. If you can find them and establish your own sect, monopolizing power and riding roughshod over people would be all too easy!”

“But didn’t the Ancient Nameless One refine all the stars? How would I find the North Star?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy fell silent for a moment before continuing, “I can also guide you in your cultivation, help you achieve results with half the effort, and surpass those at your age, while ensuring that your foundation is solid and without flaws!”

“Thank you, Big Senior Sister can guide me.”

“How can that little lass compare to my vast knowledge? My guidance is definitely more comprehensive. She can’t possibly cover every aspect, and her teachings will be riddled with gaps. With your foundation establishment as an example, your foundation establishment is...quite perfect.”

Lu Yang was rendered speechless.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had no choice but to acknowledge that despite her critical judgment, Lu Yang’s foundation establishment could be said to be impeccable.

“And...and as a woman, I am attentive to details, so I can help you chase the girl you like!”

Lu Yang could tell that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was running out of ideas and even resorted to abandoning her identity as an immortal.

“No need. Big Senior Sister told me that it’s best to ensure a robust kidney for cultivation.”

“Shallow!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy scoffed at the viewpoint. “Haven’t you heard of how a man indulged in women every night and possessed a harem of more than a hundred women in ancient times? He was cultivating the Blissful Union[1] technique, and his cultivation soared by leaps and bounds!

“Do you want to learn this type of cultivation technique? I have a few books here that would suit you.”

Lu Yang calmly asked, “Before that, tell me what happened to that man who started the harem?”

“He was attacked en masse by the women in his harem and was gruesomely killed with his body shredded apart...but that’s not the main point! The most important thing is how quickly his cultivation grew!”

“He also lost his life quickly.”

“I have also seen many spells and techniques, so I can teach you ways to deal with them. For example, there’s the mighty ability of ‘Law Follows Words,’ where anything you say becomes true. This demonstrates the pinnacle of karmic spells! Back when I was still at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, I encountered a strong enemy who knew Law Follows Words. It was really terrifying then! He was practically the favored son of heaven and earth. Anything he uttered could become reality, and it wouldn’t be an exaggeration to say that he was omnipotent.

“However, no matter how strong he was, he ultimately couldn’t defeat me!”

Lu Yang was astonished. Law Follows Words sounds like an extremely difficult spell to counter, yet the Everlasting Immortal Fairy actually defeated the person. That’s very impressive. But that also makes sense. Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy isn’t very reliable, the ancient times were a period of overwhelming chaos, where prodigies vied for supremacy and experts fought to the death, until only five became immortals in the end. The fact that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could achieve victory under such circumstances is a testament to her talent.

“How did you defeat him?”

“I ambushed him. Law Follows Words had probably protected him so well that he had hardly experienced any beatings. He shouted ‘I’m dying from the pain!’ and then he died.”

Lu Yang, “...”

What kind of useless person is that?

“Unfortunately, the legacy of Law Follows Words died with him.”

Seeing Lu Yang trapped in shock, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s confidence level was boosted. “Apart from countering spells, I can also teach you other spells and techniques. Have you heard of the mighty ability ‘Shrinking Earth To Inches?’ This is a rare spatial spell. In ancient times, Golden Core cultivators could barely master it, but under my guidance, you can learn it right away.”

“Shrinking Earth To Inches?” Lu Yang was secretly delighted. Big Senior Sister had omitted too much from her teaching process. With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy teaching me this time, there will surely be no problem.

Noticing Lu Yang’s interest, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy patiently taught him, expounding on every single step. Lu Yang took out a small notebook and nodded as he jotted down notes, appearing just like a model student.

After a while, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes turned blank as she saw Lu Yang burrow around in the earth, turning himself into all kinds of sizes. She sank into deep self-doubt about her teaching abilities.

Is there anything I, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, haven’t seen?

But I’ve really never seen something like this before.

The good news was that Lu Yang’s mastery of both Shrinking Earth and To Inches had improved. He could now shrink in size to one inch instead of three inches, and his spellcasting speed had also increased significantly.

“I know more than just this spatial spell!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy fully displayed the collection of spells an immortal ought to have.

“What else do you know?”

“It stands at the same rank as Shrinking Earth To Inches, and it’s called ‘Close Horizon From Cliff!’[2]

“Once you master Close Horizon From Cliff, any distance will appear to be right before your eyes. All it needs is one step to arrive at the destination!” Close Horizon From Cliff was harder to grasp than Shrinking Earth To Inches. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was worried that Lu Yang wouldn’t be able to learn it and suffer a blow to his confidence, so she initially had no plans of teaching it.

Now, I only wish for Lu Yang to not learn it the wrong way!

“Close Horizon From Cliff has very high requirements for comprehension. Without having learned other spatial spells as a foundation, it would be challenging to learn this. Do you have the confidence?”

Lu Yang contemplated for a while. I learned the Garment-Cleansing Incantation and could summon clean clothes, so it’s a typical example of a spatial spell.

Hence, Lu Yang nodded, and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy began to teach.

“Learning Close Horizon From Cliff is essentially the same process as learning Shrinking Earth To Inches. First, you have to memorize and recite an incantation. Listen closely...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recited a passage of obscure ancient language which was extremely hard to recite from memory.

However, Lu Yang had already opened his mental space. With his strong spiritual consciousness, he soon memorized the ancient text. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy could see that Lu Yang had a knack for learning spells.

“Next, you need to create an image of a map in your mind and imagine yourself at a certain location. As you think about it, recite the ancient incantation. When your qi, essence, and consciousness are in harmony, you’ll be able to teleport yourself to your destination with a single thought.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy reminded, “But you have to be careful. The distance of teleportation is related to one’s cultivation. Since it’s your first attempt, you shouldn’t choose a distance that is too far away.”

Lu Yang followed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s instructions and gingerly gave it a try. Simultaneously reciting the incantation and imagining Heaven’s Gate Peak in his mind, he hollered, “Close Horizon From Cliff!”

Nothing happened.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “Take a step forward. The meaning of ‘Close Horizon From Cliff’ means that your destination is close and just a step away, so you need to step forward!”

Only by stepping forward can I know whether I’ve succeeded.

As Lu Yang took a step forward, the scenery beneath his feet changed. Both he and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy were overjoyed.

Success!

“Wait, look down!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy yelled.

Lu Yang lowered his head, and cold sweat drenched him. Beneath him was a bottomless abyss! He turned to look behind him and realized that it was an overhanging cliff.

So the function of Close Horizon From Cliff is to let me stand on the edge of the cliff?

Lu Yang was not in the mood to vent, for there was nothing beneath him, and he was suspended in mid-air.

He managed to flail his legs twice before plunging into the abyss.

1. The sect with this name is almost a staple in wuxia novels. As its name suggests, it’s about leveling up through intimate methods. ☜

2. The name is an actual idiom where it means that something appears to be so close, yet it is actually as far as the horizon. ☜

Chapter 121: Tomb

Close Horizon From Cliff was a widely known spatial spell, yet hardly anyone could master it. As it delved into the original essence of spatial spells, only those with great comprehension and fortuitous opportunities could master it. After they did so, the world would be their oyster.

“So the place you thought of was the edge of a cliff. What a unique location!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy exclaimed in awe. This junior is indeed impressive! He mastered such a difficult spell like Close Horizon From Cliff so quickly.

“Unique my ass! I was thinking of Heaven’s Gate Peak. What is this place?!” Lu Yang yelled, just like how anyone would lose their composure when suddenly appearing over a cliff.

The worst thing is that I’m falling! If I crash into the hard ground, becoming a pile of mushy meat would be the best outcome I can hope for.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s expression instantly changed. If anything were to happen to Lu Yang, that little lass would definitely make me pay the price with my disintegrated soul!

“Quick, let me control your body. I’ll rescue you!”

Lu Yang could never place his hopes in the never-reliable Everlasting Immortal Fairy in such a critical moment. His speed of descent was only getting faster; he needed to find a way to land safely.

Inhaling a deep breath, Lu Yang forced himself to remain calm. Since it was pitch-black below him, he couldn’t see anything, so his fear of heights didn’t pose a problem.

“Close Horizon From Cliff!” Lu Yang prayed that the newly learned spell could teleport him back, which would be the best outcome.

The falling Lu Yang instantly vanished, reappearing over the cliff.

Lu Yang, “...”

Looks like I won’t be going back anytime soon. That doesn't matter; I have a backup plan.

“To Inches!” Lu Yang shrunk himself while retaining the original size of his clothes. He desperately grabbed the ends of his clothes and formed a makeshift parachute, finally slowing down.

“Whew—” Lu Yang heaved a sigh of relief.

Lu Yang hovered unsteadily amidst the precipitous cliff walls around him, on tenterhooks about the fate that lay ahead of him.

“Look, the cliff wall over there has a protrusion that appears to be a platform. You should land there!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy shouted.

“Where? Why don’t I see it?” Lu Yang frowned.

“On the left, it’s just to the left! Your spiritual consciousness doesn’t extend as far as mine, so I can see it first!”

Lu Yang followed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s directions and managed to land on a platform. Only when his feet touched the ground did Lu Yang finally relax. That really scared me out of my wits.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang suspiciously. “Did you really use Close Horizon From Cliff just now?” I’ve used it many times, but never once have I encountered a situation like this.

“I think so...” Lu Yang was also not very certain. He now had a better understanding of his talent in spells and knew that Yun Zhi couldn’t entirely be blamed for him going astray.

I am also partly responsible.

“At the very least, it’s a proper spatial technique, and it did work in teleporting me away,” Lu Yang comforted himself.

Moreover, there was another advantage to Lu Yang picking up Close Horizon From Cliff. The main fear of cultivators who practiced spatial spells was meeting enemies with the same expertise, where they could predict one’s teleportation destination and pursue them relentlessly.

However, Lu Yang did not need to worry about such situations. After all, even he didn’t know where he would teleport himself to.

“Speaking of which, where is this place?” Lu Yang gazed up at the sky. The precipitous cliff walls only offered him a sliver of the blue sky, making it impossible to discern his location.

I wonder how far away I am from the Dao-Seeking Sect. Or is this still the Central Continent?

“Wherever it is, don’t be scared,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy cheered Lu Yang up. “With me here to protect you, nothing will go wrong!”

Lu Yang thought to himself, Is this what they mean by counting on yourself rather than depending on gods and immortals? At least I’m aware of where my abilities stand. The gods and immortals don’t know.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy urged, “Let’s go in and check it out. This appears to be a cave abode.”

“Might as well.”

As soon as Lu Yang stepped inside, he heard a loud bang behind him—the stone doors had closed.

Despite Lu Yang gritting his teeth and exerting all his strength, the stone doors didn’t budge an inch.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s expression grew serious. “Don’t waste your strength. This door is refined by an expert. It’s not something a Foundation Establishment cultivator like yourself can move.”

With the doors tightly shut, the cave abode was now completely engulfed in darkness.

Just as Lu Yang wanted to use the Three Flavored True Fire to illuminate the surroundings, both sides of the cave suddenly glowed with a faint light; the sides of the long cave passage were lined with luminous stones.

“Luminous pearls?”

Lu Yang kept feeling that he had heard about this arrangement style of luminous pearls before. Where did I hear of it?

“We have no choice but to go deeper.”

Within the empty passage, only the sound of Lu Yang’s footsteps could be heard, creating an eerie and strange atmosphere.

Upon arriving at the end of the passage, Lu Yang saw two rows of imposing terracotta soldiers wielding various magical artifacts, as if they were guarding something. They surrounded a stele inscribed with “The Deceased Lives Eternal.”

Lu Yang finally realized where the sense of familiarity had come from. Isn’t this a tomb?

“The Deceased Lives Eternal” was a common epitaph among humans.

His blood ran cold, never expecting himself to walk into a tomb.

“This...this is a tomb?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pretended to put on a calm facade, but her slightly quivering voice gave it away.

“Seems like it.” Lu Yang nodded solemnly, feeling that he had gotten swept up in something big.

Gulp. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy swallowed nervously.

A slightly comical guess slipped into Lu Yang’s mind. “Immortal Fairy, you aren’t scared of ghosts, are you?”

“Who...who would be scared of such things? I’m a dignified immortal.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s voice was trembling.

“But you’re shivering.”

“From the cold.”

“Do you still remember your title?”

“The Everlasting Immortal Fairy.”

“With a title like yours, you’d be considered a big shot like the jiangshi[1] founder in the tomb-raiding world. What’s there to be scared of?”

Recalling how the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had vowed to protect him just now, Lu Yang was further convinced that not believing her absurd words was the wisest decision he had made.

“You don’t have to be scared. I happen to have a few books about tombs with me.” Lu Yang took out the book Tomb Raiding Takeaways, which was a gift of appreciation from the head of the Shang Family after slaying the Painted Skin Ghost. I didn’t think I'd find a use for it here.

“Oh, you have such good stuff?” Light danced in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes. Why are tombs and ghosts scary? It’s naturally because they belong to the “unknown.” With the knowledge from this book, I’ll be much less scared.

“Open it up and see what’s written. Does it introduce what type of tomb this is?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy urged.

The book had been untouched by Lu Yang ever since he obtained it, but it wasn’t too late to take a look at it now.

Flipping to the first page, he softly read out, “According to Article 532 of the Great Xia Penal Code, mortals and Qi Training cultivators found guilty of raiding tombs of historical, artistic, or cultivation value shall face imprisonment of no less than three years and no more than ten years, and a fine. For lighter offenses, imprisonment of less than three years and a fine shall apply.

“Foundation Establishment cultivators found guilty of this crime shall receive double the sentence of Qi Training cultivators.”

Isn’t this book too reliable?

1. Jiangshi is a Chinese hopping vampire or reanimated corpse, sometimes also translated as zombie. They are easily identifiable by a talisman on their forehead. ☜

Chapter 122: Appraisal-Type Magical Artifact

“What on earth is this thing?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face was one of bafflement. What is a penal code?

In ancient times, clans and bloodlines were the fulcrum of society, and people gathered as tribes. Punishment within clans would be based on “family rules” and “clan rules.” Alternatively, for those in sects, punishment for disciples was governed by “sect rules.”

There was no concept of a nation back then, so the notion of a legal system did not exist.

However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t one to be bogged down by old ways. She could roughly guess the purpose of the penal code from its content. I understand the logic, but why does a tomb-raiding takeaway journal start with an extract from the penal code?

Lu Yang coughed twice, signaling that everything was in his grasp. “Don’t mind it, Immortal Fairy. In our era, books are always written in this style. As they say, ‘assess the punishment before committing the crime.’ This lets people know what they’re getting into.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gave Lu Yang a suspicious look but eventually replied, “Oh.”

The second page was the table of contents, and its content seemed to be very proper. Judging by the headings, this book introduced the types of jiangshi, coffin specifications, dimensions of tomb chambers, and common trap mechanisms.

Shang Zhongtian certainly lived up to his infamy in the tomb-raiding community. Everything he wrote was packed with solid information—exactly what Lu Yang needed.

“Let me see, terracotta soldiers... Found it, it’s here!

The terracotta soldiers are life-sized statues made of clay and wood, and they are usually lined up in tombs as burial items. A note of caution is that if you encounter terracotta soldiers at a tomb’s entrance, you must flee right away. These terracotta soldiers could very well become animated!”

Lu Yang stiffly raised his head to look at the towering terracotta soldier. Suddenly, green light emitted from its eyes as it reached out its large hand to grab him.

“I knew nothing good would come of this!” Fortunately, Lu Yang honed his nimble footwork in the barbeque shop, allowing him to narrowly dodge the terracotta soldier’s attack.

Many more terracotta soldiers began moving. Lu Yang wanted to retreat but discovered that his escape route was blocked by the terracotta soldiers.

Toward the deeper part of the cave, it was no longer a narrow passage but a wide space, though the dim light only revealed a blurry silhouette.

Drip...drip...drip...

Intermittent sounds of water dripping from somewhere pierced through the silence. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy curled up in anxiety, praying that Lu Yang would be able to surmount this hurdle and find an exit. In the massive tomb, only the sound of dripping water and Lu Yang’s heartbeat could be heard. It was sufficient to make one’s hair stand on ends.

Lu Yang was also very scared, so he swiftly sealed his pores to prevent his hair from standing up.

He lowered his head to read the book, doing a last-minute crash course on tombs. “Jiangshi: a type of monster frequently encountered during tomb raiding. It can be classified into Purple Jiangshi, White Jiangshi, Green Jiangshi, Hairy Jiangshi, Flying Jiangshi, Swimming Jiangshi, Lurking Jiangshi, and Ba Drought Demon.[1] Purple Jiang corresponds to the Qi Training Stage, White Jiang to the Foundation Establishment Stage, Green Jiang to the Golden Core Stage, and so forth.

“Jiangshi are inherently yin beings and fear purest yang true fire the most.”

While Lu Yang was engrossed in reading, he felt a hand on his shoulder and absentmindedly swatted it away. “Immortal Fairy, didn’t you say you were scared? Why are you still in the mood to joke?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy whispered as if she was afraid of startling someone. “...I’m in your mental realm. How could I possibly tap your shoulder?”

Only then did Lu Yang turn his head sharply and see a bunch of jiangshi with purple skin behind him. The one that had tapped his shoulder earlier was a white, furry jiangshi!

“Purple Jiangshi and White Jiangshi!”

Recalling the notes in the Tomb Raiding Takeaways, Lu Yang unleashed the Three Flavored True Fire, burning the jiangshi to a crisp. Jiangshi were indeed fearful of true fire. Faced with the wall of flames, they didn’t dare take a single step forward.

“This is true fire! You can actually use true fire?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was stunned. I’ve never heard of a Foundation Establishment cultivator being able to wield true fire. “And from the looks of it, it’s the Three Esse True Fire!”

Lu Yang once again overturned the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s understanding of the world. The Three Esse True Fire had a resounding reputation among the 108 true fires. Even a Golden Core cultivator learning it would be terrifying, let alone a Foundation Establishment cultivator.

The person in question made no comments, simply flashing a cryptic smile. This will make me look very cool. Having an ancient immortal impressed by your talent feels amazing.

If I had blurted out “This is authentic Three Flavored True Fire,” I would have exposed myself. Whatever the case, they’re all true fire; it’s more or less the same.

Lu Yang spat out a mouthful of Three Flavored True Fire again. The ball of fire hovered over his shoulder, lighting up the surroundings while also intimidating any potential jiangshi lurking in the dark.

“Finding the exit of a tomb chamber is a challenging task. It requires one to hold a bagua compass, perform the Immovable Seal through hand gestures, and recite ‘Examine the walls to seek the dragon and divide the gold. Each and every wall is an obstacle to overcome and a trial to pass.’[2] Only then can I discover the exit.”

Lu Yang ruminated for a while. I don't have a bagua compass, and neither do I know the Immovable Seal.

He took out a small wooden rod from his identity jade tablet and placed it upright on the ground. “O Big Senior Sister, please protect us. O Big Senior Sister, please protect us.”

The small wooden rod fell in the northeast direction.

Lu Yang was a cautious person; he was used to intensive calculations from mathematics homework in his previous life. Now that he was in a perilous situation, it was even more crucial to be careful.

He set the small wooden rod upright again and chanted “O Big Senior Sister, please protect us.”

The small wooden rod fell in the northeast direction again.

It's confirmed. The exit is in the northeast direction.

The answer has been double-checked. It can't be wrong.

“This is a tomb chamber?” Lu Yang followed the guidance of the small wooden rod and arrived at a tomb chamber, though he didn't know whether it was the main or secondary chamber.

“Let me see how the book describes it...

The main difference between the main and secondary chambers is determined by Feng Shui and requires a bagua compass and turtle shell for divination. The specific method is as follows...” Lu Yang’s eyes were whirling from the information. The method written can’t be used at all.

“This is the main chamber,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stated with certainty.

“How do you know that?” Lu Yang was floored that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was finally proving useful.

“The characters for ‘Main Chamber’ were written above the entrance just now.”

Lu Yang stuck his head out of the door, and sure enough, the words “Main Chamber” were kindly written above it.

Is this thing written for the jiangshi?

“Look, there are so many burial goods in this tomb chamber, and they’re all treasures!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy exclaimed.

Lu Yang looked down. She’s right. The chamber is stacked with an assortment of treasures. The tomb owner was likely very wealthy when alive. I wonder why this spot was chosen for the tomb.

“Hmm? The book is glowing?” Lu Yang was astounded as he stared at the Tomb Raiding Takeaways in his hands. “This book’s been refined before?”

The light from the book aimed at one of the jade burial goods and moved up and down to scan it, as if it was appraising the jade’s value.

Lu Yang was stunned, his heart thumping against his chest. Could Family Head Shang have given me an incredible appraisal-type magical artifact?

Then, they saw light enveloping the burial item as four words appeared on the light screen.

Five years of imprisonment.

After the light shifted, it shrouded another burial item—a sharp, bronze, small sword.

The characters on the light screen changed again.

Seven years of imprisonment.

Lu Yang, “...”

Family Head Shang, what on earth is this book you have given me?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clicked her tongue in awe. So this is the current trend for books? I’ve learned something new.

1. ”Ba,” “Hanba” or “Nüba” is a drought demon in Chinese mythology. ☜

2. This line is from the well-known Candle in the Tomb series, which is about tomb raiding. Apparently, this was gibberish a character had chanted to sound impressive. ☜

Chapter 123: The Tomb Owner

Just as the screen of light was about to display “life imprisonment,” Lu Yang snapped the Tomb Raiding Takeaways closed, and only then did the flickering screen vanish.

This time, Lu Yang no longer used the excuse of “this is a hallmark of the era.” The book’s functions were truly absurd with a trace of rationality within the absurdity, which made it all the more absurd.

Fortunately, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s interest was fickle; the burial items now attracted her attention. Since the ancient era was too distant in the past, the norms and styles of burial goods had changed considerably.

For instance, the people in ancient times believed that they would head to the Nine Netherworlds[1] after they died. If they wanted to maintain their prestige and authority in the afterlife, they needed humans to accompany them as burial items. When later generations opened the tombs of ancient experts, they would often find a heap of bones as burial goods. Nowadays, people were more civilized and replaced humans with terracotta soldiers.

This reminded the Everlasting Immortal Fairy of something. “I remember that the Heaven Mandate Immortal was originally some old fellow’s burial item. Fortunately, the Heaven Mandate Immortal was lucky and managed to cheat death by feigning death, so he was brought into the tomb alive. After entering the tomb, he deactivated the feigned death technique and wantonly amassed an enormous amount of herbs and magical treasures. As the old fellow firmly believed that he would be reincarnated, he had stored several types of rare natural treasures that enhanced one’s constitution, all of which became a windfall for the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

“Seizing this opportunity, he purged his marrow, shed his mortal body for an immortal bone, and boosted his constitution. After escaping from the tomb, he had a constant stream of fortuitous encounters which allowed his foundation to grow, and he gradually gained fame, eventually rising to prominence among the younger generation and becoming a main character of the Great Era.

“Only then could he barely qualify to be my opponent.”

Initially, Lu Yang thought that the Heaven Mandate Immortal was a formidable existence. Once he heard that the latter was barely qualified as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s opponent, he decisively pulled him to the same level as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Are there ranks among immortal beings, such as Immortal and Heaven Immortal?” Lu Yang asked.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy realized that Lu Yang had misunderstood and explained, “The Heaven Mandate Immortal’s title is ‘Heaven Mandate,’ and his identity is an immortal being, so he is referred to as the Heaven Mandate Immortal. He believes that he was born under the mandate of heaven and sees himself as the protagonist of heaven and earth, so he gave himself the title of ‘Heaven Mandate.’

“There are no ranks among immortal beings. Everyone’s Dao Fruit is different, which makes it hard to distinguish which is better, so how do we classify the ranks?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words comforted Lu Yang. She could actually be a bit useful. Unfortunately, there are no history examinations on the Central Continent, otherwise, I could have scored full marks.

Alternatively, if Lu Yang’s results were not ideal, the examiner would claim that all his answers were wrong by backing it up with his hundred years of research into what the ancient period was like. At the same time, the people around him would mock Lu Yang for his ignorance and for being too full of himself, having the audacity to doubt the examiner’s answers.

It would be at this moment that Lu Yang revealed his identity as the vessel of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and slapped everyone’s face on the spot. A drape of silence would then fall over the crowd, and nobody would dare to question Lu Yang’s opinions on the ancient period anymore.

That sounds awesome.

Lu Yang had already imagined scenarios where he could pretend to be a big shot, but he could find no opportunity to apply them.

The Everlasting Immortal stopped sharing stories from ancient times, excitedly observing the various burial goods instead.

Lu Yang hadn’t relaxed his guard, and he continued to learn more about tomb raiding. “As a tomb raider, one must always remain vigilant. Even if you find the main chamber and discover burial items there, you can’t let your guard down. Some tomb owners absolutely loathe being disturbed and would set vicious traps in the main chamber, so be extremely careful...”

“Kid, go forward and take a look. Is this something from your era? It looks quite fun,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy urged Lu Yang as something caught her attention.

Just as Lu Yang took a step forward, he felt like he stepped on something, seemingly a stone tile that could sink.

Lu Yang's forehead immediately broke out in cold sweat as it dawned upon him that he had stepped on a trap. What would it be? Poison needles darting out from the ground? Rain of arrows shooting out from the walls?

There was no time for Lu Yang to think so much. Counting on his instincts, he leaped backward, attempting to evade the mechanism’s covert weapons. With the mechanism triggered, the luminous pearl above them suddenly burst forth with a brightness similar to that of a small sun. The whole chamber was illuminated, completely dispelling the eerie and frightening atmosphere from earlier.

Time passed by, and Lu Yang still didn’t notice any changes; his eyelid twitched. “So that was just a switch for turning on the lights?”

“What’s turning on the lights?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t heard of this expression before.

“Nothing.”

The more Lu Yang thought about it, the more he felt that this tomb emanated an absurd aura. Having it built against the cliff wall can still be explained as a security measure against theft, but aren’t you going too far by labeling the entrance with “Main Chamber” and having lights that can be turned on inside the main chamber?

Is this what a normal tomb ought to have?

At the very least, there were no such mentions in the Tomb Raiding Takeaways. However, it did contain one warning—the more it defies common sense, the more dangerous it is.

“No need to worry, with me around, there’d be no accidents!” After the lights were turned on, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s courage had visibly swelled, and even her voice exuded confidence.

With the luminous pearl illuminating the tomb like it was daytime, even if a ghost appeared, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would dare go over and slap it twice to let it know what a real ghost was!

As a dignified immortal, how could I possibly fear ghosts?

“That book on your left is a little interesting. Take a look.”

Lu Yang picked up the book and read out the title softly, “Tomb-Raiding Notes?” [2]

“Move your thumb; there’s another word,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said.

Lu Yang moved his thumb away, revealing the full title of the book—Anti-Tomb-Raiding Notes.

Lu Yang, “...”

He gingerly put away the Tomb Raiding Takeaways, afraid that some mystical reaction might occur between the two books if they were in proximity.

Flipping through the book, Lu Yang found that it was as the title suggested. The content described how to reasonably arrange a tomb that wouldn’t be visited by tomb raiders while offering mitigation strategies to tackle common tomb-raiding tactics. It was quite professional.

As the saying went, “For every chi of a devil, there is a zhang of Dao—it takes constant vigilance to stave off evil; such is the principle of nature.”

Lu Yang felt that if he could learn both the Tomb Raiding Takeaways and the Anti-Tomb-Raiding Notes, there would be no tomb in the world he couldn’t raid.

Retracting his gaze from the book, he turned to the tombstone on his right, which should indicate the identity of the tomb owner.

Time to see who created such a bizarre tomb.

Leaning over, the content he saw on the stele caused his hair to stand on end as he jumped back in fright.

The stele wrote:

Qin Jiunian rests here.

“Who is Qin Jiunian? Why are you reacting so strongly?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was puzzled.

Lu Yang’s voice was quivering, “Qin Jiunian...is the Dao-Seeking Sect’s First Elder!”

What on earth is going on? Is it a case of having the same name, or has First Elder fallen? If First Elder has passed away, then who is the one active in the Dao-Seeking Sect right now? Is he an imposter? What is his motive?

“First Elder is often elusive and has Senior Brother Dai Bufan oversee the Great Mission Hall in his stead. Could he be worried about his identity being exposed and deliberately reduced interactions with others?”

A torrent of questions flooded his mind, but the answer was still far from reach.

Right then, the coffin trembled, as if something was breaking free from its restraints and emerging from within!

1. Just like how there are nine layers of heaven, there are also nine places of hell. Jiuyou or the Nine Netherworlds could also refer to the deepest part of the netherworld. ☜

2. This is also the title of a popular series called The Lost Tomb, again about tomb raiding. ☜

Chapter 124: First Elder

Shock seized Lu Yang, his heart palpitating against his chest.

The coffin in the main chamber was a sarcophagus. Inscribed on it were complex and ancient patterns of the sun, moon, and stars. It was unclear which era it had been crafted, but its grand specifications certainly indicated that a puissant personage was inside.

And the Dao-Seeking Sect’s First Elder fit the criterion of “puissant personage.”

“Could the one buried inside really be the Dao-Seeking Sect’s First Elder?!” Lu Yang was on high alert, as if a formidable opponent had confronted him. Did I trigger some mechanism and resurrect the other party? Or did the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Dao Fruit revive the corpse? Or is there some other unknown reason?

The lid of the coffin slowly levitated, and an elderly man with a beard sat up from within the coffin. As soon as Lu Yang laid eyes on him, his pupils constricted.

It’s really the Dao-Seeking Sect’s First Elder!

As First Elder had been to Heaven’s Gate Peak to ask Yun Zhi about some matters, Lu Yang was not a stranger to his appearance.

Lu Yang contemplated whether he should perform the Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist to summon Yun Zhi or use Close Horizon From Cliff to once again teleport himself over a cliff.

It was then that First Elder’s weathered voice interrupted Lu Yang. Confusion clouded his gaze as he looked toward Lu Yang. “Lu Yang? Why are you here?”

Lu Yang was startled. According to his conjecture, the First Elder currently in the Dao-Seeking Sect was an imposter, while the one inside the coffin was the real deal. But I’ve only seen the fake First Elder before, so how could this First Elder recognize me?

“First Elder, you know me?” Lu Yang asked gingerly.

Inside his mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted. Lu Yang has never shown me such respect before. I’m an immortal, yet this kid Lu Yang has no sense of reverence toward me at all!

First Elder was even more bewildered at Lu Yang’s question. “Of course, I know you. Aren’t you Old Nine’s disciple, Lu Yang with the Sword Spirit Root? I also saw you through the water mirror back when you were participating in the sect’s selection trials.

“I should be the one asking you. Why are you coming here for no reason and disrupting my sleep?”

“Sl-sleep?” Lu Yang’s brain was struggling to rotate its gear in the corresponding direction. Who would sleep in a coffin for no reason?

First Elder yawned widely with tears at the corners of his eyes, clearly looking like he had just woken up. “I was too exhausted from building the tomb just now, so I decided to take a quick nap. I’m really getting old. I was never this tired in the past. I have to acquiesce to the reality of old age. Speaking of which, I’m already three thousand years old.”

“Build a tomb?” Lu Yang’s eyes widened. He had heard that when some cultivators sensed that their time was approaching, they would draft their wills beforehand, arrange the matters after their passing, and build a tomb.

Remembering First Elder’s contribution to the Dao-Seeking Sect, a wave of anguish hit him. “Are you about to...about to...” He couldn’t bring himself to utter the remaining words.

First Elder nodded. “That’s right, it’s about time to think of what I want to do after retirement. Dai Bufan said that I can still live another five thousand years after retiring and that I should find some hobbies. I thought about it and felt that building tombs is not a bad choice; I’ll end up using it sooner or later.”

Lu Yang, “...”

He had been caught up by the atmosphere such that his mind temporarily short-circuited. Only now did he recall that Fusion cultivators could live at least eight thousand years. Someone with such high cultivation like First Elder would certainly live much longer.

Give me back the emotions you cheated from me!

“You’re building a tomb so early?” Lu Yang said inwardly, This hobby of yours is really unique.

“What’s wrong with that? I heard that in some places, mortals would borrow a huge sum from the banks to buy a house, then repay the debt with a lifetime of hard work. If mortals can toil their whole lives for a house, there’s naturally no problem with me hammering away at building tombs for the latter half of my life.”

Lu Yang was rendered speechless by First Elder’s reasoning.

“This is not the only tomb I’ve built. There are others already constructed elsewhere. The one here is only at the preliminary stage. I haven’t even prepared the jiangshi yet, so I temporarily threw in a few White Jiangshi to maintain the atmosphere.

“By the way, I specifically chose a cliff wall of the Dao-Seeking Sect to build this tomb. How did you find your way here?”

Lu Yang fell silent, not keen on recalling the process. So I am still in the Dao-Seeking Sect. It seems like the teleportation distance wasn’t that far.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy commented lazily, “You definitely couldn’t have teleported far. The teleportation distance is closely related to one’s cultivation realm. You’re only at the Foundation Establishment Stage, so how far can you go? Did you really think you could ascend to the heavens?”

Meanwhile, First Elder wasn’t aware of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence.

Lu Yang tried to rationalize. “So the reason you’re often not in the Great Mission Hall is...”

“I have handed things over to Little Dai so that I can enjoy my retirement life earlier.”

Very reasonable.

Seeing that Lu Yang was not willing to elaborate on how he had gotten here, he instead asked, “Do you need me to send you back?”

Lu Yang hurriedly nodded. That’s exactly what I’m hoping for.

First Elder came out of the coffin and tapped Lu Yang, who immediately got engulfed in a gigantic bubble. As First Elder flew out of the tomb with his hands behind his back, the bubble containing Lu Yang followed.

In the blink of an eye, First Elder had already left the cliff. Only then did Lu Yang understand why First Elder had encased him in a bubble—his body was unable to withstand First Elder’s speed.

After departing from the cliff, they were greeted by an endless expanse of grassland with verdant grass that resembled a carpet. The prairie was dotted with sheeps grazing on tender grass and various demon beasts from the wilderness. Terrifying aura waves that emanated from the beasts made Lu Yang’s heart shudder.

Back when I joined the sect, I remember Big Senior Sister saying, “There are also some dangerous areas—inadequate cultivation would result in death.” This must be what she was alluding to. With my cultivation, there’s no way I can safely fall from a cliff... Why does this sentence sound so awkward?

As Lu Yang flew with First Elder, due to the immense speed, it was impossible to see the scenery below, so fear of heights was no longer a problem.

That said, during the journey, Lu Yang was a little apprehensive. Based on First Elder’s flying speed, we still haven’t reached Heaven’s Gate Peak even after flying for so long. Exactly how far away was I teleported?

Just as his thoughts started to run wild, First Elder stopped, and Lu Yang realized that they had already arrived at Heaven’s Gate Peak.

First Elder placed Lu Yang down, then turned to leave. He had encountered a challenge with his cultivation when he was sleeping in the coffin, so he wanted to consult his junior brothers for their opinions.

He went to the herb garden, but Second Elder was not around.

He went to the Physique Refinement Peak, but Third Elder was not around.

He went to the Gentleman Peak, but Fourth Elder was also not around.

“Where’s everyone?” First Elder was bewildered. I don't remember Old Two, Old Three, and Old Four being the type to wander around. I could always find them when I needed to. Why is there not a single person to be found today?

Fourth Elder’s eldest disciple, Ji Hongwen saw that First Elder was looking for his master and informed him, “It appears that Shifu has located the whereabouts of the sect leader and has gone to Heaven’s Gate Peak with Second Elder.”

“Old Nine’s whereabouts? Heaven’s Gate Peak?” First Elder could not have anticipated that he would be heading back to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

Arriving at Heaven’s Gate Peak, he asked Lu Yang if he knew where the Taciturn Daoist Priest was. Following the direction Lu Yang pointed him toward, he successfully went inside the pine first and found his six junior brothers and one junior sister enjoying hotpot together, along with the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

When the Taciturn Daoist Priest saw First Elder standing outside the cave abode, he waved enthusiastically. “It’s been a long time since we gathered together. Look, we’re just about to have hotpot together. You came at the right time, Big Senior Brother!”

“Big Senior Brother, come in quickly. You’re the only one left!”

First Elder eyed the overly zealous Taciturn Daoist Priest with suspicion.

Chapter 125: The Dao-Seeking Nine Gathered Together

In First Elder’s memory, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was only this ebullient when a conspiracy was involved.

First Elder had his guard up.

He believed that the Taciturn Daoist Priest totally had reasons to sabotage him. When the Taciturn Daoist Priest was just an infant, he was carried up the mountain by Third Elder, becoming the youngest disciple. Neither his master nor his senior brothers and sisters had experience caring for a baby, so they gradually fumbled their way through.

The Taciturn Daoist was a restless child; he could never fall asleep. Since First Elder was proficient in dreamscape spells, he used them to help the Taciturn Daoist Priest sleep soundly. When the Taciturn Daoist Priest reached an age where he could cultivate, he would often doze off while training. First Elder would then cast his dreamscape spells to startle him awake. Perhaps he had also frightened the Taciturn Daoist Priest so much that he still bore trauma from those times.

Noticing First Elder’s wariness, the seven elders also beckoned, “Big Senior Brother, come on in! We’re just waiting for you to start the hotpot!”

We can’t be the only unlucky fellows. By hook or by crook, the Dao-Seeking Nine must be assembled today!

The eight of them stood at the cave entrance, beaming widely as they called out to First Elder, yet not one dared to take a step out of the cave. From an outsider’s perspective, this scene would look especially peculiar.

In First Elder’s memory, his seven junior brothers and sisters had never been this enthusiastic before.

With plenty of experience gained in the past two thousand years, First Elder swiftly made sense of the situation. It’s an illusion!

He bit down on his tongue. Despite his attempt to use the blood from his tongue to break the illusory cage, he observed that nothing changed.

Could it be that it’s not an illusion?

I remember Lu Yang saying that Yun Zhi sealed Old Nine in a cave abode, but how did everyone else from Old Two to Old Eight also get sealed?

“So, how did all of you get sealed?”

Eighth Elder put on an earnest expression. “Big Senior Brother, here’s what happened. We heard that Yun Zhi sealed Old Nine, so we came here to check on him right away. Old Nine said that this seal cannot trap smart people. Since the seven of us believed that we were smart people, we assumed the seal couldn’t lock us in, so we each decided to give it a try and came in one after another. But well, you can see what happened.”

First Elder raised an eyebrow. “So mystical? Let me try.”

First Elder walked inside the cave abode.

Everyone cheered out loud.

Technically, what Eighth Elder said wasn’t entirely wrong. After all, which smart person would willingly get sealed?

As such, the Dao-Seeking Nine were rounded up—a cause worthy of celebration.

As the nine gathered around the hotpot, the entire cave was permeated with mist, resembling a hotpot-flavored immortal paradise. All the ingredients were provided by Third Elder. As he was a physique cultivator, he regularly consumed natural treasures, demon beasts, and spirit meat to replenish his body’s energy.

When First Elder heard everyone clarify the reason, his face had turned darker than a storm. So the eight of you were trapped here, but instead of seeking help, you were plotting how to drag someone else down into this mess?

Grandpa Ba stood forth. “It’s not that we didn’t want to get out, but Old Nine said that if we wanted to leave, the only way is to conquer our heart devil. However, our heart devils were too strong for any of us to defeat. That is why we joined forces and came up with some other ideas.

“For instance, Old Three proposed to use a spoon to dig a passage out.

“For instance, Old Four suggested shouting for help loudly to call Junior Niece Yun Zhi over.

“For instance, Old Five recommended refining the spoon into a magical treasure before digging the passage.

“For instance, Old Six...”

First Elder raised his hand, interrupting the jailbreak plan of the Dao-Seeking Nine. “Why did I hear Lu Yang say that as long as you sit in meditation properly for three days, the seal will automatically be removed? He even told me that this has been mentioned to Old Nine, so the seal should have already been lifted by now.”

First Elder wasn’t a fool; he had walked in confidently not because he was hoodwinked but because he knew the real way to leave.

Eight frigid gazes bore into the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

He calmly said, “I have made considerable contributions to the sect. Before you make a move, can you let me write a will first?”

~~~

While Lu Yang was sitting in a meditative position, he suddenly felt Heaven’s Gate Peak shake a bit, though he did not know what had happened. There’s still someone brave enough to make a move on Heaven’s Gate Peak?

Fortunately, Heaven’s Gate Peak only shook once before returning to normal, so Lu Yang didn’t think much of it. Stepping into the array left by Yun Zhi which separated the disturbances from the external world, he adjusted his breath and focused on breaking past the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage.

Yun Zhi didn’t guard his cultivation at the side, for breaking through to the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage was a natural progression for Lu Yang that would occur when the conditions were right, and accidents were unlikely to happen.

Moments later, the essence, qi, and consciousness within him reached a peak, and his psyche became clear and bright. He performed the Clear Heart and True Nature Mantra, devouring the surrounding spirit energy, as vast waves of spirit energy washed over his body.

When ordinary people broke through to either the Basic, Intermediate, or Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, they would seize the opportunity to purge their marrow, transform themselves inside out, mend the seams in their cultivation, and heal the scars left from battles.

However, this step was unnecessary for Lu Yang. He had already completely purified his marrow during the Qi Training Stage, so there were no more impurities to expel. After reaching the Foundation Establishment Stage, Lu Yang’s cultivation technique could ensure that his body remained pure at all times. Regardless of what he ate or absorbed, he could retain their essence and discharge the dross.

The “clear” in the Clear Heart and True Nature Mantra didn’t refer only to the heart but also the body!

From the Foundation Establishment Stage onward, a liquid vortex of spirit energy would form at the cultivator’s dantian. A fiery sensation pulsed through Lu Yang’s dantian. Channeling his vision inward, he could distinctly feel that the liquid vortex in his dantian was growing stronger, swallowing the external world’s spirit qi and generating a purer spirit energy that was suitable for himself.

Activating his Macrocosmic Loop[1], pure spirit energy continuously circulated in his body, strengthening every part of his body.

The vortex spun faster and faster, and spirit energy flowed through his body at incredulous speed. Finally, he felt the spirit energy forcefully break through a barrier.

Lu Yang opened his eyes, his gaze bright and clear.

Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage. Success.

Outside the array, after the puppet observed that Lu Yang had advanced to the Intermediate Foundation Establishment in a stable manner and without complications, it stood up and left.

Lu Yang suddenly recalled something from the Foundation Establishment Manual. “There’s one thing left to do.”

The Foundation Establishment Manual recorded Seventh Elder’s takeaways from breaking through to the Foundation Establishment Stage and was supplemented by various senior brothers and sisters; it clearly outlined all kinds of possible scenarios one might face.

Lu Yang gathered spirit qi in his right hand and gently tapped the lower right side of his abdomen, and he suddenly spat out a chunk of meat. The meat chunk was bloody, seeming to be a part of Lu Yang.

With a burst of sword qi, Lu Yang smashed the meat chunk into powder.

“What’s this?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had watched the process of Lu Yang’s advancement, but she had kept silent all this while for fear of distracting him. Now that he had successfully reached the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage, she could finally speak.

That was suffocating!

Lu Yang explained earnestly, “Have you heard of this saying before? One mustn’t engage in vigorous exercise after a meal. Intense activity can lead to acute abdominal pain, and in severe cases, it may be so painful that one rolls on the ground with beads of sweat the size of yellow beans covering their foreheads. That’s very detrimental to cultivation.

“Through research, the senior brothers and sisters of the Dao-Seeking Sect have found that as long as one cuts off a small piece of useless flesh during the progression to the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage, they can prevent such occurrences and even move as they wish after a meal.”

“So you were just...”

“Cutting off the appendix.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “...”

I can’t seem to keep up with the mindsets of cultivators nowadays.

1. Dazhoutian is a technique in one of the main schools of Qigong. ☜

Chapter 126: Qingfeng Sword’s Small Accessory

Ever since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been resurrected, she had suffered consecutive setbacks and traumatic blows. First, she failed to frighten Lu Yang and ended up getting beaten by Yun Zhi instead. Then, she tried to prove her worth by attempting to control Lu Yang and battle beyond his level, only to be taught a lesson.

Now, she realized that clinging on to her past experiences wouldn’t work. The thought process of cultivators nowadays was much more dynamic than those in ancient times. They even worked together and accumulated cultivation experiences across various realms, something that would have been unimaginable in ancient times. There was no shortage of overt and covert machinations between senior and junior brothers; they would scheme against one another and vie over resources. How could sects and tribes unconditionally share their cultivation experiences?

Oh, there was one exception—the Ancient Barbarian Tribe. They liked discussing their cultivation experiences within their own tribe.

Lu Yang stretched lazily before standing up to perform a set of radio calisthenics. As he loosened his muscles and heard the satisfying crack of his bones, he felt inexplicably comfortable.

“Where are you planning to go?”

“Hundred Refinements Peak. I want to get a custom-made weapon.”

Upon arriving at the Hundred Refinements Peak, Lu Yang saw that the dining hall was as lively as ever.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy exclaimed, “Eh? The food in your sect looks pretty good. So many disciples are coming here to buy the food.”

Lu Yang nodded. “The food quality is indeed pretty good.”

However, the purpose of this visit was not the dining hall but the Hundred Refinements Hall halfway up the mountain on the other side.

The dining hall sold common weapons, which were good but not necessarily suitable for everyone. And thus, the Hundred Refinements Hall was born. They specialized in selling customized weapons and had grand artifact-crafting masters stationed there.

“You are...Senior Brother Lu Yang?” a surprised voice called out to Lu Yang at the entrance of the Hundred Refinements Hall.

Lu Yang immediately recognized who the other party was. “You are Li Haoran, from my cohort!”

In Lu Yang’s cohort, there were altogether three people with a Single Spirit Root: Lu Yang with his Sword Spirit Root, Meng Jingzhou with his Single’s Spirit Root, and Li Haoran with his Fire Spirit Root.

“More than a month ago, I heard Senior Sister Zhou Lulu say that you were soaking in lava. You finally managed to come out?”

At the mention of the lava bath, Li Haoran’s expression visibly turned grim, as if he was recalling some very unpleasant experiences. “I finally met Shifu’s expectations to learn to swim in lava, eat fire salamanders raw, and successfully reached the Foundation Establishment Stage. In fact, I just came out. I was about to look for Shifu and ask him what the next steps are, but Senior Sister Zhou Lulu said that she hasn’t seen Shifu for three days and doesn’t know where he has gone.”

Lu Yang thought to himself, Could it be that Fifth Elder and Shifu share a close bond, so he decided to accompany Shifu in meditation?

“After progressing to the Foundation Establishment Stage, you need to go to the Great Mission Hall to take on missions for the sect.”

Li Haoran nodded; he had heard of this from his senior brothers.

“Do you know the way? Why don’t I go with you?” He does call me “Senior Brother Lu Yang” after all, so I should also fulfill my duties as a senior brother.

“Thank you then, Senior Brother.”

On the way to the Great Mission Hall, Lu Yang learned more about Li Haoran’s background. Both of his parents were cultivators, though they were only at the Foundation Establishment Stage. When his parents found out that their son had a Fire Spirit Root, no words could describe how elated they were, and they showered him with as much affection as they could.

This also resulted in Li Haoran becoming condescending and irascible. A reflection of this was when they were climbing the Heart-Seeking Mountain. Li Haoran’s Dao heart wasn’t steadfast, so everyone else with poorer talents reached the fiftieth step before he did, and he came in last place.

Lu Yang’s conjecture was that Fifth Elder, Zhou Xin, had discerned Li Haoran’s weakness and deliberately made him soak in lava for a year to temper his Dao heart.

And it looked like it worked very well.

In the Great Mission Hall, the two still couldn’t find a suitable mission for Li Haoran even after searching one round.

“By the way, can you craft artifacts?”

“Of course! Shifu said that my skill in crafting artifacts is already at the pinnacle of Foundation Establishment cultivators.” Those with a Fire Spirit Root were the most suited for crafting weapons, and Li Haoran had also studied knowledge on crafting weapons for a year in the lava.

“How about this? I’ll post an artifact-crafting mission, and you’ll accept it. You can complete a mission and I can also achieve my goal of getting a weapon crafted.” Lu Yang had already thought this through. The artifact-crafting masters in the Hundred Refinements Hall were at least from the Golden Core Stage, and their prices were exorbitant, but the weapon he had in mind didn’t need such a high-level artifact-crafting master.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, you don’t have to accommodate me. I can just come back to the Great Mission Hall in a few days.”

Lu Yang shook his head. “I’m not accommodating you. I just happen to need a weapon to be crafted, and you’re the most suitable choice.”

“The most suitable?” Li Haoran felt rather flattered.

Lu Yang nodded. “Yes, you are the cheapest.”

Li Haoran, “...”

After the two returned to Li Haoran’s artifact-crafting room, Lu Yang took out his Qingfeng Sword, giving Li Haoran a fright. The quality of the Qingfeng Sword is outrageously high. It’s far beyond what a Foundation Establishment cultivator like me can modify.

“No, no, no, Senior Brother Lu, you should find someone else. My skills are limited. I can’t forge a sword like this.”

Lu Yang laughed. “You've misunderstood. I’m not asking you to craft this sword. I simply want to add a small accessory to the sword’s exterior.”

Li Haoran heaved a sigh of relief. That’s simple. “Do you have a sketch?”

“Yes.” Lu Yang had come prepared and pulled out a drawing that was four meters wide, hardly looking like the “small accessory” he was talking about.

When Li Haoran saw the contents of the drawing, his expression became even stranger. Crafting this isn’t difficult, but this thing looks nothing like an ornament. At the very least, I’ve never seen a decorative item like this before.

“I’m planning to learn the Flying Sword Technique soon. I’m a sword cultivator after all. I gotta know how to use a sword. But flying around in the sky with no traffic rules is so dangerous. Out of safety considerations, I came up with this design. Here's the drawing.

“When I’m using the Flying Sword Technique, I intend to sit inside a steel shell, and the flying sword shall be fixed beneath the steel shell to provide motive power. A chair will be mounted inside the steel shell for sitting. Also, let’s install two rows of seats. After I’ve mastered the Flying Sword Technique, I can take others with me to fly in the sky too.

“This thing is called a steering wheel, and it can adjust the direction.
