“There are also windows. Mortals can’t use sand to refine glass, but it shouldn’t be a problem for us cultivators, right?

“In theory, there should be brakes, but since the source of motive power comes from me, we can do without the brakes; I can just use my feet...

“By the way, this big steel shell must be easy to install and dismantle, otherwise, it would be inconvenient during battles. “

As Lu Yang carefully elucidated the functions and the crafting requirements of the small accessory, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Li Haoran felt as if they had opened their eyes to a whole new world.

“It’s not that I have a fear of heights. I just find flying alone too lonely, so I wanted to bring a few more people along.” Lu Yang stressed repeatedly that he wasn’t afraid of heights. “Can you do it?”

Li Haoran contemplated for a bit. Although the thing in the drawing is bizarre, it’s not hard to craft. The only possible issue is that I haven’t crafted something like this before, so I’ll need to practice a few more times. “Sure, I can do it.”

“That’s great. These are Dark Lightning Metal to be used as the material. There’s this mask too. You can also refine it to make it tougher so that it doesn’t break easily.” Lu Yang whipped out the tofu mask. I’ll need a false identity when I go out next time.

Lu Yang took the initiative to offer, “As for the price, how about twenty contribution points?”

Twenty contribution points were equivalent to two thousand spirit stones; it was definitely not a low price.

Li Haoran accepted the mission.

Chapter 127: Flying With a Sword

Lu Yang stayed at the Hundred Refinements Peak for three days. during which he constantly discussed with Li Haoran how to better craft the flying sword’s accessory.

“It has to be as light as possible, otherwise, it can’t fly or it will fly too slowly.

“Say, do you think we should install an ejection seat so that in case of danger, it will automatically launch you upward and let you escape?

“Should the flying sword be mounted on top of the head? Nah, that won’t do. This is a proper Flying Sword Technique. Have you seen any sword cultivator with a flying sword perched on top of their head?”

Efforts paid off; after three days of hard work, the accessory was finally crafted.

“Why don’t you give it a name?” LI Haoran suggested.

“It looks like a carriage and can fly in the sky. Why don’t I call it a flying carriage?”[1] Lu Yang came up with a fairly plain name.

“Senior Brother Lu, why don’t you give it a try?” With the completion of the hanging accessory, Li Haoran was brimming with accomplishment and couldn’t wait to see how Lu Yang was going to fly into the sky.

Lu Yang nodded, rather excited. He sat inside the carriage and grabbed the steering wheel with both hands, but nothing happened.

“What’s wrong?” Li Haoran asked.

Lu Yang scratched his head. “I just remembered that I haven’t learned the Flying Sword Technique.”

Li Haoran, “...”

I was so zealous in crafting this for so long, and now you’re telling me you don’t even know how to fly?

“Don’t worry, I’ll learn it right now.” Lu Yang was unflustered as he asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to teach him the Flying Sword Technique.

The Flying Sword Technique was a mandatory spell for all sword cultivators and was also ubiquitous, so the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could naturally perform such an entry-level technique.

Truth be told, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t very keen on teaching Lu Yang. If he learns it the wrong way, my reputation of a lifetime will be tarnished and buried in dust.

“The so-called Flying Sword Technique uses the sword as a medium to carry one’s spiritual consciousness. The stronger one’s spiritual consciousness is, the higher the compatibility with the sword, and the faster the speed of the flying sword...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was far better than Yun Zhi in teaching, explaining the concepts in a way that was easy to understand. Before long, Lu Yang had picked up the Flying Sword Technique.

The Qingfeng Sword floated in the air and moved around freely. Lu Yang believed that it could still fly smoothly even if an elephant were to step on it.

Lu Yang’s talent in the Dao of Sword was indisputable.

He sensed an epiphany. Perhaps this is the function of the Sword Spirit Root. It can ensure that I won’t go off-kilter when learning sword techniques.

There was a groove beneath the flying carriage, and the Qingfeng Sword could be securely lodged right there.

Lu Yang got into the carriage again and gripped the steering wheel while activating the Flying Sword Technique. This time, the flying carriage began lifting off with the propulsion from the Qingfeng Sword.

It first hovered slowly; this wasn’t due to the Qingfeng Sword but because Lu Yang hadn’t completely gotten used to this completely new method of flight. By the time the flying carriage hovered at a high altitude, Lu Yang had gradually mastered the flying technique and flew increasingly faster, flying in an “8” pattern. By the end of his practice, he could already make sharp turns. It was simply inconceivable!

With the physique of an Intermediate Foundation Establishment cultivator, Lu Yang faced none of the problems like oxygen deprivation or pressure.

“Haha! I, Lu Yang, can also fly with a sword now!” Lu Yang laughed heartily. I knew that every problem has a solution. Who’s gonna say that I don’t dare to fly?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also found it novel.

On the Hundred Refinements Peak, numerous people looked up at Lu Yang flying with his sword, their eyes wide and mouths agape.

Even for the Hundred Refinements Peak, which prided itself on being progressive and at the forefront of trends, an advanced mode of transportation like the flying carriage was still revolutionary.

“Quick, look! What’s that?!” The disciples from Lu Yang’s cohort gazed at the flying steel shell in astonishment.

“I saw this when I was consulting Senior Brother Li Haoran yesterday. It’s a magical treasure for Senior Brother Lu!”

“Senior Brother Lu? The one from our cohort who possesses a Sword Spirit Root, ranked first place, and successfully became the sect leader’s disciple?” One junior male disciple’s eyes widened in admiration for Lu Yang.

If one didn’t interact with Lu Yang directly, they would be astounded by his lifetime accomplishments and think of him as a safe, steady, and reliable senior brother. Of course, those who didn’t change their initial impression even after long-term interactions with Lu Yang also existed—Man Gu was a prime example.

“Yes, that’s him! I heard Senior Brother Li say that this is Senior Brother Lu’s Flying Sword Technique!”

“Wow, that’s amazing! This is totally different from the Flying Sword Techniques I’ve seen before. It gives people an inexplicable sense of security. There’s no need to buy insurance at all!”

Among the various insurance policies offered by the Luodi Merchant Guild was flight insurance, which could be further categorized into flight loss insurance, third-party liability insurance, and so on.

“Senior Brother Lu is the same age as us, yet he can already create his own unique Flying Sword Technique. Is this the gulf between us?!”

“It’s a pity that I’m not a sword cultivator. Otherwise, I would do anything to learn this type of Sword Flying Technique!”

Only until Lu Yang flew to his heart’s content did he finally land, though he looked eager for more.

After alighting, Lu Yang noticed Li Haoran standing deferentially to one side; Fifth Elder Zhou Xin had arrived at some point.

“Fifth Elder.” Lu Yang bowed respectfully.

“Hehe, Lu Yang, right? I’ve heard all about the process from Haoran. Your idea is very innovative and may even become a mainstream mode of transportation in the future.”

“You flatter me, Fifth Elder.”

“Those who are familiar with me know that I’m not in the habit of praising people. This thing called the flying carriage can bring you considerable benefits.”

“Benefits?” Lu Yang was puzzled.

Fifth Elder turned to Li Haoran. “Now that you’re also out of seclusion, you should familiarize yourself with the main business of the Hundred Refinements Peak. We often produce unprecedented artifacts, and in order to protect our intellectual property rights and reap profits, we will periodically go to the authorities to apply for patents.

“It works the same way for the Pill Cauldron Peak. This is the primary source of income for both peaks.

“You’re just in time. A few of your senior brothers will be heading down the mountain to register for patents soon. You can straighten out Lu Yang’s thought process for his innovation and accompany your senior brothers.”

Fifth Elder then said to Lu Yang, “You have good talent and a sharp mind, born suited for the Dao-Seeking Sect. Learn well from Yun Zhi, and the Dao-Seeking Sect will be yours in the future. Try to minimize contact with that old bastard Old Nine.”

Lu Yang shrank his neck. Logically speaking, as a disciple, I should be standing up for Shifu when Fifth Elder castigates him, but I think that it’s not a bad thing to adopt the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s optimistic attitude of “just back down if I can’t win.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned, sensing that Lu Yang was thinking about something quite impolite. But I have no evidence.

“How is Shifu doing now?”

Fifth Elder simply let out a cold laugh.

~~~

In the pine forest of Heaven’s Gate Peak, the seal of the cave abode was finally broken. All the elders from First Elder to Eigth Elder had long left, leaving only the unwilling Taciturn Daoist Priest behind.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was bound like a worm as he writhed on the ground with a piece of yellow paper stuck to his forehead. He was struggling to make muffled sounds with a sock stuffed in his mouth. As the rope was a top-notch treasure, the Taciturn Daoist Priest couldn’t break free with brute force, and since the yellow paper could seal one’s power, he also couldn’t cast any spell.

As for how long it would take for the Taciturn Daoist Priest to wriggle free, that would depend on what fate had in store for him.

This was punishment for the Taciturn Daoist Priest as he was causing a ruckus by the side while the eight of them were focused on meditating and attempting to break the seal.

1. The term for “carriage” is made up of “horse” and “car/vehicle.” The new name Lu Yang proposes is made up of “flying” and “car/vehicle,” so the second character used is the same. If you think of it in a modern context, it can translate to “flying car.” However, to keep to the context of the novel and retain the wordplay, I’ll be using “flying carriage.” ☜

Chapter 128: The Five Great Immortal Sects’ Secret Meeting

Representatives of the Five Great Immortal Sects were gathered on a certain mountain peak in the Dao-Seeking Sect. This was an extremely mysterious peak; only the higher-ups of the Dao-Seeking Sect were qualified to know about it.

The four representatives sat quietly, waiting for the organizer of this meeting to speak.

Sensing that everyone had arrived, Yun Zhi woke from her comprehension. As she opened her eyes, they appeared to encompass countless worlds and an infinite expanse of time and space in an extremely abstruse manner.

The four representatives were momentarily dazed when they met her gaze. Shock rattled at their hearts. They hadn’t seen Yun Zhi for several years. Back then, Yun Zhi had already emanated an air of enigma, and they didn’t expect that this sensation would only intensify now.

The Dao-Seeking Sect is sure lucky to have recruited such a genius. And she’s even the disciple of that old bastard, the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

However, Yun Zhi’s profound cultivation was a good thing for them. With the imminent arrival of the Great Era, spirit energy was abundant, various factions revealed themselves, diabolic creeds wreaked havoc, formidable beings in slumber for tens and thousands of years were awakening, and immortals belonging to the legends were gradually surfacing.

It was easy to imagine that the formidable beings and immortals wouldn’t obediently abide by the current rules; they would definitely redefine order and divide territories according to their own will. This would spell disaster for both mortals and cultivators alike.

In fact, some cultivation experts had already awakened and attempted to stir up chaos on the Central Continent, but the Five Great Immortal Sects had joined forces to kill them before they could amount to much.

Not all immortals were easygoing and easily satisfied like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy; not to mention that the Ancient Nameless One who had refined the stars into a continent was a tough nut to crack.

Under such circumstances, the stronger the Five Great Immortal Sects were, the more likely they would be able to counter the impending calamities.

Yun Zhi spoke without much emotion, “I have called all of you here today because I have obtained some intelligence about the diabolic creed to share with you.”

The four people felt a chill in their hearts. No wonder Yun Zhi didn’t use conventional methods like transmitting an auditory message but instead invited us to come in person to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s secret peak.

This secret mountain peak was sanctified by distinguished predecessors of the Dao-Seeking Sect and further modified by Yun Zhi, allowing it to obfuscate heavenly secrets and shroud karma, so there was no fear of secrets leaking.

Although the diabolic creeds were not very strong, they worshiped immortals and acquired many immortal treasures and spells from them, which were unpredictable to defend against.

“As all of you know, over a month ago, I breached the headquarters of the Everlasting Creed and came by some intelligence, among which two pieces are worthy of our attention. One is the method to resurrect the Everlasting Immortal, and the other is the matter of ‘spies.’”

The four representatives sat up straight. Resurrecting an immortal? This is extremely valuable intel.

Despite having long heard that Yun Zhi had overturned the lair of the Everlasting Creed, they never knew how she had found it.

“The Everlasting Immortal’s Dao Fruit is very special. Even if they completely perish with their soul disintegrated, as long as someone calls out their title and immortal name, be it intentionally or unintentionally, they would get resurrected!”

A thunderbolt seemed to explode in the representatives’ minds. Indeed, no immortal’s Dao Fruit is ever simple. The Dao Fruits of immortals we have in the past are all related to elevating one’s combat prowess. This is the first time we’re encountering one purely related to survival.

“The intelligence also mentions that the Everlasting Creed has planted spies in the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, Prison Suppression Sect, and Five-Elements Sect.”

In reality, this wasn’t intelligence acquired from the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters but information that Lu Yang had obtained from the inspecting officer, Tang Yunsheng.

When Tang Yunsheng assigned the undercover mission to the trio, he had mentioned that among the Five Great Immortal Sects, excluding the Hanging Monastery which was sparse with members and the Dao-Seeking Sect which had too many lunatics to plant spies, there were spies in the three other sects.

The Five Great Immortal Sects were as follows.

The Dao-Seeking Sect: The sect famous for their Dao techniques and unorthodox imagination, as well as being the plague the four other sects warned their juniors to avoid.

The Hanging Monastery: Despite embodying benevolence and once having the master and disciple as the only two members, they were a powerful entity.

The Moon Laurel Celestial Palace: With the notion that the moon harbored unspeakable secrets, they cultivated with its aid and had moon laurel trees growing all across their land.

The Prison Suppression Sect: All demons and monsters were to be suppressed here.

The Five-Elements Sect: They believed in the unity of the five elements.

The other four immortal sects felt that the Dao-Seeking Sect didn’t fit in with them.

The Dao-Seeking Sect felt that the other four immortal sects didn’t fit in with it.

Setting aside their incompatibility, the Five Great Immortal Sects maintained a good relationship.

“So it’s regarding the matter of the spies.” The palace leader of the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace was not surprised; she was Lan Ting’s master, and Lan Ting had shared with her some information.

“Amitabha.” The abbot of the Hanging Monastery did not make any comment; there were no diabolic creed spies in the Hanging Monastery. Although their small numbers were one reason, the other reason was their differing beliefs. If the people from the diabolic creed chanted sutras and adhered to precepts all day long, their Dao hearts would crumble sooner or later, so it was too easy for them to slip up and expose themselves.

“I never expected that despite the Prison Suppression Sect suppressing all evils, we would still have the Everlasting Creed infiltrating our ranks. I will definitely conduct a stringent investigation once I get back!” The sect leader of the Prison Suppression Sect was incensed, but considering the occasion, he tried not to overreact.

The sect leader of the Five-Elements Sect had a frosty gaze. “Since there are spies among us, they’re likely not just from the Everlasting Creed. Other diabolic creeds might have also planted spies. We need to investigate thoroughly.” The diabolic creeds are truly audacious to outrightly disregard the Five-Elements Sect.

The palace leader of the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace asked, “How do we ferret out the spies?”

“Doesn’t the Everlasting Creed worship the Everlasting Immortal? Why don’t we make our disciples come together and shout ‘The Everlasting Immortal is a bastard?’” The sect leader of the Five-Elements Sect proposed.

The four of them nodded in agreement.

The sect leader of the Prison Suppression Sect chimed in, “I have another method. All of us surely have a suspect list, so we can say to them, ‘The creed leader has called out the Everlasting Immortal’s immortal name, and the Everlasting Immortal has already been resurrected, so the creed leader is ordering all members to gather at the headquarters.’”

Since the righteous path wasn’t supposed to know the method to revive the Everlasting Immortal, if the other party was a spy from the Everlasting Creed, they would likely assume that whoever said this was a fellow member of the Everlasting Creed.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “We'll inadvertently alert the enemy. The suspect list comprises not only the spies from the Everlasting Creed but also the spies from the other three diabolic creeds. Once they hear you saying this, they will certainly realize that you are hunting down the spies.”

The sect leader of the Prison Suppression Sect found Yun Zhi’s reasoning sound and did not make any further suggestions.

“By the way, the Dao-Seeking Sect has no spies, right? Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi, perhaps you could share some insights and tips?” The sect leader of the Five-Elements question also garnered support from the other three representatives.

Yun Zhi furrowed her brows, a rare sight for her. This question had thrown her off. I also don’t know why the Dao-Seeking Sect has no spies from the diabolic creed and can instead have spies infiltrating the diabolic creed. “Maybe it’s because the disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect have a simple mind while the members of the diabolic creeds have convoluted thoughts, which makes them unable to disguise themselves as our disciples.”

The five of them continued brainstorming numerous devious methods to investigate the spies, with proposals from the abbot of the Hanging Monastery being the most ruthless. If these ideas were made public, the world’s impression of the five would do a complete turnaround.

After the secret meeting concluded, the five left the peak. Three of them departed the Dao-Seeking Sect, with only the Palace Leader of the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace staying behind.

“Palace Leader Luo, may I know if anything is the matter?” Yun Zhi asked Luo Hongxia, the palace leader of the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace.

Luo Hongxia summoned Lan Ting, who was unwilling to come over. “Does the Dao-Seeking Sect have a disciple called Lu Yang? I have business with him. My Lan Ting is such a good child, but he has led her astray. I want him to compensate!”

Yun Zhi replied calmly, “Then how about letting the two of them get married and become Dao partners?”

Luo Hongxia’s expression froze.

Chapter 129: The Taciturn Daoist Priest Breaks Free

Luo Hongxia departed in a hurry.

Originally, she had planned to demand an explanation from the Dao-Seeking Sect and minimally secure a promise that they would not approach Lan Ting again. But from the looks of it now, I shouldn’t dream of it. If I stayed just a moment longer, I might even lose my little disciple.

Within the cloud of smoke, Lan Ting grumbled, “Shifu, I’ve already told you I’m fine, yet you insisted on dragging me to the Dao-Seeking Sect. What would Lu Yang think of me if he finds out?!”

“Ever since you came back, you’ve been focused on developing the Automatic Barbeque Array and attempting to use Animal Form Fist to take on someone else’s appearance, yet you still say you’re fine? I’ve told you a long time ago to stay away from those of the Dao-Seeking Sect. I learned all of this from experience!

“Back when I descended the mountain to train, I met a disciple from the Dao-Seeking Sect, and we teamed up to dispel the ghost. Afterward, we stayed at an inn for a few days, but that ghost was extremely audacious. It dared to hide under the bed of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s disciple for three whole days.

“In the end, that person discovered that something was wrong and pulled the ghost out from under the bed, demanding that the ghost split the cost of the room for those three days.

“Is that the thought process of a normal person?!”

Lan Ting asked, “Who was that person?”

“The Sect Leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Taciturn Daoist Priest.”

Luo Hongxia scoffed and continued, “Another time, both of us encountered a dismemberment case. More than a dozen children had been gruesomely killed, their bodies mutilated and limbs scattered everywhere. Only a dazed little girl survived, and we stayed by her side to protect her.

“After a while, the people from the yamen came and said that when they reassembled the bodies, they realized that every corpse was missing a part, and those missing parts happened to be able to form a little girl.

“At that moment, a chill ran straight down my spine. The little girl then revealed an eerie smile and laughed creepily. The Taciturn Daoist Priest simply knocked on her head and said, ‘Hey, why are you laughing? Can’t you see that we’re discussing something?’

“And the little girl was knocked into a daze.”

Lan Ting, “...”

~~~

Concerned about his master, Lu Yang went to the pine forest on Heaven’s Gate Peak once more, where he found the Taciturn Daoist Priest bound in a unique manner.

“I didn’t know that performance art was a thing in the Dao-Seeking Sect.” Lu Yang was baffled.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest twisted and writhed vigorously, making muffled sounds that seemed to be pleas for help.

Lu Yang removed the yellow paper from his forehead, restoring the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s power. The latter untied the ropes, spat out the sock, and successfully freed himself.

Tears were brimming in the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eyes. “Good brother, from now onward, we’ll both call each other ‘shifu!’”

Lu Yang thought it might be better to keep his master tied up.

As the Taciturn Daoist Priest stepped out of the cave abode, he spread his arms wide open and faced the sunlight, embracing nature. “It’s been ten years. I’m finally free!”

A moment later, he felt that the atmosphere wasn’t grand enough, so he conjured rain in a small area above his head.

With the rain pouring down, the Taciturn Daoist Priest was soon drenched. He opened his arms wide again and embraced freedom. “Ahhh! It’s been ten years. I’m finally free!”

Perfect.

Achieving the desired effects, the Taciturn Daoist Priest dispersed the rain clouds and turned to Lu Yang. “I’m planning to go down the mountain and narrate stories in the pingshu format. Do you want to come with me?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest had not forgotten his mission.

Lu Yang was a bit tempted but shook his head. “No, I can’t. My identity is too sensitive. It would be dreadful if someone from the Everlasting Creed recognized me.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest laughed heartily. “What’s so hard about that?”

He casually swiped across Lu Yang’s face in one swift motion, and the latter’s features began to shift subtly, eventually becoming completely different from his original appearance.

“Aren’t you just afraid of being recognized by your enemies after doing something bad? I understand. I have plenty of experience in this aspect. Don’t worry, no one from the Fusion Stage can see through my disguise!”

Lu Yang wasn’t keen on learning the sources of the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s experiences, but with his current appearance, he could indeed go out with a peace of mind.

“Can I bring along a friend?”

“Of course, you can.”

Lu Yang called over Meng Jingzhou, who was in the midst of practicing his punches to temper his body. “Do you want to go out and have some fun?”

“Is it safe?”

“A big shot is taking us. It’s guaranteed to be safe.”

“Let’s go.”

After a concise question and answer session, Meng Jingzhou was prepared to go out with Lu Yang, with no questions asked about where they were going and what fun they would be having.

How can it not be fun with Lu Yang around?

Meng Jingzhou whispered, “Who’s this?” He didn’t know the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“My shifu, the Taciturn Daoist Priest,” Lu Yang introduced smugly.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest recognized Meng Jingzhou and stroked his white beard like a benevolent elder. “Young fellow from the Meng Family, I’ve heard about you from your grandfather. I even went over to have a drink at your one-month-old banquet.”[1]

“You know my grandfather?” Meng Jingzhou was somewhat surprised as he had never heard his grandfather mention this before.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest chuckled. “I’ve known your grandfather for more than a thousand years.”

After Meng Jingzhou had his appearance altered by the Taciturn Daoist Priest in the same fashion, he asked, “How are we setting off? I have a horse carriage.”

Lu Yang waved his hand. “No need for that. I’ve just learned a Flying Sword Technique.”

“But only one person can stand on one sword, right? There’s two of us here.” Meng Jingzhou raised an eyebrow.

Lu Yang proudly took out an oddly designed flying carriage from his identity jade tablet. “You can treat this as the scabbard, just that its head is a bit bigger. When I perform the Flying Sword Technique, the flying carriage can ascend to the sky and carry a total of five people!”

Meng Jingzhou circled the flying carriage twice and knocked on its shell. Hearing a solid echo, his eyes sparkled. “What a good thing! Did you invent this?”

“That’s a given.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest also nodded repeatedly. This little disciple of mine truly has remarkable talent. He’ll definitely rival me in the future!

With excitement prancing around in Lu Yang’s heart, he sat in the driver’s seat. Meng Jingzhou rode shotgun, while the Taciturn Daoist Priest sat in the rear seat. The three of them fastened their seatbelts, a sense of novelty pumping through them.

“Take off!”

The Qingfeng Sword emitted a sound like a sword’s cry, and the flying carriage soared into the clouds.

“Shifu, which way are we going?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest pointed ahead. “To the south! The south is prosperous and has many transportation routes, perfect for pingshu!”

As the flying carriage proceeded south, they would occasionally encounter flying vessels where the passengers aboard were astonished by the sight of the flying carriage.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest tapped the back seat, and an invisible shuttle-like barrier opened up, reducing air resistance. At the same time, he employed the Flying Sword Technique to assist in the flying carriage’s flight.

Detecting the aid from his master, Lu Yang received a confidence boost, and the flying carriage’s speed elevated to another level.

With Shifu here, it’s definitely very safe!

~~~

When Yun Zhi went to check on her master, the cave abode was already empty except for a golden rope, yellow talisman paper, and someone’s sock.

Upon returning to her cave abode, she found a small note left by Lu Yang at the entrance.

I am going out to travel with Shifu for a while. Don’t worry about me.

Yun Zhi became even more worried.

Our Shifu...he can’t even tell left from right.

~~~

In the skies above a small town in the west, the flying carriage malfunctioned and plummeted straight down.

1. It is a tradition to celebrate when a baby becomes one month old. ☜

Chapter 130: “Rules”

“What’s happening?” Meng Jingzhou was appalled as the flying carriage began to plummet.

Cold sweat broke out on Lu Yang’s forehead as he desperately tried to activate the Flying Sword Technique. However, the flying carriage didn’t stop descending; he had lost all control over the Qingfeng Sword, no longer able to sense its presence.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest announced gravely, “We can’t use our spirit energy here. All spells have become ineffective!”

“What?!”

With the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s extensive knowledge and experience, he could roughly guess what was happening. If this is truly what’s happening, then the three of us are truly unlucky. But now’s not the time to be thinking about this. The top priority is to save Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

He stood up and tore open the carriage’s roof, wrapping one arm around Lu Yang and the other around Meng Jingzhou. Securing them at his waist, he leaped downward. Although they couldn’t use their spirit energy here, there were no constraints on his physical body. As an expert at the Fusion Stage, nothing would happen to the Taciturn Daoist Priest even if he jumped down from the sky.

Lu Yang attempted to open his eyes a few times to check what was happening, but the strong winds during their descent prevented him and Meng Jingzhou from doing so.

Just as the three of them were about to hit the ground, the Taciturn Daoist Priest released his grip and gently held the two of them up so that he would land first. He struck the ground with such force that it created a giant crater, following which Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou landed, caught by the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

All of this happened within a second.

Had the Taciturn Daoist Priest not held them in his arms, he would have been unscathed, but Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou wouldn’t have been able to withstand the impact.

Huff, huff, huff! Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were still reeling from the shock. This trip is really unique. We crashed just as we set off.

“What is this place?” Lu Yang knitted his brow, realizing that they were in an ordinary small town. He couldn’t figure out why they were unable to use spirit energy here.

“Why is there no one showing themselves?” Lu Yang discovered a new problem. It’s past 9pm, and the flying carriage should have made quite the noise, but why is no one coming to check on the situation?

Could it be that there’s no living person in this small town? A dead town?

No, that can’t be right. The thatched cottages and inns have candles lit, and I can see shadows flitting past the paper windows. There must be people around.

What’s going on?

There was an uncanny feeling about this place.

Lu Yang turned to Meng Jingzhou, who shook his head. The latter was equally clueless about the situation.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest approached the wreckage of the flying carriage and pulled out the Qingfeng Sword from beneath it. Yun Zhi had given the Qingfeng Sword to Lu Yang, and its high quality ensured that it was impervious to such damage.

“Hold on to this for self-defense.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest handed the Qingfeng Sword to Lu Yang. The jovial expression had completely disappeared from his countenance, now replaced with solemness.

He realized that the suppression of spirit energy in this place was extremely intense; even he couldn’t activate his spirit energy.

Suddenly, a piece of paper appeared in each of their hands; both the front and back were covered in dense text.

*

Buyi Town’s Rules

Rule 1: There is no spirit qi within the town; you are unable to utilize spirit energy.

Rule 2: From 9pm to 9am, thatched cottages and inns with closed doors are absolutely safe; anywhere else is dangerous.

Rule 3: You must leave the thatched cottages or inns between 9 - 11am and not return before 7pm.

Rule 4: Be sure to fall asleep before 11pm.

Rule 5: You cannot enter the Heaven-Grade Room.[1]

Rule 6: If you hear knocking on the door or window while in a thatched cottage or inn, do not open the door or window, regardless of what the other party says.

Rule 7: There are only spotted and white dogs in the town; there are no black dogs. If you see a black dog, run immediately.

Rule 8: The private school has been abandoned for many years. There is no private school teacher in town; the sounds coming from the private school will only be of dogs barking, not students reading.

Rule 9: The person wearing gray clothes is the private school teacher. If you meet the private school teacher, you must pretend that you did not hear whatever they said.

Rule 10: Do not make eye contact with the private school teacher; if you do, you will turn into a black dog.

Rule 11: All food in the town is provided free of charge; you can help yourself to it, but never eat steamed meat buns.

Rule 12: Be wary of the people from the authorities. Those dressed in black are from the authorities; if you encounter them, run immediately and do not look back no matter what.

Rule 13: If you feel like someone is following you, firmly believe that this is an illusion. You must not show any signs of unease or irritation.

Rule 14: The body of a deceased person is called a corpse; it is normal for corpses to move.

Rule 15: If you have questions inside the inn, ask the innkeeper. If you have questions outside the inn, ask the apothecary owner. However, you cannot speak to them.

Rule 16: After entering a black door, do not speak or eat anything inside.

Rule 17: Do not easily trust the words of strangers, but everything said by someone clad in white clothes is true.

Rule 18: There is a man-eating monster inside the ancestral hall.

Rule 19: The ancestral hall is safe.

Rule 20: The townsfolk cannot disclose anything about the town to outsiders.

Rule 21: If you leave the town or kill the town mayor, you no longer need to abide by Buyi Town’s rules.

*

Both sides of the paper were filled with rules. After Lu Yang finished reading, the paper vanished into thin air.

“What is this?” A preposterous feeling crept into Lu Yang as the rules hinted at something ominous.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest said gravely, “It’s the trick of Fusion cultivators!” Upon seeing those twenty-one rules, he finally verified his suspicions.

From the amount of suppression I’m feeling, there is more than one Fusion expert!

“Disciple, Little Meng, have you heard of the ‘Imminent Arrival of the Great Era?’”

The two nodded, though they didn’t fully understand the concept as it was too vague; they didn’t know exactly what it referred to.

“There are many signs that manifest with the imminent arrival of the Great Era, and one of them is powerful beings of other eras awakening from their deep slumber! Now that spirit opportunities are clear and the scene of Dao active, it is easier to cultivate and comprehend the Dao. Some even say that it’s possible to ascend to become immortals!

“During the Great Qian and Great Yu eras, many formidable cultivators emerged, but they were limited by their comprehension and couldn’t break through further. Thus, they devised a method to enter a deep slumber by using spirit stone marrow as a vessel to seal themselves in a deathlike state. When the scene of Dao becomes active, they will awake from their deep slumber.

“After they regain their consciousness, their bodies will require some time to fully recover. Hence, in the meantime, they will use all sorts of methods to protect themselves and prevent themselves from getting exposed. Demarcating areas, creating rules, and imprisoning visitors is one such method.

“Do you know the difference between Void Refinement and Fusion cultivators?”

The two shook their heads. These were all too distant for them.

“The difference lies in whether they have mastered ‘Rules.’”

“Rules?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou subconsciously repeated.

“A Fusion cultivator can alter the rules of reality within a certain range according to their own will. However, the modification cannot be too absurd. For example, they can’t set a rule like ‘I am invincible and undying within this area.’

“When you joined the sect, the trials you faced with the River Spirit and on Heart-Seeking Mountain are reflections of these rules.

“Fusion cultivators have weaker control over rules, so they need to establish multiple rules to restrict the activities of those within their domain. Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and immortals control rules to varying degrees, with immortals being the most extreme. Upon becoming an immortal, they can condense a Dao Fruit. It represents the rules they command, and its mighty power spans the entire world.”

Lu Yang was reminded of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Dao Fruit—as long as someone called out her title and immortal name, she could be revived.

Judging by the results, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was an undying and imperishable entity. However, from the viewpoint of the whole world, this implied that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could bypass the limitations of time, space, soul, and physical body to be resurrected—a truly terrifying defiance of natural laws!

Lu Yang shared his conjecture with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, and she nodded, affirming Lu Yang’s speculation. “You have a pretty quick mind for someone so young.”

Lu Yang temporarily ignored her teasing as he listened to the Daoist Priest continue, “Based on the rules, only this town is within the other party’s control. However, the area shouldn’t be this small for a Fusion cultivator. They must be afraid of getting discovered by the immortals of the Great Xia Dynasty!

“For the rules to restrict even me, it indicates that there isn’t only one Fusion cultivator involved.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eyes gleamed ferociously, his gaze as sharp as a sword. “The Five Great Immortal Sects and the Great Xia Dynasty have already joined hands to eliminate many awakening Fusion cultivators. It looks like I can get rid of a few more today!”

With a flick of his horsetail whisk which had a tassel as fine as ox hair, he unleashed tens of thousands of sword qi. Sword Dao was the foundation of the Taciturn Daoist Priest. With a lifetime of comprehension, he could activate sword qi without using spirit energy.

The sword qi struck the town’s barrier, shattering a hole in it. At the hole, four figures awaited the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

There’s indeed more than one Fusion cultivator!

They also had to follow the rules they set. Since they couldn’t use spirit energy within the town, they planned to take care of the Taciturn Daoist Priest outside.

“Kill him!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest laughed heartily. Striding out of the town, he released the oppressive pressure of his Apex Fusion Stage cultivation as he confronted the four other Fusion cultivators. “Did you bunch of weaklings think you can kill me?”

Before departing, he left a message for Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. “This battle may last for a few days. Stay alive in the town, you two!”

The hole in the barrier closed, and the Taciturn Daoist Priest vanished outside the town.

1. You can think of the Heaven-Grade Room as something like a presidential suite in modern terms. ☜

Chapter 131: A Dangerous Night

Despite the Taciturn Daoist Priest acting tough, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou could discern that the battle was not going to conclude so easily. In fact, the best solution would have been for the Taciturn Daoist Priest to grab the two of them and flee, but he hadn’t done so, indicating that he didn’t have the confidence to protect them both from the awakened Fusion cultivators.

Lu Yang tried to summon Yun Zhi with the Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist but realized that without spirit energy, he couldn’t even transform himself.

The Lu-Style Animal Form Fist is indeed considered a spell.

Meng Jingzhou tested his current abilities. “Although I can’t tap into my powers, my physical strength hasn’t changed much.”

That’s good news.

“What time is it now?”

Lu Yang remembered that the second rule had stated, “From 9pm to 9am, thatched cottages and inns with closed doors are absolutely safe; anywhere else is dangerous.

“It was already past 9pm when our carriage fell. The streets are now empty, likely because everyone has gone home. We must find a place to stay the night or head to the inn!”

There were a few thatched cottages nearby with lights on. Meng Jingzhou knocked on one of the doors and said politely, “Fellow villager, we are cultivators who have accidentally wandered here. Please open the door and let us stay for the night. We will definitely reward you generously. Be it gold or spirit stones, you can choose as you wish!”

Meng Jingzhou tried approaching several houses, but not a single one opened their door.

Lu Yang stopped him. “Don’t waste your energy. Have you forgotten Rule 6 which states that they mustn’t open the doors when they hear a knock on the door? We are surely not the only ones in Buyi Town. There are also ordinary civilians here, and they need to abide by the rules.”

<Rule 20: The townsfolk cannot disclose anything about the town to outsiders.> This implies that there are civilians native to Buyi Town.

Meng Jingzhou wanted to say something else when Lu Yang shushed him.

From a distance came a series of clattering sounds; the footsteps and breathing sounded heavy, signifying that the visitor was colossal in size. Judging by the frequency of the footsteps, it sounded like they had four legs or even more.

Lu Yang had no idea what kind of monster it was.

He could even see the monster’s shadow around the corner.

“Run!” Lu Yang hissed, taking to his heels with Meng Jingzhou. It was unwise to confront such an adversary without a clue about the opponent’s cultivation realm and abilities.

As the two sprinted in the opposite direction of the monster, it didn’t notice them, and they soon shook off the monster. Halting in their tracks, they quietly listened for any sounds and confirmed that there were no monsters in the vicinity. Only then did they gingerly walk along the street, eventually coming across an inn.

The inn was brightly lit, with a person in white lazily slumped over the counter and two people dressed like traveling merchants discussing which room to take.

“We’ve finally found an inn. I’m beat! Give us two Heaven-Grade Rooms.” One of the traveling merchants slapped a silver ingot on the counter.

His companion quickly stopped him. “Did you forget what the paper said? We can’t stay in Heaven-Grade Rooms!”

“You actually believe that paper?”

“Better to believe it than to dismiss it.” The companion grabbed the silver ingot and looked at the white paper, intense uneasiness settling in his heart. This town is too strange. We must leave early the next morning. He smiled apologetically to the person in white. “Please give us two Earth-Grade Rooms.”

The person in white accepted the silver without giving them the change, directly handing over three keys to them. “One group can only rent one room. Here are all the three keys for Earth-Grade Room Three.”

The traveling merchant frowned. This inn is such a rip-off. How is an Earth-Grade Room worth this much?

Lu Yang reminded the traveling merchants, “You must abide by the rules on the white paper.”

The companion of the traveling merchant recalled the rules about not easily trusting the words of strangers; unable to figure out Lu Yang’s intentions, they hurried upstairs.

Just as Meng Jingzhou was about to ask for an Earth-Grade Room, Lu Yang picked up a brush and paper from the counter, pulling Meng Jingzhou behind him. The latter immediately understood what Lu Yang was up to. Rule 15: If you have questions inside the inn, ask the innkeeper. If you have questions outside the inn, ask the apothecary owner. However, you cannot speak to them.

Lu Yang wrote on the paper: Are you the owner of this inn?

The innkeeper wrote back: Yes.

Lu Yang whipped out a silver ingot and wrote: Give us an Earth-Grade Room where no one has ever died.

The innkeeper took out three keys labeled “Earth-Grade Room Four.”

The two exchanged a glance and headed for the second floor. They noticed that there were a total of ten rooms, eight of which had black doors; only Earth-Grade Rooms Three and Four had brown doors.

Only after entering their room and sitting on the bed did they finally relax and realize that their hearts had been racing.

Lu Yang asked, “Has your family told you such things before?”

“Absolutely not! I don’t even know that a Fusion cultivator can alter reality and set rules. Those Fusion elders in my family just raise birds, tend to flowers, go fishing, and curse on the streets all the time. They don’t seem like they are this capable!”

Lu Yang agreed wholeheartedly; he also couldn’t see what was powerful about the elders of the Dao-Seeking Sect. But if someone says that Big Senior Sister has such abilities, I’ll be the first to believe it. At the very least, her impressive demeanor matches.

Light footsteps sounded, which suggested that they likely belonged to a person.

A knock came from the other side, accompanied by a gentle and servile voice, “Guests, are you asleep? The innkeeper accidentally gave you all three keys, so I can’t open the door. I have brought you freshly made dinner that is free of charge. Could you kindly open the door?”

The traveling merchants in Earth-Grade Room Three weren’t foolish; they could also sense that something was off. Abiding by the rules, they didn’t respond.

Seeing that the guests weren’t opening the door, the knocking grew louder, reverberating throughout the hallway.

“Guests, open the door! Open the door!

“I’m telling you to open the door! Do you hear me?!

“Do you think I wouldn’t bash this door down?!”

The other party dropped their pretense and banged on the door fiercely. Fortunately, the door was sturdy enough and didn’t break open.

With the merchants not falling for it, the other party shifted their tone back to a gentle one, “I’ll leave the food outside the door then.”

There was still no reply from the traveling merchants.

The other party reused the same tactic as they knocked on Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s door; they started with soft knocks before gradually increasing their force, no longer concealing their true nature.

Still, no one fell for it.

Footsteps sounded as the other party left.

“Wait, the footsteps sounded too short. It doesn’t sound like they went downstairs or upstairs. They are still on the second floor!” A chill ran down Lu Yang’s spine.

He envisioned a scene in his mind. The other party braces themselves against the wall as they hide on the ceiling, waiting for the traveling merchants to let their guard down and secretly open the door to collect their food, only to swoop down and pounce toward them...

The traveling merchants shared the same sentiments as Lu Yang; they remained cautious and had no intention of opening the door.

“Let’s sleep.” Meng Jingzhou yawned, recalling the rule that demanded them to sleep before 11pm.

He pulled a quilt from the cupboard and laid it on the floor. As he blew out the candle, the room plunged into darkness, with only the dim moonlight filtering in through the paper window.

As Meng Jingzhou looked toward the window, his heart almost stopped beating.

A dark silhouette appeared outside the window, swaying side to side as if it was clinging to the window ledge and straining its neck to peer inside.

But this is the second floor. Just how tall is this thing?!

“Check if the window is latched!” Lu Yang yelled, remembering the rule which stated that windows must not be opened!

Ever since they entered the room, they had only been focused on locking the door and completely forgot about the window. We don’t even know if the window is just closed or secured!

The two acted at lightning speed. Realizing that the window was indeed not secured, they swiftly latched it before the figure outside could knock on the window.

Making out the dark human-shaped silhouette through the window, their hearts pounded wildly.

After the narrow escape, the two made it through the first night.

Chapter 132: Danger Lurking in All Corners

By the time the two stirred awake, the first rays of dawn had already peeked through the clouds, leaving them some time until 9am.

“I was scared out of my wits yesterday!” Meng Jingzhou’s heart was still reeling as memories of the previous night flowed into his mind.

Lu Yang appeared more calm. “Let’s familiarize ourselves with the rules first. Once we grasp the rules, we won’t be scared anymore.”

Meng Jingzhou nodded.

The two corroborated the twenty-one rules with each other to ensure there were no discrepancies in their memories before they were finally relieved.

“What time is it now?”

Just then, a gong sounded outside, and the night watchman announced, “It is now 9am. The hour of the snake[1] is upon us.”

The two hurried downstairs.

On the first floor, the two traveling merchants were lashing out at the innkeeper with a saddle in hand, “We left our horse in the stable in the backyard yesterday. Why is there only a saddle left today?!”

Lu Yang recalled the colossal monster they had encountered last night. Perhaps it had eaten the horse. We didn’t hear any neighing sounds last night, which suggests that the horse didn’t even have the chance to retaliate. What a terrifying monster.

Not bothering with the traveling merchants, the two ran out of the inn.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy reminded, “These two traveling merchants carry a heavy aura of balefulness and are entangled with grievous souls. They aren’t simple merchants.”

Lu Yang nodded in acknowledgment.

Wafts of fragrant aroma drifted through the street as a restaurant opened, their freshly steamed meals arousing people’s appetites. Strangely, the restaurant was empty, with only a bamboo steamer[2] which had a sign that read “Meat Baozi.”[3]

The townsfolk of Buyi Town, who wore brown coarse hemp garments, were already accustomed to this sight. They collected their breakfast and sat down to eat, completely avoiding the meat baozi.

The two followed suit, savoring three shaobing and one bowl of soy milk.

Lu Yang noticed that the people ate very quickly, and some walked while eating, seeming very anxious.

Suddenly, a commotion could be heard from the other side of the street. A bunch of people fled, and those who had been eating abandoned their meals and ran off.

“Let’s run too!” Lu Yang grabbed a shaobing and took off.

Upon reaching the end of the street, they turned around to see what had just happened.

A group of people clad in black were approaching. There were several dozen of them, and each had sabers strapped to their waist.

“Hey, you there! Stop!” One of the people in black bellowed at someone fleeing. The person instinctively turned their head, and it spun a full three hundred sixty degrees—their neck was now drooping.

The person in black burst into laughter. He sat down at the restaurant’s entrance, lifted the lid of the bamboo steamer, and picked up a meat baozi, gobbling it up with grease dripping from his mouth.

Right then, the head of the person who died lifted and twisted itself back into place before leisurely walking away as if they had forgotten everything that just transpired.

Lu Yang analyzed, “It’s the yamen bailiffs. The rules state that we can’t eat meat baozi, yet they can. That means that the rules they need to follow are different from ours. What’s more, although there is a variety of breakfast, all the yamen bailiffs chose the meat baozi, which implies that it’s the only thing they can eat. The rules also state that we mustn’t turn our heads. It looks like it’s because turning our heads can twist our necks broken!”

Exchanging glances with each other, the two decided to leave, trying to keep a distance from the yamen bailiffs as much as possible.

“Humans at birth, they’re intrinsically kind. Similar in nature, but habits differ...”[4] As they passed by the private school, they could hear voices of people reading out loud, as if a group of adults were reciting the Three-Character Classic.

However, Lu Yang remembered one of the rules. The private school has been abandoned for many years. There is no private school teacher in town; the only sounds coming from the private school will only be of dogs barking, not students reading.

This definitely doesn’t make sense.

They scooted off but were stopped by a person clad in gray. “I haven’t seen you two before. Did you come from somewhere else?”

<Rule 9: The person wearing gray clothes is the private school teacher. If you meet the private school teacher, you must pretend that you did not hear whatever they said.>

<Rule 10: Do not make eye contact with the private school teacher; if you do, you will turn into a black dog.>

The two of them swiftly reacted; they lowered their heads and walked ahead, avoiding the private school teacher’s eyes and ignoring what he was saying.

The private school teacher was relentless, speaking alongside them, “You two are dressed very well. I assume you are cultivators? Don’t tell me you believe the rules written on the white paper? Not everything on the white paper is true. Some parts are misleading. In fact, the person who set the rules here means no malice. He just wants to protect himself and has no choice but to resort to this last tactic. Upon learning of your arrival, His Excellency specially instructed me to aid you both.

“I have a way to leave the town, but the price is that you will lose all your memories of the town. As long as you recite the Three-Character Classic in the private school for three days, you can leave the town! I’m not lying to you. Listen to the voices inside the private school. Several people have already left the town with my assistance yesterday.”

Suddenly, the private school teacher dashed in front of them and bent down to meet Lu Yang’s eyes.

Lu Yang closed his eyes in time and walked forward. Just before he squeezed his eyes shut, he noticed that the lower half of the other party’s face had no skin and was instead exposed with red muscles—a truly horrifying sight.

Seeing that the two were not paying him any attention and lowering their heads as they walked away, the private school teacher could only give up and shouted from behind them, “You only have this one chance to leave the town. You will regret not accepting my help!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke inside the mental space, “Lu Yang, don’t believe him. Only a part of what he said is true.”

“A part of it?” Lu Yang was surprised; he thought the other party was only spouting lies.

“He does have a way to let people leave the town, not in a ‘human’ form but rather as a ‘black dog.’ I saw him releasing several black dogs last night. Before he encountered the both of you, someone had made eye contact with him. That person ended up with a splitting headache and bloodshot eyes as black hair began growing on their arms. Then, they walked into the private school.”

A chill ran down Lu Yang’s spine. The private school teacher’s abilities are extremely tricky to deal with.

“Let’s go to the tailor store.” An idea had hit Lu Yang, and he needed to verify it.

The two visited all the tailor stores in Buyi Town, but none sold black, white, and gray clothes or fabric.

They also realized another problem as they wandered through the town. “Where is the ancestral hall?”

The rules state that the ancestral hall is safe, yet they also mention that there is a monster in there. Such contradictory statements definitely hint that this place is anything but simple.

Even after searching around, they still didn’t find the ancestral hall. The sky was already getting dark, and it was nearing 9pm, so they had to return to the inn.

~~~

“Welcome back, dear guests! Our inn is very safe. You don’t have to be so tense. I will protect the both of you,” the cheery waiter greeted them at the inn’s entrance. His eyes were completely black with no whites, as if he could see things beyond what ordinary people could see.

The two’s hair bristled. This is the voice that accompanied the knocking in the hallway last night!

It was him!

“Waiter, it’s not time yet. Go back to your room!” The innkeeper chased the waiter away.

The waiter stared fixedly at the innkeeper, locking eyes for a while before he left reluctantly.

Lu Yang noticed that the waiter had gone to the third floor—in other words, the Heaven-Grade Rooms.

1. I didn’t state this directly in previous chapters and converted it to contemporary time format to make it easier to understand, but ancient Chinese kept track of time in intervals of two hours, and they named each of these periods after a zodiac animal, but not with the common name. ☜

2. Zhenglong or bamboo steamer is a must as Chinese are fans of steaming. ☜

3. Baozi is ubiquitous in Chinese cuisine. They are steamed buns with various types of filling, including meat, vegetables, sweet paste, and more. The flour used to make baozi can also be different. Baozi also comes in various sizes, shapes, and colors. ☜

4. This is a very famous quote in Confucianism from the Sanzijing or Three-Character Classic where it states that human nature is inherently good. I had to tweak the translation to make it fit three words each. ☜

Chapter 133: It Is Normal for Corpses to Move

When the two returned to their room, they happened to bump into the two traveling merchants. A stark contrast to their boorish demeanor from yesterday, they were unusually friendly today, even inviting Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou into their room. As Lu Yang was unwilling to interact with them unless necessary, he declined outright.

Despite being rejected, the merchants didn’t get upset; they simply closed the door to their room.

The sound of the gong reverberated through the air, and the night watchman announced, “It is now 9pm. The hour of the pig is upon us.”

Clack, clack, clack. The rhythmic sounds of footsteps echoed again as the waiter with pitch-black eyes wandered through the corridor.

The waiter lightly knocked on the door of the room across from theirs. “Guests, are you in there? Please open the door.”

The two thought that everything would play out similarly to the night before, with the traveling merchants refusing to open the door.

Creak. The door opened.

The other traveling merchant was appalled by his companion’s actions. “Wh-what are you doing?! Why did you open the door?!

“Quick, shut the door! Hurry!

“If you want to die, don’t drag me down with you!

“Why can’t the door close?!”

Although there were supposed to be two traveling merchants, only one had spoken all this time, while the other had remained completely silent, which was very uncanny.

“Y-you, don’t come over, ah—”

Following the blood-curdling scream, nothing but stillness remained.

“What happened? The traveling merchants aren’t fools, so why would they open the door voluntarily?” A chill seeped into Meng Jingzhou’s heart.

Lu Yang mulled over it for a bit and thought of a possibility. “Do you remember the person who was killed by the authorities in the morning? He came back to life and looked no different from a living person.

“The rules state that ‘it is normal for corpses to move,’ but it doesn’t mention anything about corpses coming back to life!

“Is the person who came back to life this morning really still himself?”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes widened. “Are you saying that...one of the traveling merchants is already dead, but his companion didn’t notice at all?”

Lu Yang nodded. “Yes, exactly!”

Meng Jingzhou could feel goosebumps tingling all over him. When he saw the streets filled with people earlier today, he had thought that there weren’t many casualties. But from the looks of it now, I’m afraid that quite a number of them were living dead!

Violent knocking on the door sounded again; this time, it was Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s room.

“Help, please save me! The waiter wants to kill me!

“Open the door, please open the door!

“I beg of you, please have mercy and save me. I can give you anything, gold, spirit stones, and the locations of ancient cave ruins!

“Don’t kill me—”

Then came the muffled sound of an axe lodging itself into flesh and bones, accompanied by the agonizing screams of the traveling merchant.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged glances with each other and decided not to open the door. The room opposite had already gone silent moments ago, yet there was this sudden call for help now; everything about it screamed uncanniness. Moreover, Lu Yang had also learned from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy that the two traveling merchants weren’t good people who warranted rescuing.

The traveling merchant’s cries faded, and the waiter’s gentle knocking returned. “Dear guests, are you in there? Could you please open the door?

“Guests, are you in there? Please open the door!

“I’m telling you to open the door!

“Open this damn door for me!”

Just like the previous day, the knocking sounds grew louder until they resounded through the entire inn.

Whether it was because of the door’s superb quality or the restriction of some rules, the waiter failed to break the door down.

Lu Yang heard the waiter going upstairs, presumably returning to the Heaven-Grade Rooms directly.

No monster appeared outside the window again.

And the night passed peacefully.

~~~

When they left the inn after 9am the next day, Lu Yang noticed that the door across their room had turned from brown to black. The two traveling merchants emerged from their room, chatting and laughing together, even greeting Lu Yang with smiles.

<Rule 16: After entering a black door, do not speak and do not eat anything inside.>

Lu Yang’s gaze sharpened. These two don’t have to follow the ordinary rules anymore.

Meng Jingzhou couldn’t hold himself back from asking, “Which one of you was calling for help last night?”

The two traveling merchants were bewildered, and it didn’t look like they were faking it. “Help? Who was calling for help?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou could not figure out the situation with the traveling merchants and chose not to say anything more, leaving in a hurry.

This day, the two trailed the bailiffs from a distance and discovered that they only ate one meal a day—and it had to be meat baozi.

Meng Jingzhou secretly stole a meat baozi. Upon opening it, he found not just meat but also what appeared to be nails and hair.

After the bailiffs finished their meal, they walked through the streets and dispersed the crowd like they were chasing after ducks. Any unlucky person who accidentally turned their head immediately met with a gruesome death and then got revived.

~~~

“Have you noticed? The bailiffs roamed all across the town but never got close to the private school!”

Lu Yang spread out a map he had drawn during their stroll in town yesterday. The map marked spots like the flying carriage’s crash site, inn, private school, tailor stores, apothecaries, and the municipal office.

The map is awkwardly drawn, but the good news is that I can understand what I’ve drawn.

“It seems like the rules they follow are different; they are not one unified group!” Meng Jingzhou chuckled. This is good news. Now it’s up to us to use this information wisely.

As they walked down the street, they noticed a figure flitting through the paper window of a thatched cottage.

The rule stipulates that one must not return to the thatched cottages or inn before 7pm, so what could have been inside the thatched cottage?

“Looks like this town still has many rules we don’t know about.” Lu Yang thought, One has to abide by different rules according to their identity. The ancient Fusion cultivators must have been bored out of their minds.

“Immortal Fairy, can you see the situation outside? How is my shifu faring in the battle?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clicked her tongue in awe. “Your shifu has a profound comprehension of the Sword Dao. He’s holding his own even against four opponents.”

Lu Yang nodded, feeling reassured.

~~~

When the two returned to the inn, Lu Yang wrote on a slip of paper and handed it to the innkeeper: Are you from outside?

Meng Jingzhou watched by the side, immediately understanding what Lu Yang was trying to do. The rules state that locals can’t disclose the matters of the town to outsiders, but the innkeeper can do so, which implies that the innkeeper is not a local.

The innkeeper was surprised by Lu Yang’s question but still wrote down his answer: Yes

Lu Yang: Are you an ordinary person or a cultivator?

The innkeeper: Level Nine Qi Training Stage

Lu Yang: How did you become the innkeeper?

The innkeeper: I can’t say

Lu Yang: Are the rules you follow different from ours? What are the specific rules?

The innkeeper: I follow “Buyi Town’s Inn Rules,” but I cannot tell you the specific rules

Lu Yang: Do you want to leave?

The innkeeper’s right hand trembled slightly as he wrote: Yes

Lu Yang took out his identity jade tablet and wrote: Both of us are disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect who have accidentally entered this place, and we also wish to leave

Learning that they were disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect, the innkeeper’s hand trembled even more as he wrote: What do you need?

Lu Yang: Take off your white clothes

The innkeeper was momentarily stunned by Lu Yang’s request. The rules I follow state “As long as it is within the confines of the rules, try your best to fulfill the guests’ requests unless it contravenes moral norms.” It didn’t mention anything about taking off clothes.

Hence, the innkeeper removed his white clothes and handed them to Lu Yang, who put them away before returning to his room with Meng Jingzhou.

“Our doors have been knocked on for two days. Today shall be our turn!” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou flashed a frigid smile.

Chapter 134: The Tables Turned

It was 9pm once again, and the only guests remaining in the inn were Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

The waiter came down from the third floor, carrying an axe with blood still dripping from it. His lips curled into a smile.

Although it was an accident that he had stumbled into this town and was forced to follow its rules, these rules might very well be an opportunity for him—one to let his true nature free.

He had already lost track of how long he’d been in Buyi Town and lost count of how many people he’d killed.

These two are lucky fellows. Buyi Town is riddled with traps, yet they’ve avoided them all and survived until now. The previous batches of guests weren’t this fortunate. Unfamiliar with this place and not believing in the rules, they were soon wiped out.

Among the ten Earth-Grade Rooms, the nine doors that had turned black were evidence. And this didn’t even include the foolish ones who had ventured to the third floor to stay in the Heaven-Grade Rooms.

It’s about time that these newcomers’ luck has run out.

He decided this would be the night he’d knock on their doors until morning. Even if I can’t kill them, I have to torment them.

“Strange, the light in Earth-Grade Room Four has been on for the past two nights. Why is it dark tonight?” The waiter quickly figured out the reason and sneered. “Did you think that would make me spare you? How naive.”

He adjusted his tone as he gently knocked on the wooden door, “Guests, please open the door. Perhaps there is some misunderstanding between us.” He paused for a bit and repeated in a more steady and reassuring voice, “Guests, please open the door. Perhaps there is some misunderstanding between us.”

There was still no response.

Suddenly, a hand from out of nowhere grabbed his ankle.

“Who is it!”

He immediately looked down and saw that a dog-sized hole had somehow appeared at the bottom of the wall to Earth-Grade Room Four. A pale hand had reached out of the hole, clutching his ankle tightly.

Thud. The hand had such immense strength that it yanked him down. As the waiter crashed to the ground, his axe also flew to the side.

He desperately tried to crawl away, trying to break free, but the hand’s grip far exceeded his imagination. I can’t escape! I’ve always been the one yanking people, and now I’m the one being yanked!

I’m going to die! A ridiculous thought crossed his mind. But how can that be? I’m the hunter! The guests are the prey!

“No, this can’t be!” The waiter recalled the second rule.

<From 9pm to 9am, thatched cottages and inns with closed doors are absolutely safe; anywhere else is dangerous.>

The door to Earth-Grade Room Four is closed, so it’s an absolutely safe space for guests. If I get pulled into the room, I’ll definitely meet with a tragic end!

The waiter wretchedly clawed at the floorboards with his fingers, like a prey that was half-swallowed by a giant python, yet still attempting to escape. He screamed at the top of his lungs, “Help! Help! Save me!”

His cries were full of genuine despair.

Unfortunately for him, no one came to his rescue.

“Buyi Town’s Inn Rules” mentioned nothing about saving the waiter.

When half of his body was dragged inside, he braced himself against the walls tenaciously and exerted a final burst of strength, finally breaking free. He didn’t even bother to pick up his axe as he hurriedly limped back to the Heaven-Grade Rooms.

~~~

“He escaped?” Meng Jingzhou sighed. The waiter’s strength was astonishing; he couldn’t hold on to him even after crushing his ankle.

They had sworn to take care of the annoying waiter tonight, who had nothing better to do than to knock on their door every night. You should have gone out to inquire about us. As almighty branch leaders of the diabolic creed, when have we ever suffered such disrespect?!

After two days of observation, the two had understood the rules of the inn and swiftly designed a plan. First, Lu Yang would use his Qingfeng sword and dig a hole at the bottom of the wall according to the waiter’s stature. By making use of the rule that “rooms with closed doors are safe,” they would ensure that they could pull the waiter in without getting harmed by him; they would still hold the upper hand.

“It’s only interesting when we have an energetic prey!” Lu Yang’s lips curved into a cruel smile, his frightening voice echoing through the room.

Two dark figures walked out of Earth-Grade Room Four. One held a sword, while the other was unarmed and picked up the fallen axe. The tip of the sword scraped along the ground, emitting an irregular scratching sound, accompanied by the sound of blood dripping from the axe.

With their bloodstained weapons, two dark figures prowled the inn.

Nothing on the second floor...That means it has to be on the third floor.

There were a total of four rooms on the third floor, all of which were Heaven-Grade Rooms.

The dark figure wielding the sword knocked on the door and spoke gently, “We heard there’s free dinner here. We are hungry and would like to eat. Please open the door.”

Hearing no response from Heaven-Grade Room One, Lu Yang grew impatient and banged the door. “Open the door! We want to eat! What kind of service is this?

“There’s some misunderstanding between us. Open the door, and we can have a nice chat!

“Open the door! Open the door now! If you don’t, I’ll be bashing it down!”

The deafening knocks reverberated throughout the entire inn.

Lu Yang kicked open the door of Heaven-Grade Room One, but there was no one inside. He wanted to go in, but a force barred his way.

<Rule 5: You cannot enter the Heaven-Grade Rooms.>

The waiter was hiding inside one of the rooms, and he trembled as he heard the commotion. “Don’t...don’t be afraid. The rules say that they cannot enter Heaven-Grade Rooms. They can’t come in...they can’t come in...” He mumbled to himself over and over again, but that did nothing to quell the uneasiness in his heart.

Lu Yang had already kicked open the doors to Heaven-Grade Rooms Two and Three, but he still found no trace of the waiter.

“It has to be Heaven-Grade Room Four then!”

Without hesitation, he kicked the door open. In the darkness, he saw the waiter huddled up into a ball.

“Come out! I’ll spare your life!” Meng Jingzhou threatened menacingly.

Discerning Meng Jingzhou’s bluff, the waiter relaxed and laughed out loud. “Haha, I knew it, you also have to abide by the rules!” Only I can decide who enters the Heaven-Grade Rooms. Besides, I also hold an absolute advantage inside these rooms. No one can harm me!

Just as the waiter contemplated whether he should pull the two of them in, Lu Yang unhurriedly pulled out a wooden plaque from behind him. As soon as the waiter laid his eyes on it, his expression became one of sheer horror.

The wooden plaque read: Earth-Grade Room Four

Lu Yang had anticipated that such a scenario might occur, so he tried swapping the door plaque of Earth-Grade Room Three with that of Earth-Grade Room Four, and Room Three’s black door turned brown, proving that it had become “Earth-Grade Room Four.”

His method did work.

Switching the door plaque of Heaven-Grade Room Four to that of Earth-Grade Room Four, the barrier vanished, and they were now free to enter.

One held a sword, and one carried an axe, their lips twisted into terrifying smiles.

Under the waiter’s horrified gaze, the two stepped inside the room and considerately closed the door.

Now, this was Earth-Grade Room Four—an absolutely safe place for them.

Lu Yang sent the waiter sprawling with a kick and severed the tendons of his limbs to prevent him from escaping; Meng Jingzhou gave him two resounding slaps as payback for frightening them. Then, they made him change into the white clothes.

“Tell us everything you know!”

<Rule 17: Do not easily trust the words of strangers, but everything said by someone clad in white clothes is true.>

Chapter 135: Apothecary

“How many dangerous people are there in the inn?” Lu Yang had to verify whether the waiter was the only source of danger in the inn.

Trembling in his white clothes, the waiter held up two fingers. “T-two.”

“Who?!”

“You two.”

Meng Jingzhou kicked him. “Be honest!”

The waiter felt helpless; he couldn’t lie while wearing white clothes. You two are clearly the most dangerous in the inn.

Lu Yang adjusted his question. “How many dangerous people are there in the inn for ordinary people?”

“I’m the only one,” the waiter answered truthfully.

“Between you and the innkeeper, who’s stronger?”

“I’m stronger, but the rules we follow are different. He has a natural suppression over me.”

Lu Yang checked, “Is your power in Heaven-Grade Rooms the same elsewhere?”

“No, it is different. Based on the rules, my power is stronger in Heaven-Grade Rooms.”

“Are there others like you who have different powers in different places?”

“Yes, for example, the things in the thatched cottages in the day. They are very strong in the thatched cottages and can move freely between them, but once they leave the thatched cottages, their power will be reduced to that of ordinary people, and they will lose their ability to traverse the thatched cottages. However, I don’t know exactly what those things are.”

“Are there more? What about the bailiffs in black clothes and the private school teacher in gray clothes? Do they have enhanced powers?”

“No, but they were originally cultivators, so they are much stronger than ordinary people.”

“What’s the relationship between the bailiffs and private school teacher like?”

The waiter theorized, “My speculation is that they don’t have a good relationship, and there may even be competition between them. For instance, the bailiffs and I have the same criterion of needing to kill a certain number of people to leave the town. I’m not sure about the private school teacher, but the requirement is probably similar.”

“Do you know where the town mayor is?”

“I heard that he is in the municipal office, but I’ve never seen him come out.”

“How do we kill the town mayor?”

“I don’t know.”

“What are the town mayor’s powers and abilities?”

“I don’t know.”

“Where is the ancestral hall?”

“You can’t find the ancestral hall in the day. It only appears between 9 - 11pm.” The waiter was obedient in replying to all their questions.

The answers largely matched what Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had already deduced.

Finished with their questions, Lu Yang deftly removed the white clothes from the waiter and drove a sword through him.

As branch leaders of a diabolic creed, we naturally understand that dead men tell no tales.

“Good thing you removed the white clothes beforehand; otherwise, they would have been stained.” Meng Jingzhou stretched lazily. “We can finally get our beauty sleep.”

Lu Yang felt the same way. We have quite the harvest today, and there’ll be no more annoying knocking at the door.

The two searched the waiter’s body and found the rules of the inn, but it was of no use since they already had it figured out.

“Our rules disappeared right after we read it once. If not for our good memory, we would’ve forgotten them by now. But the waiter can keep his rules intact to ensure that they remember them correctly. Looks like the treatment the waiter and others get is entirely different from ours.”

~~~

At 9am on the third day, the night watchman’s gong woke the two of them. Despite yawning, they were satisfied with their sleep.

The innkeeper had heard the waiter’s cries for help and various noises last night, so he decided to check on the waiter in the morning. When he saw the gruesome state of the waiter’s body, he fell silent for a long while.

Are these two really from the righteous path?

Before leaving the inn, Lu Yang wrote a note for the innkeeper: The white clothes worked pretty well. We’ll borrow it for another two days.

What Lu Yang didn’t notice was the trace of fear in the innkeeper’s eyes as he looked at them. Also, why does the tone of this note feel so similar to those domineering diabolic cultivators who don’t pay back their debts? It seems to be saying, “This stuff is not bad. Lend it to me. I’ll return it when I’m bored of it.”

“It’s just an illusion, right?” Clearly, the innkeeper hardly knew anything about the Dao-Seeking Sect.

For low-level cultivators like them, most of their knowledge about massive organizations like the Dao-Seeking Sect stemmed from rumors.

And rumors were often unreliable.

~~~

After the two left the inn, they arrived at the apothecary where an apprentice dressed in gray greeted them enthusiastically, “What can I help you with, guests? Did you hear dogs barking? Or did you encounter black dogs? If you heard dogs barking, I have ready-made medicine for you.”

The apothecary apprentice presented a bubbling pot of red medicinal liquid. “This is made from Cinnabar Grass that has been ground into powder and simmered for ten hours. Drinking this will temporarily make you drowsy, but after a good sleep, the effects from the dogs' barking will vanish.
