“If you have encountered black dogs, you should quickly follow me; otherwise, you’ll soon be converted by the black dogs. There’s a well in the backyard of the apothecary. As long as you drink the water you drew by yourself, you won’t be converted by the black dogs.”

Meng Jingzhou was about to say that he wanted to see the owner, but Lu Yang stopped him. Meng Jingzhou immediately understood the reason. There’s no need to explain to the apothecary apprentice. He is considered a stranger, which means that what he says is likely false.

The two sat there, completely unperturbed and silent, regardless of how anxious and concerned the apothecary apprentice appeared.

Roughly an hour later, the apothecary apprentice walked into the backyard, and only then did the apothecary owner appear. He was an elderly man dressed in white clothes. His benevolent countenance easily invited one to trust him and confide in him about their troubles. “Did the two of you encounter any difficulties, or do you have any questions?”

The two remembered the rules stating that they couldn’t speak to the apothecary owner, so Lu Yang handed a slip of paper to him: We heard dogs barking. What should we do about it?

“You need two qian[1] of Percipient Grass. Crush it with saliva and block your ears with the residue for a quarter of an hour to remove the effects.”

Lu Yang wrote: Give us 4 qian of Percipient Grass. Also, what if we encounter black dogs?

“That would be troublesome. Anyone who encounters a black dog would involuntarily bark, and as soon as they bark out loud, they’ll be converted by the black dog. There is a solution though—sew your mouth shut with a needle and thread. If you can keep it up for an hour without making any sound, you won’t be converted by the black dogs.”

Lu Yang listened with rapt attention and wrote: How do we leave the town?

“Leave the town? That’s even more troublesome. I even think it’s impossible. There’s an ancestral hall in the town. It houses a half-naked statue of a blindfolded Buddha. If you take the Buddha statue out of the ancestral hall and smash it, a passageway to the outside world will appear. However, beware that the exit is fraught with bone-tormenting gales that enter all seven orifices and exit through them. Through this process, your body will dissolve and your spirit disintegrate, leaving only a pile of bones behind. No one can resist it.

“This is the only way to leave the town.”

Their hearts sank. It’s clear that these rules are designed to prevent people from leaving. That does make sense. The ancient Fusion cultivators hiding here definitely wouldn’t allow anything to leak out.

1. One of the measurement units used in Traditional Chinese Medicine; one qian is approximately 3.78g. ☜

Chapter 136: There’s No Way To Get Through This?

The apothecary owner slowly continued, “This place is a result of rules set by several Fusion cultivators. However, arrays have a Life Gate and a Death Gate, for the heavenly law always leaves a sliver of hope. As such, the rules formulated here must encompass a path to survival.

“That said, those Fusion cultivators wouldn’t be willing to let anyone leave, so they created this specious rule, aligning with their interests while adhering to the heavenly law’s principle to leave a glimmer of hope.”

Lu Yang resisted the impulse to cuss and continued writing: Then how do we kill the town mayor?

The apothecary owner replied: You can’t kill him. The town mayor is undying. How would you even kill him?

Meng Jingzhou clenched his fists; in his heart, he was cursing the bunch of Fusion cultivators who set those rules. You might as well not stipulate twenty-one rules. There’s no difference anyway!

Lu Yang’s expression was also grim, but he kept his cool, knowing that swearing wouldn’t solve the problem. He continued to write: Where is the town mayor?

The apothecary owner chuckled. “Are you seriously thinking of killing the town mayor? Unfortunately, I don’t know where he is. But you can ask the bailiffs. After all, they’re the closest to him. As for whether they’d tell you anything, that’s out of my hands.”

As they were leaving, the apothecary owner called out, “Since you truly seem bent on leaving this place, I’ll give you a warning. The town mayor knows everything that happens in his town. This is his ability. Be careful, you two.”

Meng Jingzhou was about to politely thank him when he remembered that they mustn’t speak to the apothecary owner, so he could only nod his head in acknowledgment.

Lu Yang remained unmoved throughout.

Meng Jingzhou whispered, “Do you think everything the apothecary owner said was true?”

Lu Yang didn’t reply right away. Only after they were a distance from the apothecary did he sneer. “Under the restrictions of the rules, what he said is naturally true, but that doesn’t necessarily mean that he’s on our side.

“Do you know the biggest difference between him and the innkeeper?”

“What?”

“The apothecary owner kept trying to make us talk.”

Meng Jingzhou was startled, and realization dawned upon him. With the innkeeper, both parties communicated through writing, but with the apothecary owner, he would reply to them verbally despite them writing the entire time.

If one party kept speaking, the other party could easily slip up and respond verbally.

“Wily old fox.” Meng Jingzhou cussed under his breath. He paused for a bit, feeling that things didn’t add up. “Hold on, if he was trying to harm us, why did he still remind us that the town mayor knows everything that happens in town?”

Lu Yang answered without hesitation, “He saw that he couldn’t stop us from trying our best to leave, so he gave us another crucial piece of information to let us know that the town mayor is undefeatable.

“This would lead to two likely outcomes. Either we give up on leaving or fall apart by ourselves before the battle even begins.”

Meng Jingzhou clicked his tongue, finding that the situation had become even more tricky. “The biggest problem now is that the town mayor knows everything we’re up to. Even if we figure out how to leave, he can still stop us!”

How can we escape right under the town mayor’s nose?

Lu Yang pondered for a moment when suddenly, an idea struck him. He took out some paper and pen, writing: Let’s communicate in writing. It might reduce the town mayor’s attention on us.

Meng Jingzhou nodded.

Lu Yang: Do you still remember the jade pendant the sect distributed to us? Every jade pendant is a symbol of our identity. As soon as the jade pendant breaks, the sect will automatically send someone over to investigate. The jade pendants are too hard for us to shatter, but we can throw them to the exit, where the gales will crush them.

A spark twinkled in Meng Jingzhou’s eyes as he did some calculations. This really seems like a good idea.

Meng Jingzhou: But how do we deal with the town mayor?

Lu Yang: We need to figure out the town mayor’s modus operandi. Let’s start with the yamen bailiffs.

Writing and drawing on the paper, the two sketched out a detailed plan, then burned it to a crisp, acting as if nothing had happened.

As the two continued walking, they found themselves in the vicinity of the private school. As usual, they could hear the sound of people reading aloud. However, according to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it was actually the sound of barking dogs altered by the rules. If someone couldn’t suppress their curiosity and entered the private school, the sound of reading would turn into barking, and something terrible would happen.

The private school teacher approached Lu Yang, once again persuading him to enter the private school, but Lu Yang kept his head lowered and turned a deaf ear to him.

He had the gift of the gab, rambling on, “Friend, we meet again. You came alone this time. It looks like you had a falling out with your companion, which means that you still believe me deep down. Don’t trust what the rules say. Nine out of ten are false. You won’t be able to distinguish them...”

Just as the private school teacher wanted to launch a surprise attack on Lu Yang by bending down to look him in the eye, everything suddenly went black before his eyes.

The clueless private school teacher had been so focused on Lu Yang that he didn’t notice Meng Jingzhou sneaking up on him from behind and throwing a burlap sack over him.

The two rubbed their hands. They had suffered quite the scare from the private school teacher previously, but this time, they weren’t afraid of meeting his eyes. We must take revenge!

Those from diabolic creeds were emotionally driven people who would always repay a grudge—a trait that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exemplified.

“Beat him!”

The two lashed out with their fists and kicks, showing no mercy to the private school teacher, who had never experienced anything like this before. He howled in anguish, “Stop hitting me, please stop!”

<Rule 9: The person wearing gray clothes is the private school teacher. If you meet the private school teacher, you must pretend that you did not hear whatever they said.>

Both of us are benevolent and soft-hearted people. We will stop beating the other party if they beg for mercy. Unfortunately, we are bound by the rules and must pretend that we didn’t hear anything the private school teacher said.

We have no choice but to keep hitting him.

Finally, the two let out a long sigh of relief, feeling satisfied after venting out on the private school teacher. Before leaving, Meng Jingzhou even spat phlegm. “Ptui! Scum! Don’t let me see you again.”

Arms around each other’s shoulders, they headed back to the inn.

After the private school teacher struggled free from the sack, he glowered fiercely at the two departing figures in the distance. “Don’t let me see you again!”

~~~

When it was 9am on the fourth day, the two went to the restaurant downstairs—the only place in town that sold meat baozi.

<Rule 11: All food in the town is provided free of charge, and you can help yourself to it, but never eat meat baozi.>

Since the meat baozi were free, they decided that they could swipe them away even if they couldn’t eat them, so they packed up all of the meat baozi with the same sack they had put over the private school teacher yesterday.

When the yamen bailiffs in black clothes arrived at the restaurant as usual, they discovered that all the meat baozi were gone.

“Who did this?!” they shouted in rage.

According to the “Buyi Town’s Yamen Bailiff Rules,” we can only eat meat baozi every day. Now that there’s none left, what are we going to eat?!

“Boss, look at those two people. Are they carrying our meat baozi on their back?” A yamen bailiff with a keen sense of smell pointed out.

Noticing the yamen bailiff’s gazes shifting to them, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were aware that they were exposed and immediately fled.

The bailiffs were originally only suspicious, but they were now certain. “It’s definitely them! After them!”

The civilians of Buyi Town realized that the usually quiet town was unusually noisy today.

“Stop, you two bastards!”

Lu Yang yelled back as he ran, “That won’t do! Rule 12 states that if we encounter people from the authorities, we have to run immediately. I’m just following the rules. Don’t make things hard on us.”

The chief yamen bailiff was fuming. “But those damn rules didn’t tell you to take away our meat baozi!”

With Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou moving at lightning speed, the yamen bailiffs couldn’t catch up with them at all.

Chapter 137: Toying with the Yamen Bailiffs

According to research by the Pill Cauldron Peak, long-term consumption of meat baozi could lead to nutritional imbalances and impaired physical development. In order to improve the diet of the yamen bailiffs, the kind Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou decided that they had to do something for them.

In the morning, the diligent Shifu Lu and Shifu Meng decided to pack up all the meat baozi, which would force the bailiffs to consume vegetarian meals for nutritional balance while also encouraging them to exercise more, run frequently, and stay active.

The yamen bailiffs gladly accepted the two experts’ advice and expressed their resolve to follow the experts’ guidance and catch up with them as soon as possible to thank them in person.

These two experts were not all just talk. To prove the feasibility of their health theories, they set an example by personally taking the field to run.

The yamen bailiffs were extremely moved and also began to run and work out, persisting through the entire morning. They were in fervent agreement with the experts’ suggestions, helping to promote the two experts for free. Before long, the whole town could hear the yamen bailiffs hollering.

“Stop right there!”

“You two bastards, I guarantee I won’t beat you to death!”

“Why are you taking the meat baozi if you’re not eating them?”

The yamen bailiffs were livid, doggedly pursuing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, who didn’t dare let the yamen bailiffs catch up with them. They instantly took to their heels, leaving the bailiffs behind them in a cloud of dust.

As they ran, Lu Yang remarked, “The rules really don’t lie! Look at how dangerous these yamen bailiffs are. They’re hot on our trail despite us not doing anything. We mustn’t let them catch us.”

Meng Jingzhou agreed wholeheartedly. “Exactly! Luckily, both of us are at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Had it been someone else, they would have been caught by now.”

The yamen bailiffs planned to take a shortcut to block them, but the two had long familiarized themselves with the town’s layout and evaded pursuit easily.

Just like that, the two led the yamen bailiffs on a chase from morning to night. When night fell, the bailiffs were panting heavily and light on their feet, clearly struggling to keep running.

As 9pm approached, the two returned to the inn, still carrying the meat baozi. The yamen bailiffs could only glower at them fiercely and reluctantly head back to the municipal office. According to the “Buyi Town’s Yamen Bailiff Rules,” they needed to stay in the municipal office between 9pm to 9am.

As for the other two, they found it a bit regretful. We’ve done many preparations in the inn. If only the yamen bailiffs entered the inn, we could have given them a surprise.

What a pity.

~~~

On the fifth day at 9am, the usually lazy yamen bailiffs arrived promptly at the restaurant. In the past, they would arrive a quarter of an hour late, waiting for the crowd to gather before suddenly appearing to scare the people. If they were lucky, they could even snap a few necks broken.

This time, for the sake of the meat baozi, they changed their habits.

After running for the whole of yesterday without eating a single meat baozi, their stomachs were already rumbling with hunger, so they rushed over. We gotta quickly eat as much as we can before those two immoral rascals mess around.

Halfway through their meal, they saw Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou coming out of the inn leisurely.

“How dare you still show your faces in front of us!” Recalling the events of the previous day, the yamen bailiffs were incensed, vowing to capture the two.

Lu Yang said unhurriedly, “I advise you not to chase us, else something terrible will happen.”

“Who are you trying to scare!” The leader of the bailiffs evidently didn’t believe Lu Yang. There are only twenty-one rules in Buyi Town. None of what he says will happen.

“Get them!”

Seeing their warning fall on deaf ears, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou sighed and turned to run.

After running for a bit, one of the bailiffs suddenly clutched his belly and rolled on the ground, his forehead breaking out in sweat. “My stomach hurts so much!”

As if it was a chain reaction, one by one, they doubled over in pain. Even the bailiff leader couldn’t endure it anymore and curled up on the ground, completely unable to stand.

“The meat baozi are poisoned...” The bailiff leader stared fixedly at Lu Yang, convinced that they were the culprits.

Lu Yang strolled over in a relaxed manner, “I’ve already told you not to chase us, but you wouldn’t listen. Look at how unlucky you are now!”

“How did you get the poison?!” The bailiff leader couldn’t figure it out. The apothecary owner couldn’t possibly have provided poison to this guy, so where on earth did he get it?

Lu Yang squatted down and patted the bailiff leader’s head, speaking amiably, “Remember, you shouldn’t engage in vigorous exercise after a meal; otherwise, it’s easy to get appendicitis. Read more books. Don’t think that everything is poison. We are from a righteous sect. How could we use poison?”

As one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Dao-Seeking Sect has always been upright in conduct and would never resort to something despicable like poisoning. At the very least, none of the living enemies have encountered the Dao-Seeking Sect using poison.

While some of the bailiffs writhed in pain on the ground, those who were fine stood fearfully, afraid to take action against Lu Yang. And thus, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou openly disappeared from the bailiffs’ sight.

What the two didn’t notice was the fear glimmering in the townsfolk's eyes as they watched from the side of the road. “It's fortunate that these two are following ordinary rules. If they were to wear black clothes and become yamen bailiffs, would we even have a chance to survive?”

“You can say that again. They even claim that they are from a righteous sect, but I suspect that they are diabolic spies who have infiltrated the righteous path!”

Nonetheless, the civilians of Buyi Town were relieved that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were on their side; otherwise, they feared that they wouldn’t live past three days.

~~~

On the sixth day, the yamen bailiffs had learned their lesson. They grabbed the meat baozi first but didn’t eat them, blocking the entrance of the inn instead.

Having anticipated this, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou escaped through the window from the second floor.

“Chase them! Don’t let them escape!” The resentment built up over the last two days had reached a terrifying peak. Remembering their pain from yesterday, they wished they could tear the two into pieces.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had become more skilled in running from all the practice, and the yamen bailiffs didn’t notice that in their pursuit, they had arrived at the private school.

When the private school teacher saw Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, he gritted his teeth and beckoned to the people studying inside.

Perhaps these people could no longer be called “people.” They were covered in black hair from head to toe and had elongated mouths, while those in a more severe state lay flat on the ground, just one step away from becoming a black dog.

“Catch them!” the private school teacher ordered.

This enraged the yamen bailiffs. How dare you snatch our people!

The private school teacher also intended to look Lu Yang in the eyes, but the latter was prepared, whipping out a bronze mirror to shield his face. “You should look at your ugly appearance instead!”

In the mirror, the private school teacher saw his skinless face and bright red eyes, and he let loose a wail of anguish. Realizing that something was happening to his body, he hastily returned to the school and sealed his mouth shut.

Even without the private school teacher’s command, the black dogs continued to embroil themselves in a battle with the yamen bailiffs.

Amidst the chaos, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou pulled one of the bailiffs away and attempted to strip him of his clothes but found that it was impossible to get them off. As such, they could only settle for searching the bailiff for the “Buyi Town’s Yamen Bailiff Rules.”

Just like the waiter, the yamen bailiffs always carried the rules with them, lest they forget. With their desired item acquired, the two absconded.

As for the yamen bailiffs, the two decided to respect their wishes. Let them fight if they want to.

Chapter 138: Everyone is Scheming

Outside Buyi Town, five Fusion experts were engaged in an all-out battle that had been going on for five days.

Four ancient Fusion cultivators controlled their territories to prevent the brunt of the battle from getting out, while the Taciturn Daoist Priest expanded his territory, launching fierce attacks.

Damn it, why do we have to face the most troublesome sword cultivator!” One of the Fusion cultivators furrowed their brow. Throughout the ages, sword cultivators have always been the pinnacle of offensive power, yet the first Fusion cultivator we face just has to be a sword cultivator. What terribly bad luck we have.

The four included Advanced Fusion cultivators and Apex Fusion cultivators, an undeniably formidable lineup. Coupled with their seamless teamwork, they were unbeatable among Fusion cultivators, all until they were up against the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Not only did they not gain any upper hand, but any slip-up could even be lethal.

Although this was partly due to them allocating part of their power to maintain the rules of Buyi Town and not yet being in a fully awakened state, the fact that the Taciturn Daoist Priest could still pose such a challenge was evidence of how terrifying he was.

“Even if it was in our era, Fusion Sword cultivators didn’t possess this level of skill!” Another Fusion cultivator spat out a mouthful of blood, his aura fluctuating. He was accidentally pierced by a sword earlier and needed to focus on healing his injuries.

“Fortunately, there’s four of us and only one of him. A prolonged battle favors us. If we can hold out for another ten days, I bet he won’t be as vigorous as he is now!”

“Nothing should happen in Buyi Town, right? If someone exploits the rules and finds a reasonable way to leave the Buyi Town, we will suffer a backlash.”

Clearly, the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s ability to break the rules of Buyi Town with sword qi wasn’t within the boundary of what was considered “reasonable.”

“What’s there to fear! Old Five is the town mayor, though he technically took over the body. Even then, he isn’t someone those two little brats can deal with.”

“True.” Reassured by Old Five’s presence in Buyi Town, the four began a prolonged battle with the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Hearing their conversation, the Taciturn Daoist Priest grew slightly concerned about Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. I told them to stay put in Buyi Town. They should be obedient, right?

Believing that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were good children who listened to him, he could afford to begin the prolonged battle against the four. Little Yun will definitely be worried about me bringing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou along. Once enough time has passed, she’ll surely come looking for me.

“One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!” the Taciturn Daoist Priest roared as if he was ready to exert all his power for a swift resolution to the battle, frightening the four.

The technique of One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords was already renowned in ancient times, so they were naturally aware of it. They watched as the Taciturn Daoist Priest raised his sword high up, golden sword qi radiating as dazzlingly as the sun. With a flick of his sword, ten thousand swords appeared, all solid and indistinguishable from one another.

One could only imagine the calamitous might of those ten thousand swords once they descended.

“Be careful! He’s going all in!” one of the four warned.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest switched his sword move again. “Person and Sword as One!” His body completely disappeared as it merged with the sword.

With no fewer than ten thousand swords present, the four couldn’t find the sword the Taciturn Daoist Priest had merged with, so frustrated that they wanted to vomit blood. We’ve never heard of such a stalling tactic!

“And you have the face to call yourself a sword cultivator!”

~~~

*

Buyi Town’s Yamen Bailiff Rules

Rule 1: Those dressed in black are from the authorities. Once the black clothes are worn, they cannot be taken off.

Rule 2: You can call out to anyone as you wish, and the person you called out to will have their neck twisted and broken.

Rule 3: There are only 50 yamen bailiffs and one town mayor in the municipal office. If you see anyone else, please ignore them.

Rule 4: From 9pm to 9am, you must stay within the municipal office.

Rule 5: You only have meat baozi as sustenance. If you don’t eat for three days, you will die.

Rule 6: The town mayor only has one head and two arms.

Rule 7: If you feel dizzy or see black hair growing on your arms and do not return to normal within two hours, you may ignore Rule 4 and immediately head to the ancestral hall.

Rule 8: You will not see the town mayor between 9pm to 9am. If you do, firmly believe that this is an illusion.

Rule 9: If a hundred people’s necks are broken because of you, you can choose whether you want to leave Buyi Town. If you leave Buyi Town, you will lose all your memories of it.

Rule 10: Under the premise that you do not violate the aforementioned rules, you must obey the town mayor’s orders.

Rule 11: In the center of the town stands a three-hundred-year-old locust tree. Between 9pm to 9am, the locust tree will turn into the ancestral hall.

*

“Finally, we know the location of the ancestral hall.” Meng Jingzhou grinned. Initially, the two had planned to cause some additional chaos to uncover the location. But things are much easier now. What a pleasant surprise.

Lu Yang’s attention was on another matter. After all, they had gone to great lengths to obtain the “Buyi Town’s Yamen Bailiff Rules” to learn the town mayor’s whereabouts. “This is a bit tricky. The rules state that ‘From 9pm to 9am, you must stay within the municipal office’ and ‘You will not see the town mayor between 9pm to 9am. If you do, firmly believe that this is an illusion.’ This suggests that the town mayor is not in the municipal office during the hours between 9pm to 9am.”

Without knowing the town mayor’s location, this meant that they could likely bump into him when heading to the ancestral hall.

“We shouldn’t confront the town mayor lightly. He probably doesn’t only have one ability, and we have no clue how powerful he is. We need to avoid him as much as possible.”

Suddenly, Lu Yang seemed to have discovered something. “Have you noticed? Between 9pm to 9am, the town mayor is not in the municipal office, and during this time, the thatched cottages and inn are safe, which leaves the streets as the only dangerous place!

“And what is on the streets? Only the monster! It’s highly plausible that the town mayor is a monster!”

Meng Jingzhou knitted his brows. “But look, the rules also state that ‘The town mayor only has one head and two arms.’ Do monsters really fit this description?”

Lu Yang nodded. “Do you still remember the dark figure we saw outside the window on our first night? It was two stories tall, and its upper body looked human. This doesn’t contradict the rules.

“The rules mention nothing about what the lower body looks like!”

Meng Jingzhou swiftly came to a decision. “We won’t return to the inn when it’s 9pm. Instead, we’ll stand beside the locust tree. Once it transforms into the ancestral hall, we’ll charge right in, smash the Buddha statue, and throw the jade pendants. Then, we’ll split up and quickly return to the inn.”

By splitting up, even if one of them encountered the monster, the other person would remain safe, ensuring that at least one of them could make it back safely.

“The monster may not even dare to eat us, for our lives are connected to our soul lamps. As soon as we die, our soul lamps will extinguish, people from our sect will barge in, and only death awaits these Fusion cultivators!” Although Lu Yang appeared to be talking to Meng Jingzhou, his words were actually meant for the all-knowing town mayor.

~~~

The two arrived at the locust tree in the center of the town, and time passed, second by second.

“The hour of the pig...” The night watchman shouted as he rang the gong.

The space where the locust tree gradually became warped and turned into a wooden ancestral hall with the words “Buyi Town’s Ancestral Hall Rules” written outside.

On tenterhooks, the two instinctively reached for the jade pendants at their waist. That was when their expressions changed drastically.

“The jade pendant has vanished!” the two shouted simultaneously.

Just then, a heavy and muffled voice echoed from within the ancestral hall. “Tee hee! Two naive children who overestimate themselves. If you could find the paper with the ‘Buyi Town’s Yamen Bailiff Rules’ amidst the chaos, couldn’t I order the yamen bailiffs to steal your jade pendants amidst the chaos?”

<Rule 10 of the Buyi Town’s Yamen Bailiff Rules: Under the premise that you do not violate the aforementioned rules, you must obey the town mayor’s orders.>

Chapter 139: Who is the Real Hunter?

“Damn it, things are really not that simple!” Lu Yang frowned. With the town mayor, or should I say, the monster in the ancestral hall, the danger level has just escalated.

“What do we do?” Meng Jingzhou’s expression was equally grim as his mind raced to find a solution.

Lu Yang caught a glimpse of the rules pasted at the entrance of the ancestral hall.

*

Buyi Town’s Ancestral Hall Rules

Rule 1: If you are wearing black or white clothes, and you feel dizzy or see black hair growing on your arms, please enter the ancestral hall, worship the Buddha statue, and drink the water before the Buddha statue.

Rule 2: The Buddha statue will not get damaged within the ancestral hall.

Rule 3: There is a man-eating monster inside the ancestral hall.

Rule 4: The ancestral hall is safe.

*

“Let’s get inside the ancestral hall!” Lu Yang decisively entered the ancestral hall. Although Rule 3 and Rule 4 seem contradictory, that's not actually the case.

Based on Lu Yang’s familiarity with the rules over the past few days, he had concluded that the rules were always true. That means there must be a logically consistent explanation for these two rules—it’s true that there is a man-eating monster inside the ancestral hall, but the man-eating monster can’t eat people in there!

That’s why entering the ancestral hall is the safest option!

The two dashed inside and finally lay their eyes on the town mayor—a monster they had never seen before.

The town mayor was half-human and half-beast, with a height that reached two stories. His upper body was not much different from a human’s, except for an additional eye between his eyebrows and a mouth that split to his earlobes, resembling a python. His lower body looked like a tall steed but also had eight human legs. Lu Yang noticed a thick tail behind the town mayor lightly resting on the ground and stirring up dust. However, the light in the ancestral hall was too dim for him to discern what kind of demon’s tail it was.

There were no ancestral tablets in the ancestral hall. In the center was a half-naked Buddha statue that was blindfolded, appearing bewitching and uncanny. Three bowls of clear water were placed in front of the Buddha statue, presumably the water that could undo the transformation into a black dog, as stated in “Rule 1 of the Ancestral Hall Rules.”

The town mayor lowered his head, not expecting to see the two visitors. “As I thought, the two of you are certainly something else, reacting so quickly. Looks like it was the right decision for me to deal with you personally.”

“Thank you for coming personally, town mayor, but why don’t you go back!” As usual, Meng Jingzhou couldn’t hold his tongue.

The town mayor said nothing more. When the flying carriage crashed, he had already noticed Lu Yang and his companions. Since the Taciturn Daoist Priest, who had the highest cultivation, had left the town, and Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were merely juniors with low cultivation, the town mayor paid no attention to them.

Later, the town mayor noticed that they had made use of the rules to eliminate the waiter. Only then did he begin to take them seriously, recognizing that they seemed to be adept at manipulating the rules and could be a potential threat.

He wanted to get rid of the two but was aware that they wouldn’t be easily hoodwinked, so he chose to play along and beat them at their own game. Cognizant of everything happening in Buyi Town, the two’s attempt to write their escape plan on paper couldn’t escape his three eyes.

Such geniuses share the same flaw. They are all too full of themselves, believing that no one can outwit their schemes. The town mayor exploited this mindset of theirs and gave them the freedom to devise a method of escape and toy with the yamen bailiffs, only to have their jade pendants stolen away at the last moment. With their plans foiled, he would then finish them off in the ancestral hall.

However, the two were very cautious and never left the inn at night, so the town mayor purposely revealed a flaw to lure them out of their den.

Now, it’s time to pull in the net!

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were aghast. As clever people, they instantly realized that this was all part of the town mayor’s elaborate scheme.

We were too careless!

Without hesitation, the town mayor’s tail struck out as swiftly as lightning. Before Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou could react, they were sent flying into a wall.

Fortunately, due to the rule that “The ancestral hall is safe,” the two were not injured; otherwise, they could have died on the spot!

Their hearts sank. The chasm between their strength and speed was too overwhelming to overcome, not to mention that the town mayor was undying. However, even if the town mayor could really die, they had no means to harm him.

The town mayor knew that he couldn’t kill the two within the ancestral hall. So I just have to push them out! I’m unbeatable outside the ancestral hall!

The gigantic town mayor charged toward the two. Sensing the danger, they tacitly struck each other’s palms to propel themselves away. As they rolled away, they evaded the town mayor’s onslaught.

“You’ve got some skill, I’ll give you that,” the town mayor sneered dismissively. But this kind of petty trick can only be used on me once.

“Go around to the back!” Lu Yang hollered. The town mayor’s enormous size will make it difficult for him to turn in the cramped ancestral hall.

By the time the town mayor turned around, he saw Meng Jingzhou lift the Buddha statue and hurl it at him.

<Within the ancestral hall, the Buddha statue will not get damaged.>

The indestructible Buddha statue is the best weapon!

“Is that all?” The town mayor remained unfazed by the massive Buddha statue carved from stone.

He threw a punch at them, breaking the sound barrier and stirring up a whirlwind in the tight space that was the ancestral hall.

As the fifth of the Fusion cultivators, he had chosen to become the town mayor not for fun. During his slumber, his body suffered complications that amounted to corporeal death. After awakening, he was only left with his soul. To vie for fortuitous opportunities in the Great Era, he took over the town mayor’s body and used ancient cultivation techniques to modify the body into its current form. Despite its hideous and odd appearance, power was of utmost importance for a cultivator. I’m the strongest in this form, and I’ll definitely stand out in the Great Era!

Unable to withstand the punch, Lu Yang was blasted away. He deftly performed a normal Tiger Fist to mimic a tiger, adjusting his body to land lightly in the nick of time and dissipating most of the force. Meng Jingzhou clung to the Buddha statue tightly and ended up flying out of the ancestral hall with it.

“Don’t let the Buddha statue hit the ground! You’ll die if it breaks!” Lu Yang shouted.

Meng Jingzhou also realized the peril he was in. What I’m carrying is not a hope of escape to the outside world but a magical treasure that is a ticking time bomb! With a bellow, his muscles bulged, his skin reddened, and his veins popped. Stomping the ground with his feet and putting all the force into his arms, he anchored both his body and the Buddha statue, preventing it from crashing to the ground.

“Quick, return to the ancestral hall!” Lu Yang yelled. Now that we’re outside the ancestral hall, we can die from one of the town mayor’s attacks anytime!

“You want to come in?” The town mayor’s mouth twisted into a cold smile. The ancestral hall was two stories high, and he was blocking the entrance. With me here, these two little brats can never get inside!

“It’s all or nothing!” Lu Yang charged at the town mayor, his footwork nimble, likely aiming to slide across from under the town mayor.

The town mayor naturally saw through Lu Yang’s intentions. He lifted his two front legs, planning to crush the annoying fellow.

Unexpectedly, Lu Yang shifted his stance and darted to the side, causing the town mayor’s feet to miss.

“We’ve finally lured you out.” An uncanny smile stretched across Lu Yang’s face.

Noticing Lu Yang’s smile, a sense of foreboding seeped into the town mayor. He saw Meng Jingzhou raise the Buddha statue again and fling it at him.

As the Buddha statue shattered, the chaotic passageway toward the outside world opened beneath the town mayor. The bone-tormenting gales from within blew toward him like tens and thousands of knives slicing his skin, the pain piercing deep into his bones and forcing a blood-curdling scream from him.

The town mayor desperately tried to get away but was trapped by the passageway. When this group of ancient Fusion cultivators designed the passageway, they had designed it such that once anyone stepped inside, there was no escape—they were doomed to die. Those who attempted to escape the town by shattering the statue would only find themselves at a dead end.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou laughed coldly. “Anyone who enters the passageway is doomed to die, yet you are supposed to be undying. I’m curious to see whether your rule or the passageway’s rule is stronger!”

From the very beginning, the two had no intention of seeking help from the Dao-Seeking Sect through their jade pendants.

It was all merely a ruse tossed to the town mayor.

Chapter 140: Talking About Body Takeover in Front of Me, Huang Doudou?

<Buyi Town’s Rule 21: If you leave the town or kill the town mayor, you no longer need to abide by the rules of Buyi Town.>

When the apothecary owner explicated Rule 21 to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, the two immediately arrived at the same idea.

If we can neither leave the town nor kill the town mayor, when these two conditions clash, which would win? Since we don’t know, let’s give it a try.

Regardless of whether the town mayor left the town or whether they killed him, both would work in their favor. If the town mayor left, Buyi Town would become their territory, and they could seek other means of escape, perhaps by starting with the private school teacher. Moreover, the two were convinced that the town mayor’s absence would have an impact on Buyi Town. That said, it would be best if they could kill the town mayor and directly overcome this ordeal. However, making the town mayor step into the passageway would be no easy task. They had no idea where the ancestral hall was or who the town mayor was.

But that was not a problem for them. As long as they stirred up chaos in Buyi Town, the town mayor would take action. The person who set the rules wouldn’t tolerate anyone breaking them, since this was tantamount to slapping them in the face directly and telling them that their rules were full of loopholes. As such, the two chose to exploit the rules to wreak havoc in Buyi Town.

Lu Yang first created a smokescreen by fabricating a function of the jade pendant and deliberately communicated with paper, giving off the impression that it was an idea he wanted to keep secret. However, since they were already aware that nothing could escape the town mayor’s eyes, how could Lu Yang possibly write their plan down?

The town mayor mocked the two for being too full of themselves, not realizing he too was conceited. Falling for Lu Yang’s trick, he focused all his attention on the jade pendants. After that, the two toyed with the yamen bailiffs several times as an affront to the town mayor, declaring to him that his men were no match for them. Since his subordinates couldn’t take care of them, the town mayor would definitely take matters into his own hands to get rid of them.

Thinking that everything would be resolved just by stealing the jade pendants, the town mayor waited for the two to walk into his trap in the ancestral hall, but he hadn’t expected that the two never intended to use the jade pendants in the first place—their goal was to make the town mayor appear in the ancestral hall.

As for how Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou discussed their plan? They needed no discussion for such a simple scheme.

After all, how could we consider ourselves branch leaders of a diabolic creed if we don’t have some crafty tricks up our sleeves?

~~~

Now, at the entrance of the ancestral hall, the town mayor was trapped within the bone-tormenting gales. As the “Undying Rule” and “Inevitable Death Rule” tussled with each other, his body was in a constant state of being mangled and regenerating, the unbearable pain making him wish he could take his own life there and then.

“What on earth is this thing?” Lu Yang had never seen a monster like the town mayor.

“It’s beastification!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stated in Lu Yang’s mind.

“Beastification?” Lu Yang ran through the cultivation knowledge stored in his mind but found no corresponding terminology. Seems like it’s a cultivation method from ancient times that has already been lost.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “This type of cultivation method was in trend for a while during ancient times. A human body could devour demons, allowing it to harness the advantages of both humans and demons. It may be very powerful, but it also has a major drawback—the user cannot become an immortal.

“Becoming an immortal requires a pure body, so such a human and demon hybrid body can’t form a Dao Fruit. As time passed, people stopped practicing it.”

Lu Yang wondered, “Could the other party also be from the ancient era?”

“Very unlikely. Those from ancient times are cognizant of the drawbacks of this cultivation method. It’s more probable that someone from later eras obtained this cultivation method but only learned its benefits and not its flaws.

“‘The more ancient and lost in time something is, the better it is.’ Such a mindset is very normal. However, ancient things may not necessarily be powerful, and there must be reasons why something has been lost in the mists of time; perhaps nobody could cultivate it or nobody was willing to cultivate it. We need to adopt an objective view.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shrugged.

Something like this was very common in ancient times. For instance, some young man accidentally stumbles across an ancient ruin and attains an ancient cultivation method, believing that he will be unbeatable in the future. However, he is unaware that it is precisely because the cultivation method is too ancient that it is flawed, and the path is completely cut off at the Nascent Soul Stage.

The pathway from the Qi Training Stage to becoming an immortal was now common knowledge, but forging this complete path required cultivation methods to be passed down through countless generations, with countless lives lost along the way.

With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s wealth of experience, she easily revealed many pieces of information that were unknown in the present day.

The town mayor glowered at the two. As someone who could cultivate to the Fusion Stage, he was certainly not a fool. Right after falling into their trap, he immediately figured out their whole artifice.

Unfortunately, it was all too late.

Finally, the “Undying Rule” succumbed to the “Inevitable Death Rule,” and the town mayor’s body disappeared.

This outcome was just as the two had predicted. From the beginning, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had already mentioned that rules could not be overly defiant of the natural order, so there wouldn’t be rules such as “absolutely unbeatable” and “absolutely undying.” As such, the town mayor’s “Undying Rule” wouldn’t be too absolute.

“Die? I am the Immortal Vanquisher True Person,[1] imperishable through countless tribulations with an indestructible true soul. How can I fail here?”

The town mayor was just a body the Immortal Vanquisher True Person had taken over, not his true body. In theory, since the town mayor’s physical body had died, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou should have passed the test. However, the Immortal Vanquisher True Person couldn’t endure such humiliation.

As a dignified Fusion expert who has lived for thousands of years and schemed against countless opponents, how could I end up getting outsmarted by two Foundation Establishment cultivators?

I can’t take this lying down! Even if I have to violate the rules and suffer damage to my soul today, I must kill these two brats!

“Hmm, you have a Sword Spirit Root?” Without the restrictions of a physical body, the Immortal Vanquisher True Person was more perceptive. He could sense that one of them had a Single’s Spirit while the other had a Sword Spirit Root, both top-tier talents that far outclassed the town mayor.

Sword Spirit Root is renowned for its offensive power. If I can possess a body with a Sword Spirit Root and combine it with my Immortal Vanquisher Secret Spell, I’ll definitely surpass my original self, and breaking through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage may even be possible! Moreover, at the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage, my Immortal Vanquisher Secret Spell can strike down immortals. I’ll be invincible then! Even when the Great Era arrives, who can stand in my way?

He cackled out loud. “Looks like this is an opportunity the heavens have bestowed upon me!” This is really an unexpected massive gain. Just when one thinks that all hope is lost, amidst the shadows of the willows, a bright path to a village appears—there will be a silver lining.[2] To him, Lu Yang was already in the bag. After all, what waves can a mere Foundation Establishment cultivator stir up before a Fusion cultivator?

Turning into a ball of gray mist, he entered Lu Yang’s mental space, planning to take over his body.

Lu Yang stared at the Immortal Vanquisher True Person in horror and disbelief. “You...you are a Fusion cultivator, but not only do you not follow your own rules, you also want to take over my body?!”

The Immortal Vanquisher True Person sneered, looking at Lu Yang in contempt. At the end of the day, he’s just a child and hasn’t seen through the original essence of the world. “Before you die, I’ll impart to you a principle so that you can accept your death.

“The strong are always right. This is an unchanging principle throughout the ages. When you cannot afford to provoke a Fusion cultivator, you should keep your tail tucked between your legs and behave like you should!”

Lu Yang sighed, “If only everyone could follow the rules and rely on their own abilities to compete. Since you don’t want to play by the rules, don’t blame me for flipping the tables on you.” He dodged to one side, revealing the person behind him as he gestured respectfully.

“Immortal Fairy, I’m counting on you.”

Then, the Immortal Vanquisher True Person saw the Everlasting Immortal Fairy casually reclining with her legs crossed. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at the Immortal Vanquisher True Person disdainfully, her lips curling into a smile that seemed to be of mockery and scorn. “Young man, you have quite the guts to be talking about body takeover in front of this immortal.”

“Hmm?” Question marks were popping out of the Immortal Vanquisher True Person’s head. Why are there two people inside the mental space? And why is the other person referring to herself as an immortal?

For no apparent reason, he felt a dreadful sense of impending doom.

1. Zhenren or “True Person” is one of a few honorific forms of address for high-level cultivators. ☜

2. This famous idiom is adapted from the poet, Lu You, of the Song Dynasty. ☜

Chapter 141: The Might of An Immortal

Within the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had her delicate leg propped up. She glanced at the Immortal Vanquisher True Person but paid him no attention. Her expression was lazy, and her eyes were half-closed. She extended her slender fingers and admired them, as if the Immortal Vanquisher True Person wasn’t in front of her.

The Immortal Vanquisher True Person barked, “Who are you?!” However, deep down he was very insecure. Lu Yang should be the only person inside his mental space. Why are there two people? This doesn’t make sense!

I also can’t discern the cultivation of this indolent woman, which means that she is at least of the same realm as I am. But why would someone like that choose to stay in the mental space of a Foundation Establishment cultivator?

The Everlasting Immoral yawned lazily, having no plans of acknowledging the Immortal Vanquisher True Person.

The Immortal Vanquisher True Person burst into rage. We are both Fusion cultivators. Do you honestly think that you’re better than I am? When have I ever suffered such humiliation? Since she has no intention of talking, I’ll let my fists do the talking!

He gathered his essence, qi, and spirit, condensing them into an Overlord Saber. His feet that were planted firmly into the ground resembled two jiao dragons.[1] As power flowed upward through his leg, crackling sounds emitted from his soul, as though a valve had been opened, spilling forth all his energy. He accumulated all his power within the Overlord Saber, its white shimmer blinding.

The phantom image of a towering Ox Devil shrouded the entire mental space. Its eyes were red, its muscles bulging, and it exhibited immense strength, clearly a demon beast that achieved its fame in ancient times.

As the Overlord Saber waved down toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it felt as if it encompassed the power of the four seas and five mountains, its sheer force evoking the impression that it was capable of world annihilation. This was the Immortal Vanquisher True Person’s signature ultimate technique, bearing the might to obliterate all obstacles in its path.

“Ox Devil Overlord Saber!”

The Ox Devil phantom began to charge toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. The Immortal Vanquisher True Person recklessly went all out in crushing her, forcing her to admit the disparity between them and recognize what the supremacy of the strong meant.

Faced with the Immortal Vanquisher True Person’s full-on attack, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t even bother lifting her eyelids, merely uttering a word softly, “Noisy.” The word was spoken indifferently and devoid of warmth, yet it carried the weight of mountains as it pressed down on her opponent.

The Immortal Vanquisher True Person felt an ineffable divine force descend upon him, so unreasonable and forceful that he had no chance of resisting. Under the pressure of the word “noisy,” the Ox Devil phantom disappeared, and the three energies dissipated from the Overlord Saber.

Thud! The Immortal Vanquisher True Person fell to his knees, unable to lift even a finger. No words could describe the terror in his heart. The opponent’s power was beyond his comprehension. This is definitely not a Fusion cultivator! It has to be at the Transcendent Tribulation or even higher... He didn’t dare let his thoughts wander further as he recalled that his opponent had referred to herself as an immortal.

There was an insurmountable chasm between the Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation stages, one that could not be overcome by any means. They were worlds apart, and the Immortal Vanquisher True Person had no way to resist. As for the discrepancies between the higher levels, those were completely beyond his imagination.

“Senior, perhaps there is some misunderstanding between us...” The Immortal Vanquisher True Person put on a conciliatory smile, trying his best to explain to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. To have been able to reach the Fusion Stage in ancient times, he naturally mastered the art of bowing and submitting when necessary.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy finally lifted her eyelids, her elegant brow furrowing as she glanced at the Immortal Vanquisher True Person, who knelt obsequiously. “Who allowed you to look at this immortal directly?”

Another wave of divine strength weighed down on the Immortal Vanquisher True Person’s head, completely erasing all remaining hopes of retaliation. Bitterness washed over his heart. He’d thought that the heavens had rewarded Lu Yang to him, only to realize that he was completely wrong when he tried to take over his body—the heavens had rewarded him to Lu Yang.

Why is there such a powerful entity inside a Foundation Establishment cultivator’s mental space?

“Now, I shall allow you to explain the situation,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said emotionlessly.

The Immortal Vanquisher True Person didn’t dare to hide anything from her. He knew that some personages had the ability to discern truth from lies, and this was not something he was willing to bet on before his opponent. “My Dao title is the Immortal Vanquisher True Person, and there are four other Fusion cultivators outside Buyi Town. The five of us are from the Great Yu Dynasty. Limited by our talents, we couldn’t progress beyond the Fusion Stage, so the Transcendent Tribulation Stage was an unattainable goal.

“I’m not sure where the rumor came from, but at that time, we heard that spirit opportunities weren’t active and spirit qi was in a dormant state, making cultivation extremely difficult. However, more than ten thousand years later, the spirit qi would gradually awaken, and the prosperity of the ancient era would resurge. When that happened, a myriad of fortuitous opportunities would emerge, and ascending to be an immortal might not be entirely impossible.

“Some said that the rumor came from the imperial palace, others said that the emperor preceptor had calculated it, and some even said that it was a revelation gained by the Imperial Astronomy Bureau from observing the sun. In any case, there were all kinds of theories.

“After we five brothers discussed, we concluded that since we couldn’t reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage then, rather than idling in the Great Yu Dynasty, we might as well seal ourselves with spirit stone marrow and quietly wait for the heaven and earth to become active again. Even if the rumor was false, we wouldn’t lose anything. After all, five Fusion cultivators would be a force to reckon with in any era or place.

“Later, the five of us found ourselves awakening beneath Buyi Town, and to our pleasant surprise, there were signs of our long-stagnant bottleneck loosening. This era is indeed much more conducive to cultivation than ours. However, there was still some time before we could fully awaken, and we didn’t want the cultivators of this era to discover us. Hence, we worked together to establish the rules of Buyi Town so that we could restore our strength and collect information in the meantime.

“I was the most unlucky. There was a problem with the spirit bone marrow that sealed me, and my physical body had died over time, so only my soul was sealed. After awakening, I took over the body of the person with the best aptitude nearby. Since my body was frail and prone to accidents, in order to protect myself, the five of us agreed that I should become the town mayor of Buyi Town.

“Just like that, I made myself an undying presence, devouring mortals and wild beasts while hastening my pace of cultivation to master the Immortal Vanquisher Secret Spell as soon as possible.”

After the Immortal Vanquisher True Person recounted everything truthfully, he didn’t dare raise his head and naturally couldn’t see the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s subtle movements.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy winked at Lu Yang, her dainty feet bouncing up and down in excitement, as if to say, “See, there are times where I can be reliable too. You should show more respect to me from now on.” Ever since her resurrection, she had faced continuous setbacks and humiliating defeats. First, she was suppressed by Yun Zhi. Then, she failed in every single attempt to showcase her merits to Lu Yang. Now that I’ve finally found a chance to hold her head high, how can I waste this opportunity to show off?

Lu Yang sighed inwardly. Immortal Fairy, with the way you’re acting, how am I supposed to find you reliable?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sensed that Lu Yang’s gaze did not reflect the respect she had imagined, so she pouted and ignored him.

I’ve clearly shown that I am very reliable.

1. Jiaolong or jiao dragon is a Chinese mythical sea creature. ☜

Chapter 142: Successfully Leaving Buyi Town

“Immortal Vanquisher Secret Spell?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy narrowed her eyes. She had never heard of a secret spell with such an arrogant name. Immortals stood at the pinnacle of the cultivation journey, undefeatable by those beneath them. If immortals can be vanquished, then what is the point of becoming one?

“Y-yes,” the Immortal Vanquisher True Person stammered as he humbly offered up the Immortal Vanquisher Secret Spell, from which he had derived his Dao title. “When I was young, I accidentally stumbled across a secret domain that was created by a formidable ancient expert, one filled with endless natural treasures. It was thanks to these treasures that I managed to reach the Fusion Stage.

“The most precious of them all was this book titled Immortal Vanquisher Secret Spell. According to the book, immortals are the monarchs of all beings and possess unrivaled power. If one wanted to defeat an immortal, one would have to blaze a new trail. The book mentioned that one could accumulate the strengths of all beings into one body, such as the transformation ability of the giant kun fish and great peng bird, the water control of the dragons, the fire mastery of the phoenixes, the wisdom of humans, and so forth; all these advantages can allow one’s mortal strength to vanquish immortals!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nonchalantly flipped through a few pages of the book before tossing it to Lu Yang. “I thought it was something impressive with all that boasting. Turns out it’s just a beastification cultivation technique.”

She had just explicated the cultivation technique of beastification. The result would be a mottled bloodline that rendered one incapable of ascending to an immortal, so it had been abandoned by people of ancient times. As for the so-called mighty power to vanquish immortals, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy scoffed at it even more. If it were really as amazing as he had bragged, why would it have been discarded?

“So you’re saying that everything in here is fake?” Lu Yang browsed through the contents, but they were too complex for him to understand in such a short time.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scratched her chin. “I reckon the person who invented the beastification cultivation technique was indignant about it being abandoned. However, everyone in ancient times knew what this cultivation technique exactly entailed and how unreliable it was, so no one would be duped.

“As such, he changed the book’s cover, added a preface, changed its name, and threw it inside a cave. Given enough time, the people who knew about the beastification cultivation technique would grow fewer. When some fool stumbles upon it and believes its contents, the beastification cultivation technique would be propagated once again.” She said disdainfully, “It’s just talking big. Who can’t do that? I could even say that I can beat that lass Yun Zhi.”

Lu Yang suspected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was giving up and letting everything rot[1].

She continued to provide him with some educational advice, “Don’t assume that everything in some ancient text is true. Counterfeiting was rampant in our time, with more things fake than real.

“We even fabricated a whole Heavenly Court system then. After one becomes an immortal, they will ascend to the Immortal Realm, where there are Human Immortals, Earthly Immortals, Heavenly Immortals, the Five-Direction Heavenly Emperor, and whatnot. Anyway, it was pretty pretty well-constructed. If you do come across it, don’t believe any of it. We made all that up for fun.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Verifying historical details of ancient times is already arduous enough as it is, yet you’re telling me that falsifying was a trend? Lu Yang’s heart went out to those old cultivators who were passionate about studying ancient times. They spend an enormous amount of effort researching what happened during the ancient era, yet they are misled by the things you fabricate, sincerely marveling at the grandeur of ancient times. They believe that there were higher levels beyond immortals and that cultivation had no limits, a stark contrast to the present time, only to end up discovering that you had made all that up for fun.

Can their old hearts suffer this brutal blow?

Fortunately, up until now, Lu Yang hadn’t heard anything about the Heavenly Court system. It was probably lost to the river of time and did not contaminate the later generations.

The Immortal Vanquisher True Person was trembling as he knelt on the ground. Listening to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eloquent elaborations, he felt he had learned of something monumental. Not only can she speak of matters from ancient times easily, but she also refers to herself as an immortal. I no longer have to doubt my luck.

And as for this Foundation Establishment youngster, although his cultivation is low, he can converse with an ancient immortal on equal terms. Could he also be an ancient immortal? Is it reincarnation or a body takeover?

The Immortal Vanquisher True Person wished he could give himself two slaps to the face. Why did I have to call myself “Immortal Vanquisher” of all names? And why was I so blind as to charge into his mental space?

Am I tired of living?!

He gingerly backed away and sensed that the pressure had diminished. This indicates that her attention isn’t on me. While they were distracted talking, he planned to seize this opportunity to sneak out of the mental space and make a run for it.

Then, he realized the mental space was as sturdy as a coffin—there was no means of escape.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy laughed coldly. Lu Yang’s mental space is essentially my house. How can anyone enter and leave an immortal’s house as they please?

“You want to leave? Then leave your life behind.”

She abhorred the Immortal Vanquisher True Person’s cultivation method. When the rules first descended, she could only imagine the number of civilians that perished under them. Furthermore, judging by the town mayor’s physical body, it could not have been achieved without slaughtering hundreds or thousands of people.

As an immortal who originated from the human race, I don’t dare claim that I am noble or have protected many humans, but I can confidently proclaim that I have never harmed anyone.

He deserves to die.

When she extended her finger, the Immortal Vanquisher True Person desperately writhed in an attempt to dodge, but no matter how hard he tried, there was no escape for him.

This was a guaranteed strike!

The moment the finger touched his forehead, the Immortal Vanquisher True Person’s soul instantly disintegrated.

~~~

“It’s so hard to deal with this person!” Outside Buyi Town, the four Fusion cultivators found their battle against the Taciturn Daoist Priest especially cumbersome. Among the ten thousand swords, they had finally found the one the Taciturn Daoist Priest had fused with. Just as they were about to confront him head-on, however, the Taciturn Daoist Priest repeated the same trick, unleashing One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords and Person and Sword as One.

Are you sure these kinds of moves can be performed in succession?!

“If you don’t come out, we’ll go to Buyi Town and kill those two little brats!” one of the Fusion cultivators bellowed in rage. This was not an empty threat; they were perfectly capable of doing something like that.

Suddenly, the ten thousand swords formed a massive sphere with the tips pointing inward, enclosing the four of them. These swords shot out simultaneously, targeting the four of them. They hadn’t expected the Taciturn Daoist Priest to unleash a burst of power, so they could only suffer a severe loss.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest revealed his true self, wielding his life-bound sword as he stared fixedly at the four. “Let’s see who dares to harm them!”

Meeting the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s gaze, the four found it especially penetrating, and a chill seeped into their hearts. If a supreme sword cultivator goes all out, we’ll lose at least two of us.

One of them snorted. “You’re just bluffing. The town mayor of Buyi Town is our companion. Did you really think those two juniors could remain unscathed just by following the rules obediently? When our companion takes those two as hostages, I’m curious to see what you can do. Are you going to disregard their lives to kill us or drop your sword and let us kill you?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest gritted his teeth as he gripped the hilt of his sword tightly. If what they say is true, then I must risk my lifespan and cultivation to kill the four of them before anything can happen!

As the two parties faced off, the four Fusion cultivators were about to taunt the Taciturn Daoist Priest that they had captured his two juniors, but that was when a teleportation array suddenly appeared outside Buyi Town. Their expressions changed drastically, and they coughed up a mouthful of blood.

“How is that possible? Someone made use of the rules to leave Buyi Town?!” They would suffer a backlash if someone left Buyi Town.

The teleportation array vanished—Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had successfully left Buyi Town. Holding the town mayor’s head, Lu Yang greeted the people in the sky with a smile, his intention to provoke them laid bare.

Cough! The four Fusion cultivators spat out blood once more.

1. ”Bailan” is a modern slang which refers to giving up and not caring about letting things get worse ☜

Chapter 143: Lu Yang Is in a Delusional Fantasy Phase

Including the Taciturn Daoist Priest, none of the five had expected Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to leave the town successfully. Even without a Fusion cultivator overseeing Buyi Town, the overt and covert rules alone weren’t something ordinary people could deal with. Surviving in Buyi Town was already hard enough, much less leaving the place.

How on earth did these two do it?

The Taciturn Daoist Priest didn’t ponder too much. While the four Fusion cultivators were weakened and spitting blood with their attention on Lu Yang, he suddenly unleashed his power. Azure sword qi emanated from all over his body, gently undulating like a pond of clear water. As nimble as a snake, the sword qi traced an arc gracefully, sending two heads flying through the air.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy exclaimed, “Your shifu is quite the capable one. He can compete with the top sword cultivators of our era. This sword of his slashed both their physical bodies as well as their three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls,[1] completely killing off those two Fusion cultivators.”

Lu Yang was astonished. Despite it being one against four, Shifu could directly kill the two of them while they were caught off guard. He definitely lives up to his reputation.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy and the Taciturn Daoist Priest didn’t have the best debuts—one was suppressed, while the other was confined in a cave for ten years. Their initial impression was so dismal that Lu Yang subconsciously overlooked their identities. One was an ancient immortal, one of the five immortals and most powerful beings in the chaotic ancient era. The other was a sect leader of one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, someone even the reigning emperor had to receive with the highest honors. Despite being the youngest of the Dao-Seeking Nine and the last to begin cultivation, his combat power was the greatest among them.

Ordinary cultivators could soar to prominence and lead a life free of worries with just the slightest bit of connection with these two, but Lu Yang didn’t feel this way at all.

Is it really because of Big Senior Sister? Lu Yang seemed to have found a reason to convince himself. The first time I met them, they suffered humiliating setbacks because of Big Senior Sister. Now that Big Senior Sister isn’t present, they can finally showcase their abilities.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest readied his sword, his eyes gleaming with vigor, as if he was about to unleash another sword attack.

The remaining two Fusion cultivators sensed the perilous situation they were in and turned to flee, not even bothering to retrieve their companions’ bodies.

However, the Taciturn Daoist Priest did not pursue them. Although he could launch another strike, the two were likely able to parry it and retaliate, especially since he had lost the element of surprise. He wasn’t afraid of going for another round of battle, but he was worried that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou wouldn’t be able to withstand the brunt of a battle between Fusion cultivators.

“Are you both alright?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest hurriedly went over to check on the two. Finding neither of them injured, he was relieved that they had held up well in Buyi Town the past few days.

“We’re fine.” As the two sensed the spirit qi in the surroundings, they couldn’t help but feel a wave of emotions wash over them. We’ve finally left Buyi Town. Having control over spirit energy feels amazing! The inability to use spells in Buyi Town had more or less stifled their talents.

“Good to hear that, good to hear that.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest heaved a sigh of relief. “It’s just that those two managed to escape.” He then looked at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou in puzzlement. “Speaking of which, wasn’t there supposed to be a Fusion cultivator in Buyi Town? How did you take care of him?” Perhaps they had received some methods to protect their lives—Lu Yang from Little Yun or Meng Jingzhou from the Meng Family.

Finding the Taciturn Daoist Priest trustworthy, Lu Yang explained, “Actually, I have an ancient immortal sealed within me who usually guides me on my cultivation and also provides power in critical moments. Even killing a Fusion cultivator is not a problem.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest gazed at Lu Yang with pity and patted the latter’s head gently. Remembering Lu Yang’s age, he came to terms with it. That’s right, it’s normal for a sixteen or seventeen-year-old child to be in a delusional fantasy phase.

When I was sixteen, I had also gone through a similar fantasy phase. I imagined I had an ancient ferocious beast sealed within me. When others angered me, the seal would loosen, and the ferocious beast’s power would leak out and harm the innocent. In severe cases, it could even lead to widespread devastation and cause irreparable loss. Therefore, to keep the ferocious beast sealed within me, I must maintain a cold demeanor at all times.

Who hasn’t been through such a delusional phase?

What ancient immortal? I’ve lived for two thousand years and have never seen an ancient immortal. How could this kid be so lucky to not only encounter an ancient immortal but also have the immortal reside within him?

Little Yun must have left Lu Yang some survival methods.

“Is the ancient immortal you speak of an old man or a beautiful woman?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest asked.

Lu Yang thought about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s appearance. When she’s quiet, she does look like a peerless beauty that rivals Big Senior Sister. “A beautiful woman.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest thought to himself, Just as I thought, my guess was on the mark! At this age, the immortals they fantasize about are either old men or beautiful women, certainly not a young man, middle-aged man, or old woman.

He stared at Buyi Town, which was still plagued by the rules, and paused for a moment before saying, “Let’s head to a nearby municipal office first, then leave the follow-up matters to them.”

There were too many civilians in Buyi Town. Although his cultivation was exceptional, he couldn’t simply rely on cultivation to solve such matters. It would require the professionals to step in. Since the case of Buyi Town involved five ancient Fusion cultivators, it was beyond what a commandery governor could handle, so the Taciturn Daoist Priest needed to find the provincial governor.

The Great Xia Dynasty had divided the Central Continent into seventeen regions, what people often referred to as the seventeen provinces. Below the provinces were commanderies, and below the commanderies were counties and towns.

As the Taciturn Daoist Priest didn’t know the way, he inquired in the nearby commanderies and learned that they were currently in Qing Province, which was in the western part of the Central Continent.

“Hold on, why are we in the western region of the Central Continent?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou looked at the Taciturn Daoist Priest suspiciously. When we were setting off from the Dao-Seeking Sect, didn’t he say that we were heading south?

The Taciturn Daoist Priest laughed awkwardly and didn’t explain, simply reassuring the two that they could just follow him.

~~~

After asking for directions throughout their journey, the three finally found the provincial governor of Qing Province.

Right as the provincial governor heard that the sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect was paying him a visit, he immediately set aside all his other matters and personally welcomed the Taciturn Daoist Priest. As the provincial governor of Qing Province, he was in charge of countless resources within the province and received reverence and flattery from many, but in terms of status and cultivation, he was a far cry from the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest didn’t engage in much small talk, directly explaining the situation in Buyi Town and letting Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou supplement the specific details when necessary.

Hearing the incident with Buyi Town, the provincial governor broke out in a cold sweat. Five ancient Fusion cultivators awakening is a serious matter. It is fortunate that the sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect discovered it in time and dealt with it appropriately. Had the five fully awakened and hid themselves somewhere, they could’ve easily annihilated several commanderies, and countless people would die then.

The provincial governor swiftly acted. He mobilized the local officials at the Divine Transfiguration and Fusion stages and sent letters to the army stationed in Qing Province and the imperial court, informing them that two ancient Fusion cultivators had awakened and escaped and advising them to remain vigilant. As for presenting the documents to the imperial court and requesting commendation for the Dao-Seeking Sect, there was currently no time for that. It would have to wait until they resolved the issues concerning the civilians of Buyi Town.

Lu Yang observed that the provincial governor didn’t deploy any Void Refinement cultivators.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest explained, “The Void Refinement Stage is very special. During this phase, a cultivator’s strength is very unstable and constantly fluctuates. At its peak, it could reach the Apex Fusion Stage, but at its lowest, it may only be at the Qi Training Stage. As such, Void Refinement cultivators prefer to stay in one place for stability and rarely take action.

“And no one would easily provoke a Void Refinement cultivator. After all, you never know what realm they may be at the next moment.”

1. This is a Daoism concept. There are three hun and seven po to a person’s soul. Only when all three hun and seven po are present will a person’s soul be complete, and the person can be healthy. ☜

Chapter 144: So All of You Are Very Reserved When I Am Around?

The provincial governor led the officials of Qing Province toward Buyi Town in a grand procession. With a seal from the provincial governor smashing down, the rules enveloping the small town shattered into invisible fragments and gradually collapsed.

This wasn’t the provincial governor’s own strength but the authority granted to him by the Great Xia Dynasty; it allowed him to mobilize a fraction of people’s powers.

The group of cultivators were no strangers to resolving such matters. With their intervention, everything about the rules including avoiding eye contact with the private school teacher and the danger of the thatched cottages in the day became nothing but jokes.

They captured the private school teacher, ferreted out the dark figure hiding among the thatched cottages, investigated how many of the townsfolk were animated corpses and living people, and studied whether those transformed into black dogs could be restored to their original selves. Everything was handled in an orderly fashion.

It was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s first time witnessing such a scene. There was no concept of a nation in ancient times, and the systems built around clans and tribes lacked such a clear division of labor and organization.

According to the Taciturn Daoist Priest, this was just the power of the imperial dynasty. If they joined forces with the Five Great Immortal Sects, they would be able to sweep through the ancient cultivators.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou managed to find the innkeeper who had been rescued. Upon seeing the two of them, he burst into tears of joy. He had never expected that the two could truly solve their predicament, especially in such a short time.

I really shouldn’t have suspected them to be diabolic cultivators.

The Qing Province officials also discovered that the apothecary owner was the town mayor’s covert accomplice, and there was tons of evidence of his crimes. Under the restrictions of the rules, the apothecary owner appeared to be speaking the truth but had actually concealed other facts, harming numerous people.

The apothecary apprentice, private school teacher, yamen bailiffs, and the restaurant owner who prepared the meat baozi were all detained, pending further investigation to reach a verdict.

The provincial governor wrote a court document on the spot to report the three’s involvement to the court, but the Taciturn Daoist Priest stopped him, asking him to remove Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s names.

However, they should still receive their due rewards, so the Taciturn Daoist Priest invited the two outstanding juniors for a meal at the most bustling restaurant in Qing Province.

~~~

“Haha, this matter is finally concluded! Although our travel plans encountered a slight hiccup, it’s ultimately a small issue. Once we’ve had our fill, I’ll take you to experience the splendor of the southern region. Since your Big Senior Sister isn’t here this time, the three of us can have fun to our heart’s content. Don’t worry, I’ll take responsibility if anything happens!” The Taciturn Daoist Priest laughed heartily. Since the authorities will handle the rest of the matters, I’m no longer in the picture. After finally getting out, it’s only natural to let loose.

“Oh? Is that so? So all of you are very reserved when I am around?” A cold voice caused the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s laughter to come to an abrupt halt.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou just realized a hush had draped over the lively restaurant. Only their table was still full of chatter and jokes. Now that the three of them fell silent, the entire restaurant was so quiet that one could even hear the sound of a needle dropping to the floor.
