The diners had long noticed the arrival of a peerless beauty at the restaurant. As soon as she appeared, she captivated everyone. Awestruck by her beauty and demeanor, everyone instinctively closed their mouths and didn’t dare to breathe, fearing that the woman would notice them.

The woman then chose a table and sat down, quietly watching the three roistering without restraint. No one saw that she was also holding two chains, each binding a soul.

Finally, the woman spoke, and only then did the three notice her presence.

“Oh...oh, it’s you, Little Yun! Come come come, sit down and eat with us.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest squeezed out a smile.

“Hello, Big Senior Sister,” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou greeted her in a docile manner.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was astonished when he saw the two chains in Yun Zhi’s hands, recognizing that they fettered the two Fusion cultivators who had escaped. “Little Yun, when did you find us?”

“The first time you performed One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords and Person and Sword as One.”

Cold sweat trickled profusely from the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s forehead. That happened just a day ago. No wonder Little Yun could catch these two.

He calmed himself down and mused, I didn’t say anything bad about Little Yun today. Phew, thank goodness.

The two Fusion cultivators in Yun Zhi’s clutches looked at her in horror. This person simply struck us with her palm from afar and sent our souls flying away. Which cultivation stage is this?! Why do we keep encountering these kinds of monsters one after another?!

What happened to “the revival of the ancient era and fortuitous opportunities everywhere?” It’s dangers everywhere!

“Initially, I was worried that you wouldn’t recognize the way and lead the two of them astray, Shifu. I didn’t expect you three to have such a good time when I’m not around,” Yun Zhi said flatly, sending chills down the spines of the three.

Meng Jingzhou was the fastest to react, pointing at Lu Yang. “It’s all because of Lu Yang! I didn’t want to come, but he called me over.”

Lu Yang quickly pointed at the Taciturn Daoist Priest. “It’s all because of Shifu! He said he had to fulfill his responsibility as my shifu and take me out to see the world!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest pointed at Meng Jingzhou. “It’s all because of this youngster’s grandfather! He entrusted me with his grandson, and that’s why I took them out to play!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s wealth of experience with getting into trouble told him that shifting the blame to someone not at the scene was the wisest option.

Yun Zhi swept her frigid gaze across the three. “Shifu, you will continue promoting the glorious deeds and achievements of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, you two will come back with me.” Yun Zhi was afraid that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou would learn from her master’s improper habits.

Before taking the two back, she told the Taciturn Daoist Priest, “Do let the provincial governor of Qing Province know that I’ve already captured the perpetrators and that he need not worry.” Yun Zhi planned to take the two Fusion captives back with her and see if she could extract any useful information.

~~~

On the way back, Lu Yang boasted to Yun Zhi, claiming that he had taken down a Fusion cultivator, and asked whether he could receive some contribution points.

Yun Zhi was baffled. “Was it not Huang Doudou who killed the Fusion cultivator?”

Hearing Yun Zhi’s words, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t even mind Yun Zhi calling her by name, asking in excitement, “So can I get contribution points?”

“You're not from the Dao-Seeking Sect, so that’s naturally not possible.”

Without a thought, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy announced, “Then I’ll join the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Lu Yang stared at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in shock. How could you just join like that? What happened to acting like a cool immortal?

Yun Zhi nodded. “It is fine to have an immortal joining the Dao-Seeking Sect. I can make an exception for you to become the Dao-Seeking Sect’s first honorary guest, but only I can know your identity. In return, you will receive this round of contribution points and a treatment similar to elders. If you agree to these terms, you can join.”

“I'll join.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy quite liked the atmosphere in the Dao-Seeking Sect. It’s very similar to my personality, which is a rare thing.

Yun Zhi brought up another matter to Lu Yang, “A few days ago, the palace leader of the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace approached me and said that she wants to offer you as compensation to Lan Ting. I thought that since you are of marriageable age and both sects are considered well-matched in terms of status, I agreed to you and Lan Ting’s union as Dao partners. However, for some reason, the palace leader suddenly changed her mind. Do you have any clue why? Is it because they feel you don’t measure up?”

Lu Yang was utterly flummoxed.

Chapter 145: The Strongest Person Among the Five Great Immortal Sects

Meng Jingzhou patted Lu Yang on the shoulder. “You’re finally also outstanding enough to have someone knocking on your door to propose marriage.”

Lu Yang glanced at Meng Jingzhou. “Also?”

Meng Jingzhou proudly shared, “Since I was a child, imperial relatives, influential ministers, and righteous sect members have come to my house to propose marriage, wanting me and their daughters to become my fiancée. However, my parents and clan elders firmly objected. Otherwise, right now, I would definitely—”

Lu Yang finished the sentence for him, “Definitely end up with kidney deficiency?”

Meng Jingzhou retorted angrily, “Definitely be a dashing young master!”

The two wrestled with each other, howls echoing through the clouds as they both used the Tiger Fist at the same time. Yun Zhi focused on flying, completely ignoring the two of them.

Lu Yang transformed himself into a tiger demon, pressing Meng Jingzhou down with one paw and forcing Meng Jingzhou to beg for mercy. The latter’s Tiger Fist was ultimately no match for Lu Yang’s true tiger form.

After their tussle, Lu Yang still couldn’t understand how his performance in Yanjiang Commandery was so outstanding to have people coming to him for a marriage proposal. Besides, why do terms like “knocking on the door to propose marriage,” “the bride’s side having a change of mind,” and “a powerful soul within” sound so familiar?

~~~

Within the imperial palace in the imperial city of the Great Xia Dynasty, a dignified man clad in black robes adorned with golden patterns sat at a high position on the dais, his expression stern. In a similarly solemn and heavy atmosphere, the officials below called him “Your Majesty.”

“Dear subjects, please rise.”

“Thank you, Your Majesty.”

The Xia Emperor swept his gaze across the officials and held up a court document. “I just received a court document from the provincial governor of Qing Province, stating that five ancient Fusion cultivators had awakened in a place called Buyi Town, which then formed a territory. The sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect happened to pass by with two disciples, so they killed three of those Fusion cultivators.”

The officials heaved a sigh of relief. The awakening of five Fusion cultivators is no small matter. Fortunately, the Taciturn Daoist Priest bumped into them. Had it been another Fusion cultivator, they would have immediately been brought down in Buyi Town.

Although the Taciturn Daoist Priest did not have the best reputation and had sabotaged many of them in their youth, his strength was undeniably the pinnacle of Fusion cultivators.

“But there were still two Fusion cultivators who escaped, and they are both at the Apex Fusion Stage,” the Xia Emperor warned the officials, hinting to them the crux of the issue. He wasn’t hoping they would abide by the rules, but cultivation methods from ancient times were very crude and treated human lives as chaff. Furthermore, this group of people had awakened precisely for the goal of seizing fortuitous opportunities in the Great Era, and they would resort to any means necessary. The Great Xia Dynasty had already learned its lesson.

The officials whispered among themselves. If the two Fusion cultivators revealed themselves, there was nothing to fear, since there were many people in court who could handle them. However, the possibility they dreaded was that the two would hide themselves and plot something in secret. It would also get more troublesome if they colluded with the diabolic creeds.

“This bunch of ancient Fusion cultivators!” The Xia Emperor sensed another headache coming. As the spirit opportunities of heaven and earth became increasingly active, more and more ancient cultivators were awakening. This resurgence of this group of Fusion cultivators was a menace. If left unchecked, they could cause catastrophic disasters and countless civilian casualties.

The good news is that no Transcendent Tribulation cultivator has awakened yet.

According to the intelligence gathered thus far, those who had awakened were at the Basic Fusion Stage, and those who awakened later possessed higher cultivation. The five Fusion cultivators that awakened in Buyi Town consisted of four Apex Fusion cultivators and one Advanced Fusion cultivator.

One could predict that there would soon be news of Transcendent Tribulation cultivators awakening. At that time, trouble would erupt from the sea in the east, the Buddhist Kingdom in the west, the Demon Region in the South, the Extreme North, and the Four Great Diabolic Creeds. The reign of the Great Xia Dynasty would become unsteady, and the rumor that every dynasty would last for only a hundred thousand years might very well prove true.

“All of this is for the sake of becoming an immortal!” The Xia Emperor’s gaze turned frosty. He was cognizant of many secrets. All this chaos was orchestrated from the shadows, and the mastermind wanted more Dao Fruits to appear.

The Xia Emperor suspected it was the doing of the Ancient Nameless One, also one of the five ancient immortals.

“Is becoming an immortal really that important?!” The Xia Emperor’s heart swelled with rage, but he displayed none of it outwardly. If the person behind the scenes truly thinks that the Great Xia Dynasty is a mere pawn they can manipulate, they’re gravely mistaken.

Not contemplating the matter of the Ancient Nameless One further, the Xia Emperor shifted his attention back to the two Fusion cultivators.

Just then, the eunuch supervisor received a court document. Upon seeing who the sender was, he hurriedly passed it to the Xia Emperor.

After reading it, the Xia Emperor’s face brightened with delight. “Good, very good!”

The officials were puzzled, curious about what the court document could have contained to make the Xia Emperor so elated.

“No need to worry about those two Fusion cultivators anymore! Yun Zhi from the Dao-Seeking Sect has caught them!”

“Yun Zhi?” Some less-informed officials were baffled, not knowing who Yun Zhi was. Among the Dao-Seeking Sect’s eight elders, there doesn’t seem to be anyone called Yun Zhi.

On the other hand, those well-informed old ministers not only knew Yun Zhi’s identity but also her terrifying abilities, so they were naturally aware that capturing those two Fusion cultivators was no difficult task.

“The Demon Region sent envoys...” the Xia Emperor began discussing other affairs with the officials.

~~~

After the court assembly adjourned, the Xia Emperor returned to the Mental Cultivation Hall[1] and reviewed the court documents.

“Your Majesty, Duke Qin, Jing Yansong seeks your audience,” the eunuch supervisor said softly.

The Xia Emperor didn’t even look up. “Come in.”

After Duke Qin entered the Mental Cultivation Hall, he saw the Xia Emperor busy reviewing the court documents and stayed silent, standing deferentially at a side and waiting for the Xia Emperor to go through the most urgent court documents.

“What is the matter, Duke Qin?” The Xia Emperor looked at Duke Qin with a solemn expression that would scare timid individuals from meeting his gaze.

“Your Majesty, we mustn’t let our guard down against the Dao-Seeking Sect. When Yun Zhi was still a disciple, she once defeated the sect leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects, setting a one-of-a-kind record. Ever since then, she has kept a low profile, but every time she takes action, it is bound to be astonishing. Over the past hundreds of years, her cultivation would have certainly reached a terrifying level.

“I am afraid that her existence may undermine the foundation of the dynasty. After all, the Dao-Seeking Sect was established during the Great Yu Dynasty, and it had witnessed the ‘division of the world into two’ and the ‘founding of the Great Xia Dynasty.’ They might entertain thoughts of replacing us.

“This is not merely my opinion. On my way to the court assembly, I even heard a waiter singing ‘The Dao-Seeking thrives, a peaceful world rises.’”

The Xia Emperor furrowed his brow, and it didn’t escape Duke Qin’s eyes. Seeing that the Xia Emperor had begun harboring suspicions toward the Dao-Seeking Sect, he made no further comments and simply took his leave.

That was when the Xia Emperor summoned the eunuch supervisor. “Go investigate who Duke Qin has met recently. Focus on his interactions with the Demon Region.”

“Understood.”

The Xia Emperor scoffed inwardly. Looks like not everyone in the court has their allegiance with the Great Xia Dynasty.

“Creating a rift between me and the Dao-Seeking Sect? What an astute idea.”

After the Xia Emperor ascended to the throne, he had visited the Five Great Immortal Sects one by one. Upon meeting Yun Zhi at the Dao-Seeking Sect, he was stunned by her unfathomable abilities. He sent people to dig deeper, but they couldn’t uncover her background and secrets, so he directly went to the imperial palace’s forbidden ground to consult the old ancestor whether he knew anything about Yun Zhi.

His old ancestor had remained silent for a long time before replying with a single sentence, “The strongest person among the Five Great Immortal Sects.”

The Xia Emperor pressed further. “And how does she compare to you, old ancestor?”

“Don’t ask anymore.”

The Xia Emperor was unceremoniously kicked out by the old ancestor, who seemed to be fuming from embarrassment.

1. Yangxin Hall was the residence of the emperor, especially during the Qing Dynasty. ☜

Chapter 146: Pure and Innocent Heart of a Newborn

From then on, the Xia Emperor realized that a sour relationship with the Dao-Seeking Sect was what would fulfill the “curse of a hundred thousand years.”

Those in the shadows only know that Yun Zhi is very strong, but they have no idea what her “strength” encompasses. If they learn how powerful she truly is, they’ll know how foolish their attempt at sowing discord is.

~~~

“Big Senior Sister, where are we going?” Lu Yang noticed that after they returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect, Yun Zhi flew past Heaven’s Gate Peak instead of stopping.

This was an area he had never set foot in before. Below them were enormous mountains and vast lakes, red lands of a thousand li, and yellow deserts with loess sediments.

“Incarceration Peak.”

Neither Lu Yang nor Meng Jingzhou had heard of this place.

Yun Zhi finally landed on an eerie mountain peak wrapped in gigantic chains, their other ends coiled around a mountain in each of the four directions.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou could feel their hair pricking up, unable to shake off the feeling that this wasn’t a good place.

Lu Yang had studied a bit of feng shui arrays, where “unobstructed flow” is a key principle. At least one of the four cardinal directions should have a connection to the external world to allow for the flow of vitality. However, Incarceration Peak was surrounded by mountains on all sides, completely blocking off any opportunities for vitality. The clouds almost touching Incarceration Peak resembled a lid that sealed off the area tightly.

Incarceration Peak was a place for imprisoning and interrogating criminals. All criminals were locked away beneath Incarceration Peak.

After the three landed, Yun Zhi opened the entrance to an array and entered the foot of the mountain while carrying the souls of the two Fusion cultivators. They descended for about five thousand meters before coming to a halt.

Upon arriving at Incarceration Peak, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou felt as if they had returned to Buyi Town—they couldn’t activate their spirit energy at all. This was not because of the Spirit Energy Disabling Array but some kind of “Rule.”

The two observed nearly a hundred cages here, most of which were empty. Only a dozen or so had people confined in them, or to be more accurate—soul bodies. Under the suppression of the “Rules,” these soul bodies were dispirited and listless. When some of them caught sight of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, they drooled at the mouth, eager to pounce over and devour them. But once they saw Yun Zhi, they immediately became obedient.

Lu Yang wondered if there were too few prisoners in this place. Even Yanjiang Commandery’s dungeon has more people.

“Be more cautious, those held captive here are ancient Fusion cultivators,” Yun Zhi reminded.

The two instantly shuddered, no longer thinking that there should be more prisoners here. Goodness gracious! More than a dozen Fusion cultivators are locked up here?

“Big Senior Sister, aren’t you worried that they’ll escape?” Lu Yang asked softly.

“Escape? Kid, don’t you think you’re underestimating this old man too much?” a childish voice sounded.

Lu Yang turned in the direction of the voice and saw a child with white hair. The child was short and had to tiptoe just to reach Lu Yang’s waist.

“Grand Shifu.”[1]

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were astonished to learn that the white-haired child was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s master.

“Grand Shifu,” the two greeted.

“Haha, do you think I’m too small?”

“No, not at all.”

The white-haired child spoke in an air of aged wisdom, “The two of you are still too young and lack experience, so you don’t understand my condition. This is a method of cultivation.”

Lu Yang quickly recalled a legend. People of ancient times often say ‘eternal virtue never departs, reverting to a pure infant state’ and ‘the crowd is lively as if partaking in a grand feast or admiring the picturesque sceneries of spring, while I remain alone and aloof like an infant that has yet learn to smile.’[2]

“Many great cultivators spend their whole lives pursuing the pure and innocent heart of a newborn, but they never attain this realm. When the pursuit is deliberate, it is no longer the mindset of a child, so how can they achieve a truly pure heart?”

“Grand Shifu, are you saying that you have already ‘reverted to the pure state of an infant’ and achieved the state of returning to one’s original nature and oneness with the universe, thus embodying the pure heart of a newborn?”

Meng Jingzhou was also surprised. The pure heart of a newborn has always existed in the legends, and none of the clan elders have achieved this state of mind. Who would have thought that someone in the Dao-Seeking Sect has succeeded?

The white-haired child smiled and nodded, displaying an approving expression.

Yun Zhi found it puzzling. “Why does this not match up with the news I’ve heard?

“Grand Shifu, my shifu said that when you were young, you were a notorious ladies’ man, lingering in brothels and hindering your cultivation. Later, you somehow woke up and worked hard in your cultivation journey. To demonstrate your resolve, you fixed your body at the age of six so that you no longer have to worry about your yang energy leaking out.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Strictly speaking, this can indeed be considered a method of cultivation.

The two recalled that when cultivators reached a certain realm, they could control their appearances. But why are there cultivators who like to adopt the appearance of a young child or an old person? Is Grand Shifu similar?

No no no, we can’t think too much about this. The two of them hastily cleared their minds.

“In any case, with me here, none of the Fusion cultivators here can dream of escaping!” The white-haired child forcibly changed the subject. “Lass Yun, you’ve captured two people?”

“Mmm, I want to interrogate them.”

“Why don’t you just search their souls?” the white-haired child suggested.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “Searching their souls will damage their minds. Fusion souls are excellent materials for crafting magical treasures. If they lose their mind and consciousness, the effects of the magical treasures will be severely compromised.”

The two Fusion cultivators trembled. Isn’t the Dao-Seeking Sect supposed to be a righteous sect? This is not the righteous sect we imagined!

Yun Zhi looked at the two Fusion cultivators in confusion, not understanding why they were frightened. “Since you caused so many people to die in fear, isn’t it only normal for you to be subjected to a similar treatment?”

Don't do unto others what you don't want done unto you. Yun Zhi thought that the two were already well aware of this principle.

Yun Zhi and the white-haired child each grabbed one of the Fusion souls and tossed them into the cages. Lu Yang followed Yun Zhi, while Meng Jingzhou followed the white-haired child.

From the outset, Yun Zhi executed a series of brutal tortures, employing a myriad of torture instruments designed for soul bodies in succession. The person cried out in pain repeatedly, and Lu Yang’s eyelids involuntarily twitched. I didn’t expect Big Senior Sister to be so harsh.

Hold on, wasn't Big Senior Sister also like this when I began cultivating? Don’t tell me that Big Senior Sister applied her experience in torture to teaching me how to cultivate...

Every time the Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw Yun Zhi use a torture instrument, she couldn’t help but shiver. It was really a wise decision to join the Dao-Seeking Sect. They shouldn’t be so ruthless to their own people, right?

“Strange, why is he not confessing anything?” Yun Zhi was perplexed. Grand Shifu has told me that the criminals will definitely spill all the beans if I follow this entire process.

Lu Yang whispered at the side, “Big Senior Sister, you haven’t asked him anything yet.”

“Oh,” Yun Zhi replied curtly. Then, she picked up the first torture instrument and prepared to start the process all over again.

The Fusion cultivator was scared out of his wits and shouted, “No, no, no! I’ll confess! I’ll tell you everything!”

“Which era are you from?”

“The forty-thousandth year of the Great Yu Dynasty.”

“Have you heard of the Everlasting Immortal or the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?”

“No, I haven’t.”

“Hmm? Are you lying?”

The man was frightened to the verge of tears by Yun Zhi’s cold visage. “I really haven’t heard of them. In our era, we only heard that there were immortals in the western Buddhist Kingdom and the southern Demon Region, and it was suspected that the East Sea and the Extreme North had immortals. I don’t even know the name of an immortal.

“If you are looking for the Everlasting Immortal, you might want to check out the Extreme North. Perhaps the immortal is frozen there. That can somewhat count as ‘everlasting.’”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was so enraged that she nearly rolled up her sleeves to hit the person.

1. Shigong is the master of the master, or in other words, the shifu of one’s shifu. ☜

2. The two phrases are respectively from chapters 28 and 20 of the Dao De Jing by Laozi. ☜

Chapter 147: Five Ancient Immortals

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy bristled with rage. “Everlasting” is a title I take pride in. How could a mere Fusion cultivator belittle it like this? “This immortal shall freeze you in ice marrow for ten thousand years, coat you in batter, then deep-fry you in oil!” she fiercely threatened.

Did you really think that immortals are easy to bully? I killed the one called Immortal Vanquisher True Person with a single poke of my finger. I don’t believe you can withstand the power of my finger!

“Calm down, don’t get yourself worked up.” Inside his mental space, Lu Yang held the Everlasting Immortal Fairy back, urging her to roll her sleeves back down.

This Fusion cultivator was called Three-Tenets True Person.[1] The information he shared was similar to what the Immortal Vanquisher True Person had confessed, the only valuable detail being the location of a cave domain. “The cave domain is really there. It contains my lifetime wealth. If you don’t believe me, you can go see for yourself. You’ll know that I’m speaking the truth then.

“However, I have set rules for that cave domain such that only those at the Foundation Establishment Stage or below can enter. That said, Foundation Establishment cultivators definitely can’t gain control of the cave domain. As long as you vow not to refine me, I’ll gift that cave to you!” The Three-Tenets True Person tried to issue a threat.

Yun Zhi didn’t agree to his terms, not intending to play along with him. Although the Dao-Seeking Sect refines souls, has an off-kilter ethos, and even recruited Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, we are still a righteous sect, so there are certain lines we mustn’t cross. That includes lying.

Yun Zhi led Lu Yang out of the prison and happened to run into the Grand Shifu and Meng Jingzhou, who were also just done with their interrogation.

Yun Zhi and the Grand Shifu corroborated the testimonies with each other and concluded that they were mostly consistent. The only discrepancy was that the Fusion cultivator the Grand Shifu had interrogated knew of someone called “Heaven Mandate Immortal.”

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal is in the East Sea, but I don’t know the exact location.”

Yun Zhi nodded, though this wasn’t any new information. Having caught numerous ancient Fusion cultivators and verifying it with ancient texts, she had long known that one of the ancient five immortals, the Heaven Mandate Immortal, was in the East Sea.

“Heaven Mandate Immortal?” This wasn’t Lu Yang’s first time hearing the name as the Everlasting Immortal had mentioned it a few times. According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the Heaven Mandate Immortal is an immortal of comparable power to her. However, considering the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s strength and character, Lu Yang didn’t yet have an accurate understanding of the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal is in the East Sea? Let’s go! Take me there to look for him. With my name, I guarantee that you will be living the high life!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy excitedly egged Lu Yang on, painting an unrealistic dream for him.

Lu Yang reminded, “Don’t forget how you died. Up until now, we still don’t know who killed you, but it must have been one of the four other immortals. Aren’t you afraid that it might be the Heaven Mandate Immortal?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt as if Lu Yang had doused her with a basin of cold water. As she calmed down, she murmured, “Pro-probably not? The Heaven Mandate Immortal was a pretty good person. He doesn’t look like someone with malicious intentions...”

“Then out of the four immortals, who do you suspect the most?”

The Everlasting Immortal fell silent. She didn’t feel that anyone could have killed her. Everyone appeared to be harmonious, and they were very polite toward me.

But I also must admit that my death had something to do with one of the four immortals.

“Then who do you think was capable of refining all the stars into a continent?” Lu Yang asked, thinking that it was a clue that could narrow the range of suspects for the Ancient Nameless One.

The Everlasting Immortal was clearly not on the same wavelength. “All five of us could.”

“...What the hell?!” Immortal Fairy, you are so powerful? Was I too casual with you previously?

Lu Yang finally realized that the term “immortal” was not just a cultivation realm but instead represented the lifelong pursuit of cultivators. It implied that they had reached the pinnacle of cultivation and possessed boundless power that could cover the sky with just one hand—refining the stars was nothing to them! The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hasn’t had the opportunity to showcase her power because she is still recovering!

Just then, Yun Zhi told Lu Yang, “The ancient immortals are the Heaven Mandate Immortal, Qilin Immortal, Epoch Immortal, and the Nine-Layers Immortal.”

For most people, immortals were lofty and inscrutable, with even an air of skepticism around their existence. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had only learned of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy through the Everlasting Creed.

However, at Yun Zhi’s position, she possessed far more knowledge than the common people, so the names of the four immortals were no secret to her. “The whereabouts of the four immortals are still unclear, but what we can be certain of is that the Heaven Mandate Immortal is in the East Sea, the Qilin Immortal is in the southern Demon Region, while the Epoch Immortal and Nine-Layers Immortal are unaccounted for.”

One of the immortals’ titles caught Lu Yang’s attention. “Qilin?” He recalled that one of the Little Herb Kings from the herb garden was the Qilin Immortality Herb.

Legends said that qilins didn’t exist and that the “qilin” ancient people saw were actually the Qilin Immortality Herb. Does the name “Qilin Immortal” mean that their original form is a qilin?

Noticing Lu Yang’s interest in the topic, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained, “The Qilin Immortal’s real name is Shihe, and his original form is indeed a qilin. According to him, he was a unique existence, born from the inconceivable convergence of the world’s fortune. In any case, there was only one qilin in my era. I am not sure about the current era, but there shouldn’t be a second qilin.”

In fact, before the Everlasting Immortal Fairy appeared, Yun Zhi had always thought there were only four immortals from ancient times; to be precise, everyone else thought so.

The most ancient of the Fusion cultivators imprisoned in Incarceration Peak could be traced back to the Great Qian era, which was over two hundred thousand years ago. According to him, there were only four immortals during the ancient era. This also matched with the ancient texts.

Before the inception of the Everlasting Creed, there was not a single record regarding the “Everlasting Immortal Fairy” in history! After the Everlasting Creed emerged, cultivators believed that they had fabricated the whole thing and that there was no such immortal in ancient times.

“I was an eminent immortal in ancient times. Even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would tremble in fear at my presence. Why are there no records of my immortal name?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was furious. The person who killed me is familiar with the special characteristics of my Dao Fruit, so they deliberately erased my existence from history.

“Wait, according to the naming convention of the four ancient immortals, shouldn’t you be called the Everlasting Immortal?” Lu Yang asked.

“It’s all because of that fellow Heaven Mandate Immortal. He said that it sounded imposing and even suggested that I call myself the ‘Everlasting Immortal.’

“How could I possibly agree? It sounds so awful. Since it doesn’t distinguish the gender, it makes it sound like I’m a male. ‘Everlasting Immortal Fairy’ sounds so much nicer!”

Lu Yang felt that “Huang Doudou” sounded nicer, but he naturally knew he couldn’t voice that out loud, else the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would surely explode in anger.

After Yun Zhi ensured that the two prisoners were locked up securely, she bid goodbye to her Grand Shifu before leaving with Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“Big Senior Sister, should we head to the ancient cave ruins the Three-Tenets True Person mentioned?” Lu Yang noticed that Yun Zhi flew out of the Dao-Seeking Sect instead of returning to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

As the cloud Yun Zhi steered was huge, Lu Yang couldn’t see what was below and naturally didn’t fear the height.

Yun Zhi nodded.

There’s value in checking out a Fusion cultivator’s lifetime wealth.

1. Sanli or “Three Establishments” refer to establishing virtue, meritorious service, and opinions. ☜

Chapter 148: Three-Tenets Cave Domain

“What ancient cave ruin?” Meng Jingzhou wasn’t around during the interrogation and torture segment.

Lu Yang filled him in, “The Three-Tenet True Person who we interrogated left behind a cave domain that contains his lifetime wealth. However, the “Rule” he set only allows those at the Foundation Establishment Stage or below to enter.”

Meng Jingzhou sharply inhaled a breath of cold air. “A Fusion cultivator’s lifetime wealth?” Lu Yang may have no idea, but I know how astonishing a Fusion cultivator’s wealth can be just by looking at my clan elders. They won’t deplete it even if they try to squander it their whole life.

He had been envious of such tremendous wealth since his childhood. If I could obtain even a fraction of it, I’d be set for life. Even a giant organization like the Dao-Seeking Sect can’t ignore the wealth of a Fusion cultivator!

“Since only Foundation Establishment cultivators and below can enter, hehe, isn’t this the perfect chance for us?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou chuckled. This type of secret domain with a restriction on one’s cultivation realm was ideal for them to showcase their skills. Big Senior Sister must have brought us here to explore the ancient cave ruins because of our talents.

The magical cloud they rode on flew incredibly fast. When people on the ground looked up, they would see a colorful cloud streaking across the sky in the blink of an eye, as if it was a figment of their imagination.

Soon, the three arrived at the location the Three-Tenets True Person had described.

Demarcation of regions during the Great Yu era was different from today. According to the current system, the Three-Tenets True Person’s ancient cave ruin was beneath the sixteenth tree from the peak of Big Wave Mountain in Huayun Commandery, which was located in the eastern part of Ji Province.

Yun Zhi touched the tree trunk. Sensing the fluctuations of space, she confirmed that there was indeed a cave domain here.

The cave domain was hidden and hard to scout out. Even someone as powerful as Yun Zhi needed to be in close proximity to verify if a cave domain existed. It was not surprising that the Three-Tenets True Person’s cave domain remained undiscovered.

Yun Zhi flicked the tree trunk with her index and middle fingers. As the space distorted, a black entrance appeared before the three.

The entrance looked like a black vortex, its center swirling continuously. Talismans flickered within due to the “Rules” established, signifying that the cave domain had a master. The entry rule for this cave domain was that only Foundation Establishment cultivators aged twenty or below could enter.

Just as Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou thought that Yun Zhi would ask them to go in, they saw her pinching the edges of the black vortex with her bare hands and ripping an enormous hole in it. At that moment, any rule disintegrated—nothing could restrict Yun Zhi.

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Shouldn’t this be our moment to shine? Why is it nothing like what we’d imagined? Are we just extras here? Why did Big Senior Sister bring us over?

Lu Yang voiced his questions, and Yun Zhi tilted her head as she sought an answer. “Didn’t you both tag along when we left Incarceration Peak? I don’t recall calling you both.”

Fine, we really are extras.

Inside Lu Yang’s mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy guffawed so hard that she almost fell over.

When the three of them entered the ancient cave ruin, a vast prairie stretched before them. Elephants were munching tree leaves slowly, and lions chased antelopes and chomped on their necks, while on the other side of the prairie lay a dense rainforest, where colossal creatures could be seen wandering through the verdure.

Lu Yang could clearly feel that his cultivation was being suppressed; he could only unleash his strength at the Advanced Qi Training Stage.

Right then, words formed by clouds grabbed their attention.

*

Danger here, leave quickly

Danger here, leave quickly

Danger here, leave quickly

*

If you insist on entering, please remember the rules of the Three-Tenets Cave Domain; they may save your life.

Rule 1: Everyone’s cultivation will be suppressed to the Level Nine Qi Training Stage.

Rule 2: You are unable to contact the outside world.

Rule 3: The Three-Tenets Cave Domain only has a prairie and no rainforest; if you see a rainforest, please do not enter.

Rule 4: Lions are kind. If a lion chases you, please do not run away; it just wants to play with you.

Rule 5: Antelopes are a type of bipedal demon beast with spiraled horns on their heads. It is normal for antelopes to laugh; please do not be afraid.

Rule 6: There are no elephants on the prairie. If you see an elephant, please make sure to seek a lion for protection; lions will protect you.

Rule 7: If you accidentally enter the rainforest, please do not panic; remaining calm is essential for survival in the rainforest.

Rule 8: The apes in the rainforest are humans in disguise, so it is normal for them to speak. However, the apes will not initiate conversations with you.

Rule 9: The water in the rainforest cannot be drunk.

Rule 10: If you encounter a Foundation Establishment demon beast, please mimic the sound of an ape; the demon beast will automatically leave.

Rule 11: All the rules above are true.

*

Then, Lu Yang noticed that there were several lines scrawled with blood beneath his feet, as if they were left in a hurry.

*

Quickly run, this place is dangerous!

Something strange has happened here!

*

Note! What I’ve written here are the real rules of the Three-Tenets Cave Domain!

All the rules of the Three-Tenets Cave Domain are fake...

*

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou trembled in fear as they took in the bloody handwriting. The last sentence was incomplete, leaving a long smear of blood, as if someone had desperately tried to crawl out of the cave domain, only to be bitten by some terrifying entity and dragged right back with an appalling trail of blood.

An unsettling chill seized them. What on earth is inside this cave domain?

“There are very glaring problems with these rules; they are filled with contradictions. Is the first or second set of rules correct?”

“Based on our experience in Buyi Town, the first set of rules seem more formal, so perhaps it’s the correct one?”

“Not necessarily. Just because a rule appears more formal doesn’t mean that it’s correct. The second set of rules seems to have been hastily written, but it may also be a form of rules.”

The two found themselves in an impasse. Their strength was reduced to the Level Nine Qi Training Stage, yet the place was swarming with Foundation Establishment and Golden Core demon beasts. Since they couldn’t fight with brute force, they could only rely on their wits. However, there were currently two sets of rules, and they couldn’t discern the correct one. Once they made a wrong decision, it could likely consign them to their demise.

“Don’t panic, there must be a solution. One rule says that the lions are kind, while the other says that lions eat people. One rule says that elephants will kill us, while the other says that elephants will protect us. We can lure both the elephants and lions together in one place and see which would protect us. That way, we’ll be able to determine which set of rules is the real one...”

“Could it be possible that both rules are partially true and false just to sabotage people?”

“That makes it a bit tricky.”

Just as the two were racking their brains over a way out, they saw Yun Zhi raise her hand and gently deliver a strike with her palm. However, it clearly did not belong to the Qi Training Stage.

The palm wind encompassed terrifying power as it howled on a rampage, frightening the lions, antelope, elephants, and apes into fleeing in all directions. Regardless of whether they ate or protected people, they were all equal before this palm strike—they could only run for their lives.

The attack tore through the prairie and rainforest, creating a distinct path to their destination.

How could the rules here possibly restrain Yun Zhi?

Chapter 149: Ancient Transcendent Tribulation Cultivator

“Hold on, there’s something off about the ‘Rules’ here.” Yun Zhi furrowed her brow. She had sensed something amiss the moment she struck. Her palm strike should have shattered the rules in this place, yet they’d only appeared to dissipate on the surface. Even if she had held back her strength, it still didn’t make sense.

“There are two types of ‘Rules’ here.” Yun Zhi figured out the reason. The first set of rules was written with clouds, but something strange happened, and the second set of rules that was written with blood emerged.

The two sets of rules conflict, throwing the whole cave into disarray! Someone has deliberately caused this chaos to prevent anyone from leaving. Moreover, the external set of rules can compete with the original set of rules, which implies that the person who left behind the second set of rules is more powerful than the cave domain’s master.

And the Three-Tenets True Person is already at the Apex Fusion Stage.

“Heh, who dares disturb the slumber of this venerable one?”

The sound of ice cracking reverberated through the cave, and an overpowering aura wave burst forth from the other end of the path, as if a sovereign from the nine heavens had descended and was looking down at the world with indifference. Rays of light pierced through the firmament, while one’s heart palpitated as the aura waves grew increasingly stronger, like it could sweep through everything in its way.

“Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy quickly ascertained his cultivation realm.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s expressions shifted drastically. Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage? This is the most formidable opponent we’ve ever encountered. Why is there a Transcendent Tribulation expert in a Fusion cultivator’s cave domain?

With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s extensive knowledge, she soon figured out the reason. “It’s very simple. This cave domain is an ideal hiding spot, so awakening here allows a safe harbor to restore their strength gradually. However, the downside is that they can’t detect changes in the outside world promptly. For instance, the Three-Tenets True Person could sense the changes in spirit opportunities and wake up in Buyi Town, but this Transcendent Tribulation cultivator here may not awake even long after the battle of the Great Era concludes.

“Therefore, he came up with a clever plan. Since the Three-Tenets True Person can awaken in time, after he awakens, he will inevitably return to the cave domain. When he discovers changes to the ‘Rules,’ he’ll take action, triggering the awakening of this Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

“He also established a new set of rules in this cave domain to ensure that those who accidentally enter this place would lose their lives so that they wouldn’t disturb his slumber.”

Lu Yang broke out in cold sweat, surprised by the complex web of factors at play.

“Aiya, what are you scared of? I can easily trample a mere Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator dead.” Huang Doudou boasted shamelessly. Anyway, with Yun Zhi around, she’ll take care of everything.

“I am the Blood Devil Venerable Lord. Who are you? State your name.” The Blood Devil Venerable Lord eyed Yun Zhi coldly. To have broken the rules with such ease, she has to be at least at the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage too. But so what? He was confident that he could still hold his own even if he faced off with an Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

“Blood Devil Venerable Lord?!” Meng Jingzhou exclaimed softly.

“You know him?” Lu Yang asked.

“Yes, I do.” As Transcendent Tribulation cultivators were few in existence, every one of them earned a place in the historical records, so Meng Jingzhou had heard of the Blood Devil Venerable Lord’s title. When he couldn’t fall asleep as a child, his mother would often frighten him with stories of the Blood Devil Venerable Lord.

“The Blood Devil Venerable Lord is a diabolic cultivator who has slaughtered countless people. Legend says that he wrote the names of all the cities on pieces of paper and rolled them into balls. Whichever he picked, he would use the people of that city to cultivate. His cultivation journey is paved with bones!

“He also once supported a Yu emperor and became the imperial preceptor, wielding immense power over the Great Yu Dynasty. For some reason, he subsequently vanished. Some say that he died under a lightning tribulation due to his evil deeds, but from the looks of it now, he has been hiding here all this while!”

Yun Zhi announced, “Yun Zhi of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

The Blood Devil Venerable Lord was puzzled by Yun Zhi’s lack of reaction. Was my name not passed down to this era? That doesn’t matter. I’ll just unleash carnage to remind the world of my name.

In contrast to Fusion cultivators, Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would swiftly return to their peak after awakening.

A blood-colored titan roared as it rose to the sky. It turned the “Rules” into axes that casually swung them. The whole space shook, as if the cave domain could crumble under its might.

Yun Zhi raised one hand before her chest, radiating boundless golden light. She looked like a Bodhisattva stepping out of a mural, holy and inviolable. With a push of her palm, the beams of golden light pierced through the darkness toward the blood-colored titan.

The blood-colored titan blocked it with the two axes formed from the “Rules,” but they gradually dissolved under the golden light, along with the hardened shell of the blood-colored titan.

Blood drained from the Blood Devil Venerable Lord’s face. “No way, you’re not at the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage!”

Tearing space apart, he turned on his heels. A battle with an Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation cultivator will not end so quickly. It’s not worth recklessly provoking such an enemy for the sake of pride. After ripping the space apart, I will be randomly transported to somewhere in the world, and they’ll never be able to find me.

The Blood Devil Venerable Lord was just about to cackle loudly and talk tough when he saw a graceful figure walking over in the brilliant golden light. Although her steps appeared to be slow, they were actually at lightning speed. In the blink of an eye, she was already standing before him.

“Wait, you’re not at the Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation Stage at all. Even Advanced Transcendent Tribulation cultivators don’t possess your level of techniques. You’re at the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage or perhaps even—”

“You know too much,” Yun Zhi replied frigidly.

Clasping her hands together, she squashed out the Blood Devil Venerable Lord’s soul. A Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s physical body is an excellent material for crafting artifacts. I must be careful not to crush it.

Yun Zhi took out a Jade Cleansing Bottle[1] and trapped the Blood Devil Venerable Lord’s soul within, planning to interrogate and torture him slowly after returning to the sect.

The entire process was as effortless as the light breeze in the cave domain, looking like nothing had transpired.

The lions and antelopes danced in pairs, working hard to prove that they were good demon beasts that had harmonious relationships with each other, while the elephants lay on their back with their limbs pointed upward in an attempt to feign death.

“Looks like ancient Transcendent Tribulation cultivators may hide within cave domains,” Yun Zhi mused to herself. This is a possibility I haven’t considered before. I have to inform the four other immortal sects and the Great Xia Dynasty after we leave this cave domain.

“Let’s go,” Yun Zhi said lightly as she strode gracefully toward the exit.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged glances with each other and hurried to catch up with her. There was no danger along the way, or at least, that was how it seemed to the two of them.

However, it was a completely different story for the demon beasts—a fearsome great devil queen with a chilling aura led her two attendants to roam the cave domain wantonly, spreading terror and instilling fear in their wake.

When the trio reached the end, they saw several enormous golden treasure chests and piles of spirit stones, where premium-grade spirit stones were in greater numbers than high-grade spirit stones. It was a treasure trove that made one drool. Not only were the Three-Tenets True Person’s treasures here, some of the Blood Devil Venerable Lord items also lay here.

Yun Zhi opened the golden treasure chests, revealing a dazzling assortment of natural treasures and secret manuals. Even with Meng Jingzhou’s experience, he struggled to identify the origins of these treasures in such a short time.

However, Yun Zhi could easily determine the items’ names and functions. “Dragon Transformation Grass. If a jiao dragon consumes and refines this, it can increase its chance of becoming a dragon by thirty percent.” Transforming into a dragon was a jiao dragon’s lifelong dream, so it was obvious how valuable this item was.

“Bodhi Fruit. Ingesting this can enhance one’s wisdom root at the expense of permanently losing their hair.

“Red Sun Vajra Sand. It is an essential ingredient for crafting high-grade fire-type magical treasures.

“Liuli-Glazed Heavenly Cleansed Water. Applying it to your whole body can preserve your physical form for a hundred thousand years.

“A Fusion demon beast’s inner core...

“A Fusion dragon’s tendon...

“Blissful union powder...” [2]

There seems to be quite the collection of treasures with “-ion” in them. [3]

1. A magical item belonging to Guanyin in Journey to the West. ☜

2. This is often depicted as an aphrodisiac for bedroom affairs. The first character in Chinese shares the same first character for “Fusion Stage.” ☜

3. To be more accurate, all the items have the character “合(he)” in them. I could only squeeze out the “-ion.” ☜

Chapter 150: That Bastard Heaven Mandate Immortal

Unfortunately, some of the natural treasures had lost their medicinal properties due to improper storage and were now reduced to ordinary goods, while some were no longer as valuable due to time. For instance, the Blissful Union Powder had expired. The Dragon Transformation Grass was another example. Two thousand years ago, the Dragon Tribe had found a stable way to grow it, causing its price to plummet.

“They still have archaeological and commemorative value. We can sell it to the Dragon Tribe’s museum,” Yun Zhi murmured. It’s rare to have wild Dragon Transformation Grass so well-preserved. I didn’t see a wild Dragon Transformation Grass when I visited the Dragon Tribe’s museum.

Huang Doudou scoffed, “These junk? Back when I was alive, I wouldn’t even bother picking these things from the ground! Wait until you find my treasure trove. I’ll show you what real treasures look like!”

Lu Yang rolled his eyes, pretending he didn’t hear the Everlasting Immortal Fairy as he continued rummaging through the treasures with Yun Zhi.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stomped her foot angrily. Back in ancient times, countless cultivators lost their entire fortune just for a chance to meet me and hear me say a few words! What I say are immortal words that can benefit people for a lifetime!

This boy really doesn’t know what’s good for him. Hmph, I shall ignore him!

Suddenly, Lu Yang uncovered a thick book that was packaged exquisitely and soft to the touch, clearly not an ordinary item. Perhaps this thick book was really not ordinary, for the Blood Devil Venerable Lord had even specially left a note on the book’s origins.

Lu Yang read out loud, “I acquired this book on immortal spells from a black-market stall. According to the stall owner, its origins, material, and contents are unknown. What is certain is that it is sealed by a powerful array and is an item from ancient times.

“I laughed at the vendor's ignorance and for not recognizing the treasure he possessed. Opening my heavenly eye, I spotted the word ‘immortal’ below the seal. This is not just an ancient item but an item belonging to one of the four ancient immortals. Since this book was written by an immortal, it could likely be the immortal spells in the legends!

“Alas, the ancient seal was formidable. Despite dedicating my whole life to it, I still could not open it.”

Lu Yang exclaimed, “Immortal spells!” His heart raced. I didn’t expect the legendary immortal spells to be hidden here! What a fortuitous opportunity! What’s more, this is such a thick book. It either contains an overly complex immortal spell or several immortal spells. Regardless of which, this book is extremely valuable!

He tried to open the book but was unable to do so, just like the Blood Devil Venerable Lord.

“Hmm? This thing looks familiar.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s strong willpower had enabled her to ignore Lu Yang for a full twenty seconds.

“Have you seen this before, Immortal Fairy? Can you open the seal?” Lu Yang asked.

“Of course, this kind of small seal can be broken with a finger.”

Following the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s instructions, Lu Yang carefully infused his spirit energy inside, and the seal really did come undone.

He restrained his excitement and opened the ancient text. The bottom right corner had the author’s name written—Heaven Mandate Immortal.

It’s really written by an immortal! Lu Yang was delighted. The Heaven Mandate Immortal must be a reliable immortal. If the four other ancient immortals were like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, wouldn’t the ancient era have been doomed?

Shifting his eyes upward, he saw the book’s title—Comprehensive Culinary Compendium.

“Huh?” Lu Yang flipped through a few pages and found that the contents matched the title exactly—it was a detailed guide on how to cook myriad demon beats.

To hell with your damn immortal spells! Heaven Mandate Immortal, you’re not reliable at all! Why do you have to put a seal on something like this? What, are you afraid that the human race will cause the demon beasts to go extinct by eating them?

At this point, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had also sensed that something was wrong and knitted her brows. “Wait a minute, I have eaten all kinds of demon beasts out there and compiled my culinary experiences into a book. It’s supposed to be my proud work. How did it become the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s?” She gnashed her teeth. “That bastard Heaven Mandate Immortal stole my work after I died?”

“So you were the one who wrote it. That makes a lot more sense.” Lu Yang finally rationalized everything.

“What did you say?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s expression looked like the lull before a storm.

“Ah, no, I meant that the Heaven Mandate Immortal must have had a lot of time on his hands to write his name on a book like this.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that Lu Yang was severely underestimating her. “Kid, you don’t have a discerning eye, belittling my work like that. If you can master this book of mine, you can become a Transcendent Tribulation spirit chef. There will be no lack of people outside fighting over this book. It’ll be utter chaos and madness!

“When I cooked for the other four back then, they felt unworthy to partake of my food. They would come up with all sorts of excuses and didn’t dare to come over!”

“Are you sure it’s not because your cooking was awful?”

“Nonsense! The food I made radiated golden light. How could it be awful?!”

As the human and immortal bickered, they circled back to the matter of the Heaven Mandate Immortal and couldn’t reach a consensus even after half a day. Lu Yang informed Yun Zhi about it, but she simply frowned and made no comments.

On the other hand, Meng Jingzhou had discovered some cultivation techniques. Although some were lost to time and some had been modified, it was overall a satisfactory outcome.

When Yun Zhi was sifting through the treasures, she suddenly revealed an astounded expression. “This is the cultivation takeaways of someone with the Immaculate Celestial Physique?” I didn’t expect to find something like this here, and it even belongs to a Basic Fusion cultivator at that.

Cultivation insights of those with celestial physiques were rare, and cultivation insights suited for the Dao-Seeking Sect were even rarer.

Lu Yang asked inside his mental space, “Immortal Fairy, did you have celestial physiques in your time? Can they become immortals?”

From what Lu Yang knew, there were twenty types of celestial physiques in the world. They were constitutions even rarer than Single Spirit Roots. Whenever a cultivator with a celestial physique advances to the Fusion Stage, they would automatically develop “Rules” with terrifying and unpredictable power that would be difficult to defend against.

He had heard that there were two people in the Dao-Seeking Sect with celestial physiques—Tao Yaoye and her shifu, Sixth Elder. Tao Yaoye had a Metamorphic Celestial Physique while Sixth Elder had an Immaculate Celestial Physique.

Huang Doudou was still seething over “the shameless Heaven Mandate Immortal stealing her intellectual property,” but her fury dissipated quickly. I, Huang Doudou, am a magnanimous person.

She shifted her attention upon hearing Lu Yang’s question. “Celestial physique? We had them back in my era. The history of celestial physiques goes back much further than you can imagine.

“The concept of celestial physiques can be traced back to the most ancient era. At that time, humans still didn’t know how to cultivate and could only rely on trial and error. Foundation Establishment, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration were attained by relying on the special characteristics of celestial physiques.

“I only know of one immortal with a celestial physique, and that was the Nine-Layers Immortal. He was a formidable opponent with strength comparable to mine!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s expression grew solemn at the mention of the Nine-Layers Immortal, acknowledging his power.

“The Nine-Layers Immortal was the first to become an immortal among us. According to him, his celestial physique played a significant role in helping him ascend to an immortal!”

Lu Yang sneakily asked, “So, does Big Senior Sister have a celestial physique? What exactly is her cultivation level?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled. “Guess.”

Lu Yang’s face darkened. How am I supposed to guess?

“Lu Yang, when you return to the sect, hand this cultivation record to Sixth Elder. The insights fit her best.”

~~~

And thus, the three returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect with a substantial harvest.

Yun Zhi went to Incarceration Peak to interrogate the Blood Devil Venerable Lord, Meng Jingzhou returned to the Physique Refinement Peak to train, while Lu Yang headed to Speckless Peak to pass the book on cultivation insights to Sixth Elder.
